Chapter 1400: Has he already condensed a Saint Soul?

Chapter 1400: He has already condensed a Saint Soul
?
"Damn it, he's impossible to kill!"
Ancestor Xuangui said helplessly.
This was also his first time encountering such a difficult opponent as Ye Tian; if it were other supreme domain ancestors, even if their strength was comparable to Ye Tian's, they would be besieged and killed by these four-star 44 kings, or worn down to death.
But Ye Tian could escape into the depths of the void and easily recover all his strength, and possessed the Undying Saint Skill, healing his injuries too quickly; even their trump cards couldn't instantly inflict heavy damage on Ye Tian.
Therefore, they couldn't do anything to Ye Tian.
If this continued, Ye Tian wouldn't die, but they would instead be severely wounded and fall one by one.
"What should we do?"
Ancestor Xuangui asked via message.
Ancestor Yuanfeng was also quite helpless; in this situation, he had no solutions either.
Unless they possessed a top-tier sacred artifact that could instantly kill an invincible domain ancestor-level being, only then would there be hope of killing Ye Tian in one blow.
But they didn't have such a top-tier sacred artifact! "Let's send a message to Lord Ancestor Quezhan, he was the one who told us to act. We can't kill Ancestor Wanfa; if he doesn't care, once Ancestor Wanfa targets us, we won't be able to resist him, unless we stay in the branch forever and never come out!"
Ancestor Yuanfeng said.
"This is the only way!"
Ancestor Xuangui and the others responded one by one.
In the distance.
Ancestor Quezhan received messages from Ancestor Yuanfeng, Ancestor Xuangui, and the others.
"A bunch of good-for-nothings!"
Ancestor Quezhan cursed under his breath.
However, he had already anticipated all of this, he was just a little unwilling.
Now, Ancestor Yuanfeng and the others had sent messages asking for help; clearly, they were truly at their wit's end.
If Ancestor Yuanfeng and the others continued to fight Ye Tian, it was likely that a few more four-star 44 kings would fall.
Four-star 44 kings were not... cabbages; they were the foundation of the Ghost Fox Organization's future! Although the final decision was made by the leader, if too many four-star 44 kings fell, he would also suffer severe punishment.
Therefore, no more four-star 44 kings could be allowed to fall.
"Ancestor Qingyang, it's your turn to act. Once you successfully kill Ancestor Wanfa, all the benefits you ask for will be given to you.
Remember, you must use all your strength to kill Ancestor Wanfa, do not hold anything back.
I know you've always hidden your strength, I'm not sure exactly what level it has reached, but I hope you don't get careless, understand?"
Ancestor Quezhan reminded him.
"Lord Ancestor Quezhan, rest assured, Ancestor Wanfa is just a mere trifle, it won't be difficult for me to kill him!"
Ancestor Qingyang said with a smile.
However, what Ancestor Qingyang didn't know was that Ye Tian's Eternal Undying Saint Body had reached its most critical moment.
If the shackles of the Eternal Undying Saint Body's perfection and ultimate realm were likened to a barrier, then this barrier was now covered in cracks and could shatter completely at any moment.
If Ye Tian wished, he could even forcefully break through to the ultimate realm of the Eternal Undying Saint Body right now.
However, Ye Tian did not do so.
He thought that the Ghost Fox Organization might still have trump cards or hidden kings who hadn't made their move; he planned to wait until that person made their move before breaking through to the ultimate realm of the Eternal Undying Saint Body.
As the number one Saint Body in the Dark Saint Domain, the Eternal Undying Saint Body was incredibly powerful; once it reached the ultimate realm, its power would skyrocket many times over.
Only then would the Eternal Undying Saint Body truly be the Eternal Undying Saint Body.
Suddenly.
Ancestor Yuanfeng and Ancestor Xuangui retreated one after another, while a figure rapidly streaked from a distance, arriving before Ye Tian in an instant, blocking Ye Tian and preventing Ye Tian from pursuing the other four-star 44 kings.
Ye Tian did not continue his pursuit, but instead stared at Ancestor Qingyang.
From the investigation of his replication talent, Ye Tian learned Ancestor Qingyang's name and general background.
"A four-star 44 king of the Ghost Fox Organization, it seems to be a hidden four-star 44 king!"
Ye Tian thought to himself:.
Ancestor Qingyang was not a Saint-gifted one, but his strength was probably far from simple; he put pressure on Ye Tian.
Clearly, Ancestor Qingyang was very powerful! "Ancestor Qingyang, it's him, hasn't he broken through to the invincible domain ancestor realm yet?"
Ancestor Xuangui and the other four-star 44 kings recognized Ancestor Qingyang's identity.
The outside world didn't know Ancestor Qingyang, but they knew that the Ghost Fox Organization had such a four-star 44 king, and an incredibly ancient four-star 44 king; when they first joined the Ghost Fox Organization, Ancestor Qingyang was already a four-star 44 king.
Moreover, Ancestor Qingyang had been out of contact for a long time; they even thought Ancestor Qingyang had already broken through to the invincible domain ancestor realm, unexpectedly, he was still in the supreme domain ancestor realm.
"Ancestor Qingyang, let's besiege Ancestor Wanfa together!"
Ancestor Xuangui suggested.
"A bunch of good-for-nothings, get out of my way, don't interfere with me!"
Ancestor Qingyang said very impolitely.
"You...."
Ancestor Xuangui and the others were extremely annoyed.
They were all four-star 44 kings, yet Ancestor Qingyang actually called them good-for-nothings; it was simply too detestable! Just as Ancestor Xuangui and the others were about to retort, Ancestor Quezhan's voice descended: "Everyone retreat, let Ancestor Qingyang deal with Ancestor Wanfa alone!"
"Yes!"
Ancestor Xuangui and the others obediently retreated; they dared not defy Ancestor Quezhan's orders, otherwise, they would be seeking death.
In reality, it would have been the best approach for them to assist Ancestor Qingyang against Ye Tian, but Ancestor Qingyang was too arrogant and believed those few four-star 44 kings were good-for-nothings, perhaps even interfering with his attacks during battle.
Therefore, he decided to fight Ancestor Wanfa alone.
"Ghost Fox Organization, Ancestor Qingyang, I ask for your guidance!"
Ancestor Qingyang introduced himself.
"War Gate, Ancestor Wanfa, I ask for your guidance!"
Ye Tian also simply said.
As soon as his words fell, the battle began.
Ancestor Qingyang, holding the Qingyang Sword, charged towards Ye Tian.
The Qingyang Sword was not a sacred artifact, but a sacred artifact had been integrated into the weapon, creating this type of weapon that could enhance combat power; such weapons were called Saint Soldiers! In reality, Saint Soldiers could not unleash the full power of a sacred artifact, but some sacred artifacts were truly unsuitable for combat; for example, Ancestor Qingyang was skilled in sword techniques, so if he didn't have a sword-type sacred artifact, he naturally could only choose this method.
This was also a type of weapon commonly used by invincible domain ancestors; transforming sacred artifacts into Saint Soldiers, the effect was quite good.
"Saint Skill: Sword Star!"
Ancestor Qingyang thrust his sword.
With a tearing sound, the void was pierced through, as if ignoring space and time, directly hitting Ye Tian's body.
*Puff puff!!* Ye Tian's Golden Body Saint Skill and Saint Armor Saint Skill both failed to block this sword; all were broken, and even the somewhat damaged Golden Star Armor was pierced, leaving a sword hole on his body.
This time, Ye Tian was injured, and not lightly.
If Ye Tian hadn't used the Undying Saint Skill to quickly heal his injuries in time, he would probably have been severely wounded.
"So strong!"
Ye Tian said solemnly.
Compared to Ancestor Xuangui and the others, Ancestor Qingyang's strength had completely risen to another level.
Moreover, he couldn't perceive the strength of Ancestor Qingyang's Soul Saint Light; as if it had returned to its original simplicity, the Soul Saint Light and his own power were completely integrated, only then could it be completely imperceptible.
"Could it be that he has already condensed a Saint Soul!!!"
Ye Tian guessed! To read the version without underlines, please download Stone Novel.

Chapter 1401: Eternal Undying Sacred Body, Extreme Realm!

Chapter 1401: Eternal Undying Sacred Body, Extreme Realm
!
The Sacred Soul is the ultimate pursuit of the ultimate domain ancestors. The ultimate domain ancestors on the Top Ten Sacred Gates' Ultimate Power List, as well as those four-star 44 kings of the Ghost Fox Organization, their pursuit is... to condense a Sacred Soul.
But in reality, how many can condense a Sacred Soul? Countless ultimate domain ancestors cultivated arduously for endless years, almost falling into madness, yet still failed to condense a Sacred Soul, and even on the path of seeking opportunities, one by one they perished.
Even if they didn't perish, it was only after endless years of despair that they abandoned this idea, choosing instead to break through to the Invincible Domain Ancestor realm and give up on condensing a Sacred Soul.
Therefore, among the ultimate domain ancestors, those who can condense a Sacred Soul are too few. Even Sacred Gifted Ones find it difficult to condense a Sacred Soul.
After all, Sacred Gifted Ones only have an advantage in cultivating Sacred Skills, but in condensing a Sacred Soul, they have no advantage.
Every genius who can condense a Sacred Soul at the ultimate domain ancestor level, after becoming an Invincible Domain Ancestor, is not weaker than a Sacred Gifted One, and may even surpass ordinary Sacred Gifted Ones.
Ye Tian also somewhat didn't expect that the Ghost Fox Organization actually had such a talented individual.
"This pressure is finally a bit interesting!"
Ye Tian smiled, without the slightest hint of panic.
"Smile"
Azure Sun Domain Ancestor frowned, certain that things might be somewhat unexpected, and therefore he didn't want to waste time.
Immediately.
Azure Sun Domain Ancestor activated the projection sword of the Grand Dawn Sword.
The Grand Dawn Sword is not an ordinary sacred artifact; it is a powerful sacred artifact ranked among the top hundred on the Sacred Artifact List. Even its projection sword possesses power comparable to sacred artifacts ranked within the top thousand on the Sacred Artifact List.
What's more, the Grand Dawn Sword projection can unleash a terrifying strike, powerful enough to slay some mighty Invincible Domain Ancestors.
Boom!!!! The golden Grand Dawn Sword emerged from Azure Sun Domain Ancestor's body, like a ten-thousand-zhang giant sword, its might intimidating the endless territories.
"This is.... the Grand Dawn Sword!!!!"
"No, wait, it's not the real Grand Dawn Sword, it's the projection sword of the Grand Dawn Sword!"
Ye Tian was surprised.
This kind of projection is similar to the War Realm Tower projection in the Profound Void Sacred Realm; it is actually a physical sword and can exist independently.
Basically, sacred artifacts in the top hundred of the Sacred Artifact List, by using some special secret methods and paying some price, can cultivate and give birth to a projection artifact.
For example, Ye Tian's Primordial Creation Well, if he knew the secret art of cultivating projection artifacts, after paying some price, he could also create a projection version of the Primordial Creation Well.
Unfortunately, he doesn't know such secret arts, nor would he create such sacred artifact projections, because there's no need.
Even if he created one, he wouldn't dare to use it, for fear that the secret of the Primordial Creation Well would be exposed. At that time, it wouldn't be just some ultimate domain ancestors that would be attracted, but Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, or even Ancestors.
The appearance of the Grand Dawn Sword's projection sword indeed made Ye Tian feel a true crisis.
Just at this moment, Ye Tian unleashed a Time Sacred Skill — Time Shards! He wanted to glimpse into the future, otherwise, he would easily stumble.
Crack!!!! A corner of the future appeared before Ye Tian.
In the future vision, Ye Tian failed to dodge the Grand Dawn Sword's strike; even the Eternal Sacred Skill couldn't freeze the Grand Dawn Sword, and the Grand Dawn Sword shattered space-time with a single strike, blasting into his body.
This sword strike, despite all his efforts, still heavily wounded him.
A projection sacred artifact like the Grand Dawn Sword, Azure Sun Domain Ancestor could only use once in a short period.
Ye Tian prepared to escape into the depths of the void to heal his injuries, and after his injuries recovered, he would immediately fight Azure Sun Domain Ancestor again.
But just as he was about to escape into the depths of the void, a gray light emanated from Azure Sun Domain Ancestor's body; that light transformed into a small knife, instantly piercing through his body.
Then, that gray light obliterated his soul, and severed the connection in the ethereal realm, crossing endless dark forbidden domains, striking towards an unknown place.
That place was—"the Profound Void Sacred Realm!"
Ye Tian was extremely surprised; this corner of the future showed him being struck down.
Of course, this corner of the future is not fixed; it is merely the most likely scenario to occur if there is no interference.
"That is a Karma Sacred Skill — Causality Annihilation!!!!"
Ye Tian said in surprise.
Karma Sacred Skills are extremely rare. Although Ye Tian possesses many Sacred Gifts, he does not have a Karma Sacred Gift, therefore, he hasn't tried to cultivate any Karma Sacred Skills.
Moreover, Karma Sacred Skills are not that easy to cultivate; they are too difficult to get started with.
Without a Karma Sacred Gift, it's likely even Invincible Domain Ancestors would find it difficult to cultivate a Karma Sacred Skill to the introductory or minor accomplishment realm.
"Azure Sun Domain Ancestor actually knows a Karma Sacred Skill, and that Karma Sacred Skill is probably cultivated to the major accomplishment realm; it seems he must have had an astonishing encounter,"
Ye Tian thought.
From the future vision, when Azure Sun Domain Ancestor fully unleashed his power, his Sacred Soul appeared.
The Sacred Soul, the Grand Dawn Sword's projection sword, plus the Karma Sacred Skill — Causality Annihilation, ultimately slew this clone body of his, and then attacked his main body from afar.
Although separated by vast territories, the power of the Karma Sacred Skill was somewhat weakened. Moreover, his main body was protected by the Profound Void Sacred Realm and the Primordial Creation Well, so even if Azure Sun Domain Ancestor's power was stronger, he couldn't kill him through the Primordial Creation Well, but he could still injure him.
In addition, this clone body of his would definitely perish.
But the premise of all this was that Ye Tian didn't know Azure Sun Domain Ancestor's plan. Now that he knew, it would be somewhat difficult for Azure Sun Domain Ancestor to kill him.
Ye Tian was very clear that his strength simply couldn't contend with Azure Sun Domain Ancestor.
Even if he was a monstrous genius, he had to admit that his current strength was far inferior to Azure Sun Domain Ancestor.
Therefore, he must complete a breakthrough to contend with Azure Sun Domain Ancestor, and even slay Azure Sun Domain Ancestor.
"Then break through!"
Ye Tian murmured.
"Eternal Undying Sacred Body, break through for me!"
Buzz!!!! Ye Tian's body suddenly shattered, endless power of forbidden grand dao protected Ye Tian, and endless rules rippled, allowing Ye Tian's body to undergo a perfect transformation.
At this moment, his body was slowly reassembling; this was a breakthrough of breaking down to rebuild! And this process simply couldn't be interrupted.
Azure Sun Domain Ancestor could only watch Ye Tian break through, without any means to stop him.
"This is the Eternal Undying Sacred Body, currently breaking through to the extreme realm!"
Azure Sun Domain Ancestor didn't know much about the Eternal Undying Sacred Body, only knowing that it was the number one Sacred Body in the Dark Sacred Domain. As for how powerful the Eternal Undying Sacred Body at the extreme realm was, he also didn't know.
"It probably won't boost his strength too much; I should still be able to kill him!"
Azure Sun Domain Ancestor murmured in his heart.
However, his confidence suddenly dropped significantly. Even though he told himself he could still kill Ye Tian, his body was somewhat tense.
Soon.
Ye Tian completely finished his breakthrough; his body had already undergone a qualitative change, completely reaching the extreme realm of the Eternal Undying Sacred Body.
It was at this moment that Ye Tian truly understood the reason why the Eternal Undying Sacred Body was called the number one Sacred Body.

Chapter 1402: The Tables Turn, Ye Tian's Terrifying Power!

Chapter 1402: The Tables Turn, Ye Tian's Terrifying Power
!
"Power of Eternity!"
Ye Tian enlightened.
Once the Undying Saint Body of Eternity was raised to its extreme realm, the Power of Eternity would be born.
The Power of Eternity could grant Ye Tian even greater explosive power, and it could also elevate Ye Tian's defense to a terrifying degree, making it an eternally unbreakable defense.
In short, once he possessed the Power of Eternity, it would be difficult for Ye Tian to fall.
After the Undying Saint Body of Eternity broke through, Ye Tian's strength was far greater than before.
At this moment, because Ye Tian had just broken through, his aura could not be fully contained, reaching an incredibly terrifying level, which startled even Ancestor Qingyang.
"This.... it's just the Saint Body breaking through from the perfect to the extreme realm, how could his aura surge so much?"
Ancestor Qingyang was dumbfounded.
"Never mind!"
Ancestor Qingyang continued to activate the Projection Sword of the Grand Dawn, aiming it at Ye Tian, unleashing a full-power strike.
The power of this strike even carried the power of his Saint Soul! Ancestor Qingyang's Saint Soul and main body merged, transforming into a colossal giant, who then thrust the Projection Sword of the Grand Dawn forward.
This sword shattered space and time, capable of annihilating everything.
Yet Ye Tian showed no fear.
"Golden Body Saint Art!"
"Saint Armor Saint Art!"
"Power of Eternity!"
....Layers of defense stacked up, forming a thick Eternal Shield.
Boom!!!! The Projection Sword of the Grand Dawn descended, piercing Ye Tian's Eternal Shield.
"Ancestor Wanfa definitely can't block the Projection Sword of the Grand Dawn!"
Ancestor Quezhan, from afar, said coldly.
Ancestor Xuegang, hidden in the shadows, was also a bit nervous, but he couldn't help Ye Tian.
If Ye Tian weren't just a clone, he would truly be in a panic.
In the eyes of the War Gate, Ye Tian's talent was recognized by all high-ranking members; his future achievements were immense, with a high probability of reaching the Supreme Ancestor level.
The War Gate did not lack Invincible Ancestors, but it specifically lacked Supreme Ancestors.
Whether in the Dark Saint Domain or the Dark Destruction Domain, Supreme Ancestors were extremely rare, truly top-tier existences.
Therefore, in the eyes of the War Gate, one Ye Tian was more precious than ten thousand top-tier powerful Ancestors.
If Ye Tian were to fall, the War Gate's loss would be immense.
Fortunately, it was a clone; if Ye Tian's true body were involved, the War Gate would never allow him to challenge the Ghost Fox Organization like this.
Of course, Ancestor Xuegang also didn't want this clone of Ye Tian to fall here, as it would leave a knot in Ye Tian's heart.
"I hope Ancestor Wanfa can withstand this strike!"
Ancestor Xuegang murmured.
Under everyone's gaze, the Projection Sword of the Grand Dawn collided with the Eternal Shield.
Crack!!!! The Eternal Shield cracked, forming a fissure, but it was merely a crack; the Eternal Shield did not shatter.
"He blocked it!"
Ye Tian breathed a sigh of relief.
Although he had just used the Time Shard Saint Art to glimpse a future scene and knew that the Eternal Shield could block the Projection Sword of the Grand Dawn.
But now that it was truly blocked, he finally relaxed.
"How could he block it? This was a full-power strike from the Projection Sword of the Grand Dawn!"
Ancestor Qingyang was bewildered.
He had planned to heavily injure Ye Tian with one sword, or after killing Ye Tian, immediately unleash the "Fruitless Annihilation" karmic Saint Art to kill Ye Tian's true body across endless territories.
But he never expected that even a full-power strike from the Projection Sword of the Grand Dawn couldn't heavily injure Ye Tian, so the Fruitless Annihilation Saint Art couldn't possibly kill Ye Tian, let alone his true body! "You just attacked me, now it's my turn!"
Ye Tian sneered.
At this moment, Ancestor Qingyang felt a crisis, and it was a death crisis.
"Not good!"
Ancestor Qingyang was greatly alarmed.
Immediately, he wanted to escape.
After all, he had already condensed his Saint Soul; if Ancestor Quezhan hadn't come to find him, he would have stabilized his newly broken-through Saint Soul realm and then proceeded to challenge the Invincible Ancestor realm.
Once he reached the Invincible Ancestor realm and obtained a natal Saint Talent most suitable for him, he could then cultivate a Saint Art most suitable for him, and further cultivate that Saint Art to the perfect realm, or even the extreme realm.
In that case, his strength would reach a terrifying level, and perhaps in a short time, he could even reach the level of the Ten Emperors of the Ghost Fox Organization, not inferior to Ancestor Quezhan.
Therefore, he didn't want to die, at least not in this meaningless battle.
He still had an infinite future, how could he die here! At this moment, he regretted it! If he had known this, he shouldn't have agreed to Ancestor Quezhan's request to take on this mission.
With his status and the qualification of having condensed a Saint Soul, even if he refused, Ancestor Quezhan's anger wouldn't do anything to him.
After all, he was about to reach the Invincible Ancestor realm and would be one of the Ten Emperors in the future. Could Ancestor Quezhan do anything to him? No! Therefore, even if he refused, he would only suffer a minor punishment for now, which wouldn't affect him much.
"Quick, rush into the Thunder Island branch! Ancestor Wanfa won't be able to kill his way in either!"
Ancestor Qingyang said.
"Escape?"
Ye Tian sneered and unleashed the Five Elements Seal.
After his strength greatly increased, Ye Tian's Five Elements Seal became many times more terrifying, instantly sealing the void, making it difficult for Ancestor Qingyang to break through the blockade.
If he could still use the Projection Sword of the Grand Dawn, perhaps he could tear apart the Five Elements Seal with one strike.
But right now, he couldn't continue to use the Projection Sword of the Grand Dawn.
"Eternal Saint Art!"
Ye Tian froze time, and also froze Ancestor Qingyang.
Next, Ye Tian fully unleashed the Void Slash Saint Art.
Poof! The Void Slash Saint Art struck Ancestor Qingyang's body.
At this moment, Ancestor Qingyang finally broke through the Eternal Saint Art and woke up, but he couldn't avoid Ye Tian's Void Slash Saint Art.
With a bang! Ancestor Qingyang was directly sent flying, the power of the Void Slash permeated his body, injuring him, and the injuries were not light.
If it had been before, Ye Tian's Void Slash Saint Art wouldn't have been able to injure Ancestor Qingyang at all.
Ye Tian's strike being able to injure Ancestor Qingyang meant that Ancestor Qingyang was in danger.
Next, Ye Tian went all out, unleashing one Saint Art after another.
Although the same Saint Art could not be cast continuously, casting different Saint Arts consecutively was not affected.
Under the barrage of Saint Arts, Ancestor Qingyang was dazed, his injuries growing heavier and heavier, while his counterattacks couldn't harm Ye Tian.
In this way, Ancestor Qingyang's injuries gradually approached critical levels.
If this continued, Ancestor Qingyang might fall.
Whoosh! An aura of an Invincible Ancestor appeared, and it was extremely terrifying, even stronger than Ancestor Xuegang's aura.
He was Ancestor Quezhan of the Ghost Fox Organization.
As soon as Ancestor Quezhan appeared, Ancestor Xuegang also appeared, fearing that Ancestor Quezhan would attack Ye Tian.
In terms of strength, Ancestor Xuegang was indeed no match for Ancestor Quezhan, and there was even a certain probability that he would be killed by the opponent, but he had to step forward; this was the mission given to him by the Supreme Ancestors of the War Gate.
"Ancestor Quezhan, what are you doing?"
Ancestor Xuegang blocked Ancestor Quezhan and asked.

Chapter 1403: Supreme-level Domain Ancestor Appears!

Chapter 1403: Supreme-level Domain Ancestor Appears
!
"Our Ghost Fox Organization concedes, the challenge ends here!"
Sparrow War Domain Ancestor said angrily.
"Sorry, the challenge cannot just end like that!"
Blood Gang Domain Ancestor shook his head, "Besides, whether the challenge ends or not, I have no right to decide, that's the Myriad Law Domain Ancestor's business!"
Sparrow War Domain Ancestor looked at Ye Tian: "Myriad Law Domain Ancestor, end the challenge immediately!"
The reason he was so eager to end the challenge was because Azure Sun Domain Ancestor was in danger.
Azure Sun Domain Ancestor had condensed a Saint Soul, and a Saint Soul-level supreme Domain Ancestor was too important to the Ghost Fox Organization.
Even if he was displeased with Azure Sun Domain Ancestor, he absolutely dared not let a Saint Soul-level supreme Domain Ancestor die, otherwise, once the leader got angry, he wouldn't be able to bear the wrath.
Therefore, Azure Sun Domain Ancestor could not fall.
Ye Tian heard Sparrow War Domain Ancestor's message, but ignored it, not even pausing his movements, still attacking Sparrow War Domain Ancestor, vowing to kill Sparrow War Domain Ancestor.
As time passed, Sparrow War Domain Ancestor's injuries became increasingly severe.
Just then, Sparrow War Domain Ancestor once again activated the projection sword of the Grand Dawn Sword, but still failed to break through Ye Tian's Eternal Shield.
He even used the Karma Saint Skill 'Fruitless Annihilation', but still couldn't harm Ye Tian.
Karma Saint Skills are very effective against those weaker than oneself, even able to ignore the distance between a clone and the main body, directly slaying the main body.
But if the opponent's strength is greater than one's own, Karma Saint Skills become useless.
Therefore, Karma Saint Skills are also known as the most useless, and also the most terrifying Saint Skill.
Seeing that Azure Sun Domain Ancestor was about to collapse, Sparrow War Domain Ancestor was also very nervous.
But he dared not act, if he did, he could instantly rescue Azure Sun Domain Ancestor, not even Blood Gang Domain Ancestor could stop him.
However, once he did that, the War Gate would have a reason to act.
Perhaps the War Gate wouldn't destroy the Ghost Fox Organization, but killing an invincible Domain Ancestor like him wouldn't be difficult.
"Sparrow War Domain Ancestor, save me!"
Azure Sun Domain Ancestor cried for help.
"You told me to act, now I'm in danger, you can't just stand by and watch me die, and I've condensed a Saint Soul, the leader will protect me once he knows!"
However, no matter how Azure Sun Domain Ancestor pleaded for help, Sparrow War Domain Ancestor dared not act.
"Azure Sun Domain Ancestor, just hold on a little longer, the leader is almost here!"
Sparrow War Domain Ancestor said.
He had already sent a message to the leader, and the leader, upon learning that Azure Sun Domain Ancestor had condensed a Saint Soul, was now rushing over.
He dared not act, but if the leader acted to save Azure Sun Domain Ancestor, even the War Gate wouldn't kill their leader.
Suddenly.
A suppressive aura descended.
At this moment, Blood Gang Domain Ancestor's expression became extremely solemn.
"Could he have come?"
Blood Gang Domain Ancestor said in shock.
This "he" was the leader of the Ghost Fox Organization—Ghost Fox Emperor, Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor, who was also a legendary existence, extremely powerful. Although he couldn't be considered one of the most heaven-defying among Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, he had been a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor for a long time.
Legend has it, he was a descendant of a Progenitor, merely without a Saintly Talent.
Both Supreme-level Domain Ancestors and Progenitors have a certain chance of giving birth to offspring with Saintly Talents, it's just that Progenitors find it more difficult to have offspring.
And Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor was not born to that Progenitor while the latter was in the Progenitor realm, but was one of the many offspring born when the Progenitor was at the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor stage.
Of course, this was a rumor, its authenticity could not be verified.
Blood Gang Domain Ancestor had also never met this... Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor, after all, their circles were different. Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor's circle was that of Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, while Blood Gang Domain Ancestor's circle was limited to Invincible Domain Ancestors.
Therefore, he had never met Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor.
But now, a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor had descended, his aura was very unfamiliar. If not Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor, then who could it be? Crack! The void split open, and an eerily handsome man walked out from nothingness.
He ignored Blood Gang Domain Ancestor, and looked at Ye Tian instead.
With just one glance, Ye Tian felt as if he had been frozen.
At this moment, Blood Gang Domain Ancestor also couldn't help much.
"This battle ends here!"
Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor said.
"No!"
Ye Tian refused.
"You dare to defy me?"
Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor sneered.
"So what if I do?"
Ye Tian said.
He wasn't afraid of Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor, not to mention the War Gate backing him, just the fact that he wasn't his main body right now made him unafraid of Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor.
Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor didn't have Karma Talent, so he probably wouldn't have Karma Saint Skills, therefore, Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor couldn't kill him.
Unless Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor personally went to the Profound Void Saint Realm to kill him, but in that case, the War Gate couldn't possibly ignore it....
.
Therefore, he was fearless.
"You're very bold, do you think I dare not kill you? Even if I really kill you, the War Gate won't care! Do you believe me?"
Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor threatened coldly.
"Ghost Fox, who said our War Gate wouldn't care....
"
A figure descended.
Then, a figure appeared, it was none other than one of the War Gate's Vice-Leaders whom Ye Tian had seen before, the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor—Fire Mark War Ancestor.
"Fire Mark War Ancestor, didn't you go to the Primeval Progenitor Realm?"
Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor frowned, then smiled, "So it's just a clone, your clone only has one-third of your main body's combat power. I didn't expect that while your main body entered the Primeval War Realm, you still sent out a clone to protect this little fellow, it seems your War Gate truly values him greatly! What a pity, only a clone of you has arrived, do you really think you can contend with me with just a clone?"
"Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor, if it weren't for your father, what do you think you are?"
Fire Mark War Ancestor scoffed.
Fire Mark War Ancestor's words also confirmed that Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor was indeed the son of a Progenitor.
At this moment, the rumor was no longer a rumor, but a fact.
"Fire Mark War Ancestor, do you want to fight me?"
Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor asked.
"If you dare to interfere, then I dare to act, even if it's just a clone, suppressing you won't be a problem!"
Fire Mark War Ancestor said disdainfully.
"Hmph, who can't boast? Although you and I haven't fought before, I've been famous longer than you. You're just the weakest of the War Gate's thirteen Vice-Leaders, with just a clone, you're still no match for me!"
Ghost Fox Emperor Ancestor said coldly.

Human Realm.

Chapter 1406: Saint-grade Ore Vein!

Chapter 1406: Saint-grade Ore Vein
!

"A mountain range!"

If it were an ordinary ore vein, it wouldn't emit such fluctuations; it must be extremely precious.
As for what kind of ore vein it was, if it couldn't truly form, he wouldn't be able to discern it.
As time passed, this mountain range gradually revealed itself, transforming into a treasure land, standing firm in this area.
At the same time, many Domain Ancestors also learned about the situation of this ore vein.
"It's a Saint-grade ore vein!"
A Supreme Domain Ancestor exclaimed in shock.
"Saint-grade ore vein!"
Ye Tian was also quite surprised.
The value of a Saint-grade ore vein is far greater than that of a single Saint Artifact; it's truly a treasure mine! The ore materials produced by Saint-grade ore veins can be used to refine Saint Weapons. Many Supreme Domain Ancestors desire to possess a Saint Weapon that suits them. Saint Artifacts specifically for combat are relatively rare, so refining Saint Weapons using ordinary Saint Artifacts combined with Saint-grade materials is the mainstream approach.
However, Saint-grade materials are too scarce. Without Saint-grade materials, using only ordinary materials makes it impossible to transform a Saint Artifact into a Saint Weapon.
One can imagine how high the value of a Saint-grade ore vein is.
For example, a Saint-grade ore vein like the one before them is enough to supply a major power with materials to refine a large number of Saint Weapons, without worrying about a shortage of Saint-grade materials.
One must know that ordinary sects are not qualified to possess a Saint-grade ore vein; only Saint Land-level powers have one.
Moreover, Saint-grade ore veins are not... sustainable ore veins. Once they are depleted, they are truly depleted. Therefore, many Saint Lands may not necessarily have many Saint-grade ore materials.
The many Domain Ancestors did not rush to seize it, because Saint-grade materials are difficult to mine, and even if they fought, it would be a waste of time.
Furthermore, other Domain Ancestors would not simply sit by and watch them slowly mine the Saint-grade ore vein.
More importantly, with the appearance of this Saint-grade ore vein,
in the Saint Realm, the human race would not allow a Saint-grade ore vein to be plundered and mined by others.
"This Saint-grade ore vein belongs to our human race. Everyone, please leave." Ye Tian appeared on the Saint-grade ore vein, addressing the non-human Domain Ancestors.
As for the Domain Ancestors from outside the human race, although they were unaware of Ye Tian sweeping through the Ghost Fox Organization's four-star 44 kings, the matter of Ye Tian previously slaying two four-star experts outside the Human Realm had spread far and wide.
Therefore, knowing how powerful Ye Tian was, they dared not provoke him.
Unless they were Supreme Domain Ancestors ranked among the top of the Ten Great Sacred Sects' Supreme Powerhouses list, they wouldn't dare to contend with Ye Tian even slightly.... otherwise, they wouldn't dare to act presumptuously.
Consequently, these non-human Domain Ancestors retreated one by one, without uttering a single word.
Ye Tian then began to set up a grand formation, enveloping this Saint-grade ore vein to prevent other Domain Ancestors from secretly infiltrating and mining it.
In addition, Ye Tian dispatched dozens of Domain Ancestors to guard this place, including several top-tier Domain Ancestors.
Should anyone intrude here, they would immediately send a message to him, and he would rush over at once.
....Dark Saint Domain, Qingyuan Sacred Land.
Qingyuan Sacred Land is a declining Sacred Land, ranked last among the seventy-two Sacred Lands, and might even have its title as a Sacred Land revoked.
Although there have always been seventy-two Sacred Lands, in reality, it doesn't mean they cannot be replaced; rather, they are frequently replaced.
For instance, if some sects become very powerful and give birth to Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, while the Supreme-level Domain Ancestors of certain Sacred Lands fall, those Sacred Lands will be replaced by such sects.
In the past, Qingyuan Sacred Land was merely a sect, known as Qingyuan Sect. Later, a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor was born, and it seized a Saint Realm, thus entering the ranks of Sacred Lands.
But now, the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor of Qingyuan Sacred Land is severely injured and has been in secluded cultivation for recovery. Furthermore, there are no outstanding powerhouses at the Invincible Domain Ancestor level in Qingyuan Sacred Land.
Apart from that Supreme-level Domain Ancestor, Qingyuan Sacred Land's strength is even inferior to some top-tier sects. The sects ranked among the top few actually conceal Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, but without a Saint Realm as their headquarters, they cannot become Saint Land-level powers.
One Saint Realm and one Supreme-level Domain Ancestor are the two necessary conditions to become a Sacred Land.
One can imagine that once something happens to the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor of Qingyuan Sacred Land, Qingyuan Sacred Land will immediately be expelled from the ranks of Sacred Lands and replaced by those top-tier sects.
Therefore, Qingyuan Sacred Land's situation is extremely perilous, and it has always sought opportunities to strengthen its power.
At this moment, the news of a Saint-grade ore vein being born in the Xuanxu Saint Realm became known to Qingyuan Sacred Land, immediately drawing its attention.
Qingyuan Sacred Land is quite poor among the Sacred Lands. The Saint Realm it possesses is also a resource-scarce Saint Realm, considered an incredibly ancient Saint Realm where resources have been over-mined, and even its origin has been damaged, making it difficult for Saint-grade ore veins to form.
Once they acquire a Saint-grade ore vein, they can forge many Saint Weapons, thereby arming Qingyuan Sacred Land's Invincible Domain Ancestors.
In that case, Qingyuan Sacred Land's strength would directly rise by a notch.
Inside Qingyuan Sacred Land.
An elder of Qingyuan Sacred Land, Elder Qingxu, and the contemporary Sacred Lord of Qingyuan Sacred Land, Sacred Lord Qingfeng, were discussing the matter of the Saint-grade ore vein in the Xuanxu Saint Realm.
"Sacred Lord, a Saint-grade ore vein has appeared in the Xuanxu Saint Realm. Once our Qingyuan Sacred Land obtains this Saint-grade ore vein, our strength will surely greatly increase!"
Elder Qingxu said excitedly.
"Our Qingyuan Sacred Land's strength is too weak; are we qualified to intervene?"
Sacred Lord Qingfeng said worriedly.
"Sacred Lord, rest assured. Those Sacred Sects shouldn't covet a mere Saint-grade ore vein to the extent of fully contending for it. At most, some Domain Ancestors within the Sacred Sects might be interested.
As for other Sacred Lands, they might be wary of the War Sect's strength and might not act immediately.
Therefore, as long as we act quickly and immediately seize this Saint-grade ore vein, and as long as we don't kill any Domain Ancestors from the War Sect, we won't offend the War Sect.
This is an opportunity. We only need to dispatch a few Invincible Domain Ancestors, and then, by understanding our Sacred Land's Saint Artifact—the Qingyuan World Pearl—we can directly sever the void where that Saint-grade ore vein is located, seal it within the Qingyuan World Pearl, and then instantly depart from the Xuanxu Saint Realm."
Elder Qingxu suggested.
"It's a bit risky!"
Sacred Lord Qingfeng hesitated.
"Sacred Lord, this is a great opportunity! If a Saint-grade ore vein appeared in the Dark Saint Domain, where would our chance be? Could it be that the Sacred Lord wishes for our Qingyuan Sacred Land to fall out of the ranks of Sacred Lands?"
Elder Qingxu quickly tried to persuade him.
"Alright, let's do it!"
Sacred Lord Qingfeng gritted his teeth and decided.

Domain Ancestor Mili suggested.

Domain Ancestor Wansheng said.

"Collect!"

"It's a success! Quickly tear through the Profound Void Saint Realm's world barrier and leave!"
Domain Ancestor Wansheng said excitedly.
Human Race, Human Realm.
Ye Tian's main body was cultivating, and the moment the Saint-grade ore vein's formation was broken, he sensed it.

Boom!!!! The void rippled open, and Ye Tian's gaze crossed the void, seeing the two Invincible Domain Ancestors—Domain Ancestor Wansheng and Domain Ancestor Mili.
The Saint-grade ore vein had been taken by them, and at this moment, these two Invincible Domain Ancestors were preparing to break through the world barrier and leave.
If it were an ordinary Saint Realm Lord, they might not have had enough time to stop them, as it would take time to rush there.
Furthermore, a Saint Realm Lord of the Supreme Domain Ancestor level would also be unable to prevent two Invincible Domain Ancestors from leaving.
However, Ye Tian was not an ordinary Saint Realm Lord; he also controlled the Primordial Creation Well, and his degree of control over the Saint Realm was unparalleled.
The Saint-grade ore vein had disappeared, and two Invincible Domain Ancestors appeared there. Clearly, the result was the demise of the Human Race Domain Ancestors guarding the Saint-grade ore vein.
"I didn't expect anyone would actually dare to attack the Saint-grade ore vein!"

This world power far surpassed the level of a Supreme Domain Ancestor; although it was far from enough to kill them, it did obstruct them, preventing them from instantly breaking through the Profound Void Saint Realm's world barrier and leaving.
Bang bang!! Domain Ancestor Wansheng and Domain Ancestor Mili were forcibly knocked down during their attempt to teleport away. "It seems we must face Domain Ancestor Wanfa!"
Domain Ancestor Wansheng and Domain Ancestor Mili frowned.

The Saint-grade ore vein was the most important; they truly couldn't waste time here.

Therefore, Ancestor Mili wasn't worried about not being able to leave.

Ye Tian fully activated the power of the Profound Void Holy Realm to empower himself. At this moment, his strength reached an incredibly terrifying level of amplification.
Through the Time Shard Saint Technique, he glimpsed a corner of the future, knowing that the strength of these two invincible domain ancestors wasn't too terrifying and wouldn't threaten him. Only then did he dare to intercept them; otherwise, he wouldn't have rushed forward so rashly.

Ye Tian instantly sealed the void, blocking Ancestor Mili.
It would be extremely difficult for Ancestor Mili to break through the Five Elements Seal and escape.
After all, he wouldn't give them time to break the Five Elements Seal. Coupled with the effect of the Primordial Well of Creation, Ye Tian could mobilize all the power of the Profound Void Holy Realm, making it even harder for them to leave.

Only top holy lands and the Ten Great Holy Gates possessed many techniques. For invincible domain ancestors like them, acquiring even one Saint Technique was quite good.
Two Azure Wind Giant Hands covered a section of the void, targeting Ye Tian. Such an attack intensity was enough to easily capture any supreme domain ancestor.
If Ye Tian didn't have the Profound Void Holy Realm, he would struggle to contend with these two invincible domain ancestors with his own strength. After all, these two invincible domain ancestors were not weak; although not as strong as Ancestor Xuegang, they could definitely withstand several moves under Ancestor Xuegang's attack.
Ye Tian was confident in killing ordinary invincible domain ancestors, but he couldn't contend with these two invincible domain ancestors.

But as countless invincible domain ancestors found themselves unable to advance to Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, the Dark Holy Domain began to categorize invincible domain ancestors into different tiers.
For example, those closest to Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, almost just one step away from advancing to invincible domain ancestors, these types of invincible domain ancestors possessed incredibly terrifying combat power, known as One-Step Invincible Domain Ancestors. Those slightly weaker in combat power were called Two-Step Invincible Domain Ancestors, and finally, there were Nine-Step Invincible Domain Ancestors.
Under normal circumstances, those who could advance to invincible domain ancestors were all geniuses with strong combat power. As for those invincible domain ancestors who barely advanced using some special treasures, after cultivating to the peak of the invincible domain ancestor realm, they would roughly be... Nine-Step Invincible Domain Ancestors.
And some newly advanced invincible domain ancestors, if their combat power was inferior to a Nine-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor, could only be called ordinary invincible domain ancestors.
And he, as a Five-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor, was already very powerful, yet he was actually injured by a supreme domain ancestor.
This indicated that even if Ye Tian's strength hadn't reached the combat power of a Four-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor, it had definitely reached the combat power of a Five-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor.
Of course, they could also see that Ye Tian was leveraging the power of the Profound Void Holy Realm, but his inherent combat power was definitely not weak either.
"Eternal Saint Technique!"
Time was frozen. Ye Tian, with the fastest speed, slashed at Ancestor Wansheng, directly severing Ancestor Wansheng's head.
However, in an instant, Ancestor Wansheng regenerated his head.
Ancestor Mili and Ancestor Wansheng couldn't injure Ye Tian at all, while any of Ye Tian's attacks could injure both of them.
But an invincible domain ancestor is... an invincible domain ancestor, possessing an invincible domain body, their physical body is practically immortal and indestructible. Even if Ye Tian's strength was great, it would be difficult to obliterate their physical bodies and souls.
As time passed little by little, the injuries of Ancestor Mili and Ancestor Wansheng grew heavier and heavier.
Fight! Fight! Fight! Ye Tian fought like a madman, displaying almost all of his strength, like a terrifying supreme demon god, striking fear into the hearts of both Ancestor Mili and Ancestor Wansheng.
This battle also attracted many domain ancestors. One by one, domain ancestors arrived in this area and witnessed the great battle.
Immediately, they were greatly shocked by Ye Tian's combat power.
"Ancestor Wanfa's strength has actually reached such a level!!!!"
Ancestor Qingyu said in shock.

Saintess Qingyi was also extremely shocked. There was a time when she could still fight Ye Tian, but now the gap between them was too vast.
Although she had now also advanced to a supreme domain ancestor, compared to Ye Tian, she was simply not on the same level.

Chapter 1409: Saint Lord Qingfeng's Plea for Help, Crying Blood Emperor!

Chapter 1409: Saint Lord Qingfeng's Plea for Help, Crying Blood Emperor
!
As time passed, the injuries of Ancestor Mili and Ancestor Wansheng grew heavier.

"Let's call for help!"

Ancestor Wansheng agreed. There was no other way; Ye Tian's Five Elements Seal was too terrifying. While fighting Ye Tian, they couldn't spare attention to break the Five Elements Seal, and they couldn't defeat Ancestor Wanfa in the Profound Void Sacred Realm, so they could only call for help.

Upon learning this news, Saint Lord Qingfeng was very hesitant, unsure of what to do.
Should he rescue them? If he did, he would definitely have to send out top-tier invincible domain ancestors, otherwise, Ancestor Mili and Ancestor Wansheng couldn't be saved at all. Moreover, certain treasures would have to be used, or there wouldn't be enough time for rescue.

This way, they would completely offend Ancestor Wanfa and the War Gate.
Even if the War Gate didn't destroy their Qingyuan Sacred Land, a casual suppression would make life difficult for Qingyuan Sacred Land, and it might even lose its title as a sacred land.
If it lost its sacred land title, other forces would not let Qingyuan Sacred Land off the hook.
By then, Qingyuan Sacred Land would surely be annihilated.
But if they didn't rescue them, Qingyuan Sacred Land would suffer a great loss, not only losing two invincible domain ancestors but also the sacred artifact, the Qingyuan World Pearl.
And once the Qingyuan World Pearl fell into Ancestor Wanfa's hands, if Ancestor Wanfa investigated, he would be able to find out that this sacred artifact, the Qingyuan World Pearl, belonged to Qingyuan Sacred Land.
By then, Qingyuan Sacred Land would still be exposed.
"We must save Ancestor Mili and Ancestor Wansheng, but it cannot be our renowned invincible domain ancestors from Qingyuan Sacred Land!"
Saint Lord Qingfeng thought to himself.
After pondering for a few seconds, he thought of someone.

The Crying Blood Emperor's strength was formidable; he was also a Two-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor.
However, the Crying Blood Emperor was on the wanted lists of multiple Sacred Gates, pursued by invincible domain ancestors and even supreme domain ancestors from the Sacred Gates.
However, the Crying Blood Emperor was extremely difficult to kill. His true form was a river of blood, cultivating into a human form from the blood river and growing to this day. No one knew where his true form was; usually, only his clones were dispatched.
The strength of these clones was inferior to his true form, possessing only the power of a Three-Step Domain Ancestor. But even if a clone fell, it could form another clone after a period of recuperation.
It was precisely because of the unique nature of his clones that he could seize countless opportunities and wasn't afraid of being hunted by others.
For instance, many invincible domain ancestors had killed him many times, but they had only killed his clones.
Only supreme-level domain ancestors proficient in karmic sacred techniques could easily kill the Crying Blood Emperor.
However, the Crying Blood Emperor's clones were not that easy to find, and supreme-level domain ancestors wouldn't idly spend vast amounts of time hunting down an invincible domain ancestor.

Moreover, once humanity produced sacred-weapon-grade artifact refiners, these sacred-grade mineral veins would be of great use.
In short, sacred-grade mineral veins were strategic resources of immense importance to a power.
In the days that followed, the Profound Void Sacred Realm passed through a period of peace.
Ye Tian also continuously cultivated in seclusion, constantly improving his Soul Sacred Light.
However, Soul Sacred Light was difficult to improve. Without great opportunities, the progress speed would be very slow.
In the blink of an eye, a hundred million years passed in the Profound Void Sacred Realm.
For Domain Ancestors, a hundred million years was not that long.
But for humanity, a hundred million years was extremely long.
Now, humanity had changed too much.
Not to mention that the number of human Domain Ancestors had increased dozens of times, even the Supreme Domain Ancestors had reached double digits.
For example, Ye Tian's relatives had basically all stepped into the Supreme Domain Ancestor realm, and several talented geniuses among humanity had also entered the Supreme Domain Ancestor realm.
Besides Supreme Domain Ancestors, humanity also had many more top-tier Domain Ancestors.
The Profound Void Sacred Realm was extremely rich in resources, and there were many opportunities that could help Domain Ancestors break through to the top-tier Domain Ancestor realm. Therefore, if human Domain Ancestors obtained even a few good opportunities, they could break through to the top-tier Domain Ancestor realm.
This led to humanity having a great many top-tier Domain Ancestors, even more than many sects in the Dark Sacred Domain.
In terms of overall strength, humanity was already comparable to the sect-level powers of the Dark Sacred Domain.
At this time, Ye Tian also made some progress, but unfortunately, the progress was not very fast; his Soul Sacred Light only increased by thirty percent.
A hundred million years, and the Soul Sacred Light only increased by thirty percent. This speed was simply too slow compared to his previous progress.
"No wonder those Supreme Domain Ancestors in the Dark Sacred Domain all desire various opportunities, even fighting desperately for a single treasure. The progress from arduous cultivation is simply too slow!"
Ye Tian lamented.

If it were other Supreme Domain Ancestors, a hundred million years would probably only yield a maximum of one percent increase in Soul Sacred Light.
On this day.

At this moment, the War Gate was also ready to open the War Realm Tower at any time, allowing many War Emperors of the War Gate to descend.
Of course, this was a last resort; they would only make this choice if these Holy Sects collectively attacked and besieged them.
"Ancestor Guhai, since we've come, we can't return empty-handed. Give up some slots!"
Ancestor Xuehen from the Dark Holy Sect spoke.
Ye Tian spoke up: "Esteemed Invincible Ancestors, it is possible to get slots, but they must be purchased. It's impossible to obtain them for free.
Even some of the War Gate's top-tier Ancestors must purchase slots if they want them!"
"Purchasing slots, ridiculous!"
Many Invincible Ancestors were very displeased.
If they had to purchase slots, wouldn't their coming here as Invincible Ancestors be a complete waste of time?
Their goal was... to obtain some slots for free; that was their demand.
"Ancestor Wanfa, let me handle this!"
Ancestor Wulei, one of the eight Invincible Ancestors of the War Gate, spoke.
"Then I'll trouble Ancestor Wulei!"
Ye Tian knew very well that his standing was too low; these Invincible Ancestors completely ignored him, and he couldn't threaten them.
In a word, it was still a matter of strength.
If he possessed the combat power of a first-step Invincible Ancestor, and with the help of the Profound Void Holy Realm's power, he should be able to unleash combat power surpassing a first-step Invincible Ancestor, easily suppressing these troublesome Invincible Ancestors.
At that time, who would dare to say another word? "Ancestor Wulei, what do you want to say?"
Ancestor Xuehen said.
Ancestor Wulei was very low-key and rarely made a move, so although others knew that the War Gate had such an Invincible Ancestor, they didn't know much about him.
At this moment, Ancestor Wulei said: "Everyone, in the Dark Forbidden Zone, strength is paramount. If you want to obtain Holy Tablet slots for free, then show your strength. If any of you are confident in defeating me, I can persuade the other seven Invincible Ancestors of the War Gate not to stop you.
But if you lose, then you cannot interfere. How about it?"
"Ancestor Wulei, this..."
Ancestor Guhai and others frowned, feeling that this was simply giving away slots to other Holy Sects for free! Ye Tian didn't speak. He felt that since Ancestor Wulei dared to say this, he must have absolute confidence in himself, otherwise, he would lose face.
Moreover, Ancestor Wulei was far from simple; he was a Sacred Gifted, and possessed three Sacred Gifts, one of which should be his innate Sacred Gift.
Such an Invincible Ancestor was extremely powerful, perhaps having reached the combat power of a first-step Invincible Ancestor.
"Ancestor Wulei, you are too arrogant. Then I shall experience your strength!"
Ancestor Xuehen said.
"Enter my Void Territory to fight, so as not to damage the Profound Void Holy Realm!"
Ancestor Guhai of the War Gate said.
"Alright!"
"Alright!"
Ancestor Wulei and Ancestor Xuehen both agreed.
The Void Territory was a special fragment that could transform into a domain. Fighting within it made it almost impossible to cause significant damage.
Of course, it could also be used to suppress others.
But Ancestor Guhai certainly wouldn't dare to control the Void Territory to suppress Ancestor Xuehen, as that would be a foul.
Just then, Ancestor Guhai flipped his palm, and a small rhombus-shaped fragment appeared.
"Go!"
Ancestor Guhai waved his hand.
This fragment transformed into a vast territory, covering this area, and Ancestor Wulei and Ancestor Xuehen both flew into this Void Territory.

Chapter 1416: Gu Heng, whose Invincible Domain Body underwent three transformations...

Chapter 1416: Gu Heng, the Domain Ancestor whose Invincible Domain Body underwent three transformations
!
The Void Territory.
Five Thunder Domain Ancestor and Blood Scar Domain Ancestor began to fight. Originally, the battle's impact from an Invincible Domain Ancestor would be terrifying, but within the Void Territory, the fluctuations were confined to a certain range.
Blood Scar Domain Ancestor transformed into countless blood-colored figures. This was a special combat avatar, but it couldn't exist for long. However, it was terrifying in battle. If those of the same rank had no way to counter it, they would be instantly killed.
"This is Blood Scar Domain Ancestor's famous Saint Skill—Blood Shadow. It's a Saint Skill he created himself; others cannot learn it!"
Someone commented.
Facing the Blood Shadow Saint Skill, other Two-step Invincible Domain Ancestors would be very solemn. But Five Thunder Domain Ancestor merely smiled faintly, clasped his hands together, and his entire body began to expand, transforming into an earth-shattering Thunder Body.
Countless blood shadows struck Five Thunder Domain Ancestor's Thunder Body. However, countless blood shadows were annihilated by the Thunder Body's thunder power, and the Thunder Body was not shattered.
"No, this isn't the Thunder Extreme Saint Body. The Thunder Extreme Saint Body isn't this powerful!"
Blood Scar Domain Ancestor was dumbfounded.
Soon, he noticed a clue.
"Your Thunder Extreme Saint Body has broken its limits."
Blood Scar Domain Ancestor said solemnly.
If the Saint Body breaks its limits, the Saint Body will gradually transform towards an Ancestral Body.
This is just like Saint Skills; once a Saint Skill breaks its limits, it will transform into an Ancestral Skill.
The same applies to Saint Bodies! However, for a Saint Body to transform into an Ancestral Body, the difficulty is greater. Even if it breaks its limits, it's impossible to transform into an Ancestral Body all at once.
At this moment, Five Thunder Domain Ancestor smiled and said, "Blood Scar Domain Ancestor, my Saint Body is still far from reaching the Ancestral Body realm, but it already possesses a trace of Ancestral Body characteristics, which is the Half-step Ancestral Body realm! With your strength, you probably can't completely break through my Five Thunder Saint Body's defense!"
"Half-step Ancestral Body, impressive. I am indeed not your opponent. You must have reached the combat power of a One-step Invincible Domain Ancestor, right? I am no match!"
Blood Scar Domain Ancestor directly conceded defeat.
In reality, he only possessed the combat power of a Two-step Invincible Domain Ancestor. Although infinitely close to a One-step Invincible Domain Ancestor, he was not yet one.
Blood Scar Domain Ancestor's concession meant that Blood Scar Domain Ancestor would no longer interfere.
"Is there anyone else who wishes to spar?"
Five Thunder Domain Ancestor asked.
"I'll give it a try!"
Mo Xie Domain Ancestor of the Azure Sky Sacred Gate spoke.
"Mo Xie Domain Ancestor, please proceed!"
Five Thunder Domain Ancestor said calmly.
Mo Xie Domain Ancestor flew into the Void Territory, and began to engage Five Thunder Domain Ancestor.
Mo Xie Domain Ancestor was seen holding a black longsword. This was his top-tier Saint Weapon—the Mo Xie Sword. It was specially forged for him by a Supreme-tier Domain Ancestor. Its power was terrifying, comparable to the top hundred weapon-type Saint Artifacts on the Saint Artifact Ranking.
"Ten Thousand Swords!!!"
Countless sword lights slashed towards Five Thunder Domain Ancestor. Each sword light contained immense power.
"One-step Invincible Domain Ancestor!"
Many Invincible Domain Ancestors had previously heard rumors that Mo Xie Domain Ancestor was merely a Two-step Invincible Domain Ancestor. However, the strength he now displayed reached that of a One-step Invincible Domain Ancestor. And not just an ordinary One-step Invincible Domain Ancestor; he had probably already been promoted to a One-step Invincible Domain Ancestor long ago.
"He hides his true depth!"
Many Invincible Domain Ancestors thought to themselves.
At this moment, Five Thunder Domain Ancestor did not sit idly by. Instead, he also unleashed his Saint Skill—Five Thunder Seal! Boom!!!!! Five thunder seals appeared, blasting towards Mo Xie Domain Ancestor's countless sword lights.
Instantly, the Five Thunder Seals and Mo Xie Domain Ancestor's Ten Thousand Swords Saint Skill collided, and both were annihilated in the collision.
Mo Xie Domain Ancestor's sword qi was completely annihilated. However, one of Five Thunder Domain Ancestor's Five Thunder Seals remained. This single Five Thunder Seal tore through space-time, slammed into Mo Xie Domain Ancestor's body, and instantly severely wounded him.
If Invincible Domain Ancestors were truly to fight to the death, it would likely take a very long time.
Therefore, Mo Xie Domain Ancestor would not renege and insist on fighting to the death.
At this moment, he was injured. Furthermore, his strongest attack could not harm Five Thunder Domain Ancestor. This already counted as a loss.
"I concede!"
Mo Xie Domain Ancestor conceded.
"Anyone else?"
Five Thunder Domain Ancestor asked.
Many Invincible Domain Ancestors fell silent. Most of them were Two-step Invincible Domain Ancestors. There were indeed some One-step Invincible Domain Ancestors, but they believed their strength was inferior to Five Thunder Domain Ancestor's. If they forced themselves to fight, they would not only lose but also expose their own strength, which was completely unnecessary.
Just as everyone was about to give up, an Invincible Domain Ancestor spoke.
"Five Thunder Domain Ancestor, I'll challenge you!"
Everyone looked over, only to see that it was an Invincible Domain Ancestor from the Immortal Sacred Gate—Gu Heng Domain Ancestor! Gu Heng Domain Ancestor was very low-key, and his specific strength was unknown.
At this moment, for Gu Heng Domain Ancestor to dare challenge Five Thunder Domain Ancestor, his strength must have definitely reached the combat power of a One-step Invincible Domain Ancestor.
"Gu Heng Domain Ancestor, make your move!"
Five Thunder Domain Ancestor said, still unperturbed.
Gu Heng Domain Ancestor entered the Void Territory, and the aura on his body began to spread.
Rumble!!!!! An incredibly ancient and powerful aura suppressed all ages, far surpassing the momentum of a Two-step Invincible Domain Ancestor.
Moreover, Gu Heng Domain Ancestor's physique was actually filled with supreme majesty. This was not an Invincible Domain Body.
"You've broken the limits of your Domain Body!"
Five Thunder Domain Ancestor was surprised.
"Indeed, I have already broken through the Domain Body's progression, and am transforming towards a Supreme Domain Body. The shackles between Invincible Domain Ancestor and Supreme Domain Ancestor can no longer hinder me.
For an Invincible Domain Ancestor to transform into a Supreme Domain Ancestor, nine transformations are required. And I have already completed three transformations.
You should know what three transformations represent. Although I haven't surpassed the scope of a One-step Invincible Domain Ancestor, I subtly exceed the combat power of a One-step Invincible Domain Ancestor. If you only have the strength you just showed, I'm afraid you won't be able to defeat me!"
Gu Heng Domain Ancestor said.
"Congratulations, Gu Heng Domain Ancestor. It seems your Immortal Sacred Gate is about to produce another Supreme-tier Domain Ancestor!"
Five Thunder Domain Ancestor congratulated.
"Congratulations, Gu Heng Domain Ancestor!"
"Congratulations, Gu Heng Domain Ancestor!"
"Congratulations, Gu Heng Domain Ancestor!"
One after another, Invincible Domain Ancestors offered their congratulations, their tones filled with envy.
Within the Dark Sacred Domain, there was no shortage of Invincible Domain Ancestors whose strength surpassed Gu Heng Domain Ancestor's. There were even monstrous talents whose combat power exceeded that of a One-step Invincible Domain Ancestor. But what did that matter? As long as they couldn't break the limits of the Invincible Domain Body, they couldn't be promoted to a Supreme-tier Domain Ancestor.
An Invincible Domain Ancestor was almost considered the limit of Domain Ancestors. Under normal circumstances, an Invincible Domain Body could hardly break its shackles. This was also why Supreme-tier Domain Ancestors were so rare.
The Sacred Gate also had no good way to help Invincible Domain Ancestors cultivate a Supreme Domain Body. Everything depended on fortuitous encounters, or endless years of grinding.
It could be said that no Invincible Domain Ancestor had a hundred percent certainty of breaking through to the Supreme-tier Domain Ancestor realm. They could only rely on a certain amount of luck.
And now, Gu Heng Domain Ancestor had already broken through the shackles. By cultivating step by step, he could break through to the Supreme Domain Ancestor realm.
At this moment, many Invincible Domain Ancestors looked at Five Thunder Domain Ancestor, eager to know if Five Thunder Domain Ancestor would concede.
However, Five Thunder Domain Ancestor was not flustered in the slightest. Instead, he revealed a smile.
Clearly, Five Thunder Domain Ancestor still had complete confidence in himself.

Chapter 1417: Twenty Percent Soul Holy Light!

Chapter 1417: Twenty Percent Soul Holy Light
!
Gu Heng Domain Ancestor took action; today would be his battle for fame.
He did not believe that even after breaking the shackles of an Invincible Domain Ancestor and transforming his Invincible Domain Body three times, he would still be no match for Five Thunders Domain Ancestor! "Ancient Shaking Punch!"
Gu Heng Domain Ancestor threw a punch toward Five Thunders Domain Ancestor, shaking the entire Void Territory and causing it to tremble incessantly.
If it were an ordinary first-step Invincible Domain Ancestor, they would likely be blown apart if they tried to take this punch head-on.
However, at that moment, a lightning spear appeared in Five Thunders Domain Ancestor's hand. This lightning spear was not a physical weapon but was condensed from a certain type of power.
"A Saint Technique? No, it surpasses Saint Techniques; it's an Ancestral Technique!"
Ye Tian recognized it.
He had previously seen the Supreme Domain Ancestor, Fire Pattern War Ancestor, take action. Fire Pattern War Ancestor had performed an Ancestral Technique, so he recognized the fluctuations of its aura.
The move Five Thunders Domain Ancestor performed clearly contained the aura of an Ancestral Technique; it was obviously... an Ancestral Technique.
Five Thunders Domain Ancestor thrust the lightning spear forward with immense force. In an instant, it shattered Gu Heng Domain Ancestor's Saint Technique, the Ancient Shaking Punch, and broke through his defenses in a single strike, directly piercing through the Invincible Domain Body that Gu Heng had transformed three times.
Pfft! Pfft! Pfft! Gu Heng Domain Ancestor spat out blood repeatedly and retreated rapidly, his face filled with utter horror.
"You... you've comprehended an Ancestral Technique? How is this possible?"
Gu Heng Domain Ancestor said in disbelief.
The other Domain Ancestors were also incredibly shocked, as if all of this was too abnormal.
How many... Supreme Domain Ancestors had never even comprehended a single Ancestral Technique? On what basis did Five Thunders Domain Ancestor manage to do so? For an Invincible Domain Ancestor to master an Ancestral Technique, the difficulty was simply too great!
It was practically harder than breaking through to become a Supreme Domain Ancestor! Gu Heng Domain Ancestor had broken the shackles of an Invincible Domain Ancestor and was destined to become a Supreme Domain Ancestor in the future, which was already impressive. But Five Thunders Domain Ancestor was even more formidable, having mastered an Ancestral Technique while still an Invincible Domain Ancestor. How heaven-defying was that!
"This is Five Thunders Domain Ancestor's Five Thunders Saint Spear. It was originally a Saint Technique. It seems Five Thunders Domain Ancestor has not only pushed his Saint Body past its limits to possess a trace of Ancestral Body characteristics but has also pushed his Saint Technique past its limits, advancing it to the level of an Ancestral Technique!"
Gu Hai Domain Ancestor thought to himself.
He had to admit that he greatly admired Five Thunders Domain Ancestor; at the very least, he could not achieve this himself.
Having mastered an Ancestral Technique, Five Thunders Domain Ancestor's strength had already broken the limits of a first-step Invincible Domain Ancestor. His combat power was even comparable to a weaker Supreme Domain Ancestor.
Gu Heng Domain Ancestor was naturally no match for Five Thunders Domain Ancestor. If they truly fought to the death, he would likely be killed directly.
"I concede!"
Gu Heng Domain Ancestor said helplessly.
With Gu Heng Domain Ancestor's surrender, the other Invincible Domain Ancestors did not dare to challenge Five Thunders Domain Ancestor either.
The Dark Saint Domain certainly possessed Invincible Domain Ancestors who could rival Five Thunders Domain Ancestor, but none were present here.
"Five Thunders Domain Ancestor won!"
Ye Tian breathed a sigh of relief.
Now, these Invincible Domain Ancestors had no way to pressure the Human Race or forcibly seize the Saint Tablet slots.
"Thank you, Five Thunders Domain Ancestor!"
Ye Tian felt...
"Just doing my duty!"
Five Thunders Domain Ancestor said indifferently.
The Invincible Domain Ancestors of the various major powers did not dare to act recklessly. Those Paramount Domain Ancestors who wanted Saint Tablet slots could only purchase them.
Consequently, one by one, the Paramount Domain Ancestors of the Saint Gates almost exhausted their entire fortunes, and some even had to borrow resources and treasures from Invincible Domain Ancestors to barely afford a single Saint Tablet slot.
It could be said that Ye Tian made a huge profit this time!
Because the price Ye Tian set was too high, many Paramount Domain Ancestors were unwilling to buy and could only choose to give up.
In the end, Ye Tian found that out of the 100 Saint Tablet slots, quite a few were still left. He distributed some to the War Gate, giving them to several Invincible Domain Ancestors of the War Gate for them to allocate, which served as a form of repayment to them.
The remaining Saint Tablet slots were given by Ye Tian to a newly selected group of Domain Ancestors from the Human Race.
Just like that, all the Saint Tablet slots were fully distributed.
Afterward.
Ye Tian entered one of the Saint Tablet worlds he had selected and began to refine the world core.
Before long, the refinement of the world core was complete.
"Close the world entrance!"
With a thought from Ye Tian, the world entrance closed. This way, outsiders would not be able to enter unless they broke the Saint Tablet.
However, the Saint Tablet was incredibly sturdy. Unless one possessed the power to shatter the Profound Void Saint Realm, it was impossible to break the Saint Tablet.
Only an Invincible Domain Ancestor like Five Thunders Domain Ancestor had a hope of breaking the Saint Tablet; almost no other Invincible Domain Ancestor could do it.
Therefore, going into seclusion here was very safe, with no worries about being disturbed.
The Saint Tablet world was like a starry sky, and Ye Tian sat cross-legged there to begin his cultivation.
Wisps of starlight fell into Ye Tian's soul, helping him temper the Soul Holy Light.
This starlight was naturally not actual starlight but the power of the Saint Tablet, which aided in tempering the Soul Holy Light.
"The cultivation speed is so fast!"
Ye Tian was overjoyed.
Immediately, he circulated the Endless Domain Law, frantically tempering his soul and continuously generating Soul Holy Light.
Furthermore, in this place, his comprehension would also receive a significant boost.
"No wonder everyone wants to enter the Saint Tablet world. The benefits of cultivating here are too numerous. Even a third-tier Paramount Domain Ancestor who comes here to cultivate could eventually become a first-tier Invincible Domain Ancestor!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Day after day passed, and Ye Tian's Soul Holy Light continued to be born, increasing in quantity.
Initially, Ye Tian's entire soul had only a small amount of Soul Holy Light, but now the Soul Holy Light gradually covered the surface of his soul, already occupying a certain proportion.
In the blink of an eye, 300,000 years had passed.
After such a long period of bitter cultivation, Ye Tian's Soul Holy Light had increased greatly.
"Soul Holy Light covering one-fifth of the soul!"
Ye Tian looked into his soul sea at the Soul Holy Light that covered one-fifth of his soul and was immediately very satisfied.
It could be said that his Soul Holy Light had increased tenfold during this cultivation session.
Previously, when he cultivated bitterly on his own without the help of the Saint Tablet world for a hundred million years, he had only barely increased the original total amount of Soul Holy Light by thirty percent. But now it was tenfold, showing how effective the Saint Tablet world was.
Soul Holy Light covering one-fifth of the soul was equivalent to twenty percent Soul Holy Light. Moreover, his twenty percent Soul Holy Light was likely stronger than the Saint Soul of an ordinary Paramount Domain Ancestor; after all, his soul was too powerful.
Unfortunately, having cultivated to this extent, it was difficult for the Soul Holy Light to grow further because the boost from the Saint Tablet world now had a very average effect on him.
In terms of strength, Ye Tian's current power was much greater than in the past. After all, with the massive increase in Soul Holy Light, his strength naturally skyrocketed.
"A single Saint Tablet world can only allow my Soul Holy Light to grow to twenty percent. At this rate, tempering will become harder and harder later on. I'm afraid I'll need seven or eight Saint Tablet worlds, or even more, before my soul can completely transform into a Saint Soul!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Furthermore, the same Saint Tablet could only provide an effect once. For example, if he were to go to another Saint Tablet world within this same Saint Tablet, it would be of no use. In fact, the 100 Saint Tablet worlds of this Saint Tablet were all essentially the same.
"There are very few Saint Tablets in the Dark Saint Domain, and the slots for many Saint Tablet worlds have long since been used up. With my status, obtaining one Saint Tablet world slot from the War Gate is likely the... limit. Expecting to condense a Saint Soul with the help of Saint Tablets is probably a pipe dream!"
Ye Tian shook his head.
Therefore, he had to rely on other opportunities to have any hope of condensing a Saint Soul!
