Chapter 1418: Sealing Off the Profound Void Sacred Realm!

Chapter 1418: Sealing Off the Profound Void Sacred Realm
!
The Profound Void Sacred Realm held many opportunities, and as time passed, even more would be born in the future.
If the Profound Void Sacred Realm were to become an Ancestral Realm, the opportunities would be even greater, potentially even giving birth to opportunities and treasures helpful to Ancestors.
However, it would take time for the Profound Void Sacred Realm to grow. It was unknown how many ages it would take for the current Sacred Realm to evolve into an Ancestral Realm, and Ye Tian could not wait forever; that would be far too long.
He wanted to use opportunities to condense a Sacred Soul, and he could not rely on the Profound Void Sacred Realm for that; he had to seek out new opportunities.
In the blink of an eye, another million years passed.
By this time, the effects of the Sacred Tablet World had become mediocre for many Domain Ancestors, and for some, it had almost no effect at all.
Aside from the Domain Ancestors of the Human Race, many Domain Ancestors from other factions had left the Sacred Tablet World.
For instance, Saintess Qingyi and others had left the Profound Void Sacred Realm and returned to the Dark Sacred Domain.
For them, continuing to stay in the Profound Void Sacred Realm was undoubtedly a waste of time, as the Sacred Tablet was almost the greatest opportunity a Sacred Realm could offer; any subsequent opportunities would be quite ordinary.
.
They had no idea that the Profound Void Sacred Realm could be promoted to an Ancestral Realm, and thus they had no further expectations for it, naturally choosing not to stay.
The Domain Ancestors of the Battle Gate also left one by one, and even the eight Invincible Domain Ancestors of the Battle Gate departed.
After all, there was no longer any necessity for them to remain, and there were many matters to attend to in the Dark Sacred Domain, as well as opportunities that belonged to them there. It was already quite impressive that they had stayed in the Profound Void Sacred Realm for so long.
Over the next few hundred thousand years, the Domain Ancestors of other factions were almost entirely gone, with only a few remaining in the Profound Void Sacred Realm.
The Human Realm.
Ye Tian was currently listening to a report from the Sacred Hall.
"Lord Myriad Law Domain Ancestor, this is the progress report for the Human Race's Domain Ancestors!"
Blue Universe Domain Ancestor, a newly promoted Supreme Domain Ancestor of the Human Race and one of the guardians of the Sacred Hall, reported.
Ye Tian looked it over and was very satisfied with the progress of the Human Race's Domain Ancestors.
The Human Race now possessed approximately one million Domain Ancestors, over thirty thousand top-tier Domain Ancestors, and five hundred Supreme Domain Ancestors. All five hundred of these individuals had been promoted through the Sacred Tablet World.
In the Sacred Tablet World, their soul tempering speed was very fast, and their progress was immense. Coupled with a lack of shortage in cultivation resources and the fact that the Sacred Tablet World could amplify their cultivation speed, they were able to promote to Supreme Domain Ancestors one by one.
With 500 Supreme Domain Ancestors, ordinary sects did not even have such a scale.
Some weaker sects only had a few dozen Supreme Domain Ancestors and one or two Invincible Domain Ancestors, and that was it.
One could imagine how great the Human Race's current progress was.
Having grown so much in such a short time, the Human Race now had the capability to completely control the Profound Void Sacred Realm.
On this day.
In the Human Sacred Hall, Ye Tian gathered several hundred Supreme Domain Ancestors and held a Human Race meeting.
One by one, the Supreme Domain Ancestors of the Human Race arrived, each filled with curiosity, not knowing what this meeting would be about.
Boom!!!!! Ye Tian descended into the Sacred Hall, his gaze sweeping over the Supreme Domain Ancestors.
"This meeting is regarding the control of the Profound Void Sacred Realm. The Profound Void Sacred Realm is now our Human Race's territory, but because there weren't many Human Domain Ancestors before, and there were many Domain Ancestors from other factions in the Daoshan Territory, we couldn't completely seal off the Profound Void Sacred Realm.
But now, with a million Human Domain Ancestors, I propose sealing off the Profound Void Sacred Realm, just like those Sacred Lands and Sacred Gates in the Dark Sacred Domain; outsiders are not permitted to enter the headquarters."
Ye Tian proposed.
At this moment, Qinghe Domain Ancestor, one of the Human Race's Supreme Domain Ancestors, spoke up: "Lord Myriad Law Domain Ancestor, once we seal off the Profound Void Sacred Realm, other factions will surely resist. Moreover, the Battle Realm Tower in the Profound Void Sacred Realm is a place of opportunity for many Domain Ancestors and Half-step Domain Ancestors. If we seal the Profound Void Sacred Realm and they cannot enter the Battle Realm Tower, I fear they will unite to suppress our Human Race in the regions outside the Profound Void Sacred Realm!"
Ye Tian smiled and said: "They won't dare to suppress us; they barely have any Supreme Domain Ancestors, so how would they dare suppress our Human Race.
Furthermore, I am not forbidding them from entering the Battle Realm Tower.
We can open a world passage directly to the Battle Realm Void, which will remain a public area.
Except for the Battle Realm Void, all other places will be sealed, and outsiders will not be permitted to enter.
I am doing this for the sake of the Human Race. Otherwise, when treasures are born in the future, other factions will come to snatch them, and it might even attract Domain Ancestors from the Dark Sacred Domain, which would not be a good thing.
If we seal the Profound Void Sacred Realm, other Domain Ancestors will have no way to perceive what treasures have been born here. Even if an astounding opportunity appears, it will belong only to our Human Race!"
"I agree with Lord Myriad Law Domain Ancestor's suggestion!"
"I agree as well!"
"Agreed!"
Many Supreme Domain Ancestors were in full agreement. Many opportunities originally belonged to the Human Race, only to be snatched away by Domain Ancestors of other factions, which had left them quite frustrated.
Previously, it was because the Human Race's strength was weak and they had no choice.
But now, the Domain Ancestors of the Dark Sacred Domain were almost all gone, and those remaining were mostly weaklings. Therefore, they had the strength to seal off the Profound Void Sacred Realm and monopolize the various future opportunities of the realm.
With the majority of the Domain Ancestors in agreement, Ye Tian issued the order.
At the same time, Ye Tian began to utilize the power of the Profound Void Sacred Realm to construct massive arrays in various parts of the realm to seal it off. Even a Supreme Domain Ancestor would not be able to easily enter the Profound Void Sacred Realm.
Soon, many Domain Ancestors from the Daoshan Territory began to send messages to Ye Tian.
"Alliance Leader, why are we no longer allowed to enter the Profound Void Sacred Realm?"
"Alliance Leader, why are you driving us Domain Ancestors out of the Profound Void Sacred Realm?"
"Alliance Leader, such actions by the Human Race are a bit excessive!"
....Regarding the messages from these Domain Ancestors, Ye Tian had only one sentence: This is my command! No matter how dissatisfied or angry those Domain Ancestors were, Ye Tian continued to execute the plan.
There was no other way; others did not know the situation of the Profound Void Sacred Realm, but Ye Tian knew it very well.
The Profound Void Sacred Realm was constantly growing, and it was feared that even more opportunities would be born in the future. If the realm were not sealed, this secret would likely leak out.
Originally, the Sacred Tablet was the greatest opportunity of a Sacred Realm, but for the Profound Void Sacred Realm, the Sacred Tablet was definitely not its greatest opportunity.
Therefore, taking advantage of the departure of the Dark Sacred Domain's Domain Ancestors, he quickly sealed the Profound Void Sacred Realm so that opportunities would not leak out. Even if more great opportunities were born, it would remain an internal matter for the Human Race.
As time slowly passed, after Ye Tian had completely sealed the Profound Void Sacred Realm, other Domain Ancestors were unable to enter.
At first, they made a fuss, but they gradually came to accept it.
Additionally, there were some opportunities in the Daoshan Territory itself, and even quite a few natural domain worlds and precious treasure lands were born, which also attracted the attention of these Domain Ancestors.
In this way, another few million years passed.
On this day.
A message came from the Battle Gate that made Ye Tian extremely excited.

Chapter 1419: The Second Sacred Monument Slot!

Chapter 1419: The Second Sacred Monument Slot
!
"The Primordial Ancestral Realm has come to a close!"
Ye Tian received this news from the War Gate.
After such a long time, the ten Supreme Sacred Gates and numerous Sacred Lands had maneuvered against one another—essentially a game played between the Sacred Gates—and a final result had been reached.
As for what that result was, Ye Tian wasn't entirely clear.
In truth, there wasn't much he understood about the specifics.
He only knew that after the Holy War, the War Gate had obtained many slots to enter the Primordial Ancestral Realm. However, having entry slots only represented an increased opportunity to obtain treasures; it didn't guarantee that one would actually acquire a massive amount of them.
For instance, some factions might only send in one person, but if that person was strong enough, they could still obtain many treasures.
But if there were many people, working together also provided sufficient standing.
However, judging by the tone of several Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, the War Gate's harvest was quite substantial.
Yet, one Invincible Domain Ancestor had fallen, and three Supreme-level Domain Ancestors were heavily injured.
The fallen Invincible Domain Ancestor was also one of the Thirty-Six War Emperors, with strength second only to the Five Thunders Domain Ancestor. Falling in the Primordial Ancestral Realm was simply an unpredictable turn of events.
Perhaps before long, the War Gate would select a new Second-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor to be ranked among the Thirty-Six War Emperors.
These matters had nothing to do with Ye Tian. What he cared about was another matter—an opportunity belonging to the Primordial Ancestral Realm.
This opportunity was reserved for Paramount Domain Ancestors; only Paramount Domain Ancestors were permitted to enter. If the opportunity was sufficient, it would be enough for Ye Tian to condense a Sacred Soul.
This opportunity was a special world within the Primordial Ancestral Realm—the Sacred Soul Realm! The Sacred Soul Realm was a unique world capable of birthing a type of creature called Sacred Soul Beasts. Once a Sacred Soul Beast was hunted, one could absorb Sacred Soul power to strengthen their own Sacred Soul.
These Sacred Soul Beasts could not be taken out of the Sacred Soul Realm; they could only be born there due to the realm's unique laws.
Additionally, the Sacred Soul Realm produced many treasures and even Sacred Items. Almost all Sacred Items born in the Sacred Soul Realm were soul-type Sacred Items. When paired with a Sacred Soul, they could unleash terrifying soul attacks to annihilate an enemy's soul.
For example, the Ice Crystal Snow Lotus Fruit that Ye Tian had consumed previously was a treasure that could also be found within the Sacred Soul Realm.
It was easy to imagine that the Sacred Soul Realm was an ultimate treasure land for Paramount Domain Ancestors.
However, the Primordial Ancestral Realm only opened once in a very long age, and the Sacred Soul Realm would only open along with it.
Previously, many Paramount Domain Ancestors had been striving to strengthen their Soul Sacred Light precisely to prepare for entering the Sacred Soul Realm.
Otherwise, so many factions wouldn't have sent their Paramount Domain Ancestors into the Sacred Monument Worlds of the Profound Void Sacred Realm to strengthen their Soul Sacred Light and increase their power.
The stronger one's power, the better their chances of survival upon entering the Sacred Soul Realm.
Moreover, many Sacred Soul-level Paramount Domain Ancestors from the ten Sacred Gates had likely been suppressing their cultivation, refusing to break through to the Invincible Domain Ancestor realm, just to prepare for this opportunity in the Sacred Soul Realm.
Ye Tian didn't dare claim his strength was the absolute strongest. After all, there were many monstrous geniuses in the Dark Sacred Territory, such as those with Sacred Talents who had already condensed Sacred Souls, coupled with the gifts bestowed by their parents.
They possessed many trump cards and startling secret treasures.
Consequently, they also posed a threat to Ye Tian.
However, once he condensed a Sacred Soul, his strength would skyrocket, and he would fear nothing! "When the Sacred Soul Realm opens, I must go. It's useless for a clone to go and improve Soul Sacred Light; if the main body doesn't improve, my cultivation still won't progress!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
This was also a flaw of the duplicated bodies. If a duplicated body improved its cultivation and the main body improved along with it, how wonderful that would be! However, such things could only be wished for.
Ye Tian needed to head to the Primordial Ancestral Realm. With his main body away from the Profound Void Sacred Realm, he was worried about the safety of the humans there.
Thus, Ye Tian withdrew his duplicated body from the War Ancestral World and then condensed a duplicated body again within the Profound Void Sacred Realm.
This way, the duplicated body would guard the Profound Void Sacred Realm, while his main body left the Profound Void Sacred Realm to head toward the Dark Sacred Territory.
Ye Tian didn't use those treasures for rapid travel. In fact, he could easily afford them, but there was no need to use them.
He spent tens of thousands of years traveling to reach the Dark Sacred Territory and arrived at the War Ancestral World.
There was still some time before the Sacred Soul Realm opened; otherwise, many Paramount Domain Ancestors who were still roaming the Dark Forbidden Territory would also need time to return.
Ye Tian took advantage of this time to enter various treasure lands of the War Gate. Although he had entered these places before, it had always been with a duplicated body, meaning the cultivation gains were essentially wasted.
But now that his main body was here, the cultivation improvements were real and solid!
In the blink of an eye, another several hundred thousand years passed.
By this time, Ye Tian's Soul Sacred Light had improved further, now accounting for roughly twenty-one percent of his total soul.
Such an improvement was quite fast, but it was achieved with the help of many treasure lands and numerous resources. Going forward, many of the War Gate's treasure lands would no longer be of much use to him.
On this day.
An order was issued by the War Gate: Ye Tian's application for a Sacred Monument slot had been approved.
The War Gate governed over a dozen Sacred Realms in total. Combined with the Sacred Monuments in the Ancestral Realm, they possessed quite a few Sacred Monuments. However, over the long ages, the Sacred Monument slots had naturally been carved up until not many remained.
It was also because Ye Tian had previously contributed many slots from the Profound Void Sacred Realm's Sacred Monument to the War Gate that his application was approved this time, though he only obtained one Sacred Monument slot.
This Sacred Monument slot was located in the Red Maple Sacred Realm under the War Gate's jurisdiction. This Sacred Realm was born five Domain Eras ago.
A Domain Era is the time from the birth of an ordinary domain to its Great Destruction, roughly equivalent to one hundred million universe years—a universe year being the lifespan of an ordinary universe.
From this, one could imagine how long five Domain Eras were.
After such a long time, the Sacred Monument slots of the Red Maple Sacred Realm had not yet been exhausted; only three slots remained.
And now, Ye Tian was taking one of them.
The War Gate gave this slot to Ye Tian in the hope that he could increase his strength before entering the Sacred Soul Realm, thereby obtaining more benefits within it.
It would still be a long time before the Sacred Soul Realm opened, so there was enough time for Ye Tian to cultivate in the Red Maple Sacred Realm's Sacred Monument World for a long period.
After entering the Red Maple Sacred Realm, Ye Tian entered its Sacred Monument World and began his cultivation.
Just like that, tens of millions of years passed.
By this time, Ye Tian's Soul Sacred Light had increased significantly.
"The Soul Sacred Light now occupies thirty-three percent of the soul!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Improving from twenty-one percent to thirty-three percent was a massive leap. Although it seemed small compared to his previous progress, it was normal. After all, the stronger the Soul Sacred Light became, the harder it was to increase it further.
If the rate of improvement remained the same, wouldn't four or five Sacred Monument Worlds be enough for a Paramount Domain Ancestor to birth a Sacred Soul? That was impossible!
With a soul as powerful as Ye Tian's, if he wanted to completely transform his soul and birth a Sacred Soul, he would likely need dozens of Sacred Monument Worlds, or even more.
In other words, if not for the opportunity of the Sacred Soul Realm, he would likely need an endless amount of time to birth a Sacred Soul.
It had to be said that Ye Tian's luck was good, as he happened to encounter the opening of the Primordial Ancestral Realm's Sacred Soul Realm!

Chapter 1420: The Primordial Ancestor Emerges!

Chapter 1420: The Primordial Ancestor Emerges
!
The Red Maple Holy Realm's Holy Stele World no longer had any effect on Ye Tian, so he emerged from seclusion and returned to the War Ancestor Realm.
He inquired and found that the opening date for the Holy Soul Realm had not yet been decided.
After all, to the Supreme-level Domain Ancestors and even the Primordial Ancestors of the Holy Gates, a mere tens of millions or even hundreds of millions of years was nothing more than the time it took to take a nap.
In this way, another few million years passed before the opening date of the Holy Soul Realm was finally set.
"Eight million years from now!"
This was the time now decided.
At this moment, the Ten Great Holy Gates and a few Holy Lands were all preparing, planning to send some Peak Domain Ancestors into the realm. However, in reality, many Holy Lands were unwilling to send people in, because if a disciple fell, the loss would be devastating.
And the possibility of such a fall was very high.
Although the Holy Soul Realm held countless opportunities, if one could not survive, no amount of opportunity would matter! Therefore, those Holy Lands did not force their disciples to enter the Holy Soul Realm; if a disciple truly wanted to enter, they would be given a slot, but if they didn't want to, they didn't have to go.
Of course, if one's luck was good, it was truly possible to obtain great benefits.
But the probability of such good luck was far too low! In the blink of an eye, eight million years passed.
On this day, the Fire-Pattern War Ancestor notified Ye Tian and the other Peak Domain Ancestors that the Holy Soul Realm had opened.
In the War Ancestor Realm, at a world entrance:
A massive warship was docked there. When Ye Tian arrived, he felt a terrifying aura emanating from the ship, making him feel like a mortal facing a terrifying prehistoric beast.
"Domain Ancestor Wanfa, this is our War Gate's Emperor-grade warship—the Green Dragon Ship. The power of this warship alone can reach the level of a One-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor.
It is a warship forged by the Primordial Ancestors. It is said to have been crafted using the bones of Supreme-level creatures, which is why it retains a trace of the pressure of a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor creature!"
Qingyu Domain Ancestor introduced.
"So that's how it is!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Whoosh! Whoosh! Whoosh!!! One by one, the Peak Domain Ancestors flew into the warship, and Ye Tian also entered the vessel.
They needed to use this Green Dragon Ship to travel to the Primordial Ancestral Realm.
The location of the Primordial Ancestral Realm was no ordinary place; it was a highly dangerous forbidden zone. Even an ordinary Invincible Domain Ancestor could not travel to the Primordial Ancestral Realm and might accidentally perish within the forbidden zone.
Therefore, these Peak Domain Ancestors could not possibly fly to the Primordial Ancestral Realm on their own, but by taking the Green Dragon Ship, they could reach it with ease.
This time, a total of over a thousand Peak Domain Ancestors from the War Gate were heading to the Primordial Ancestral Realm. Every Peak Domain Ancestor was an elite, but with so many entering the Primordial Ancestral Realm, many would likely perish—not just from the dangers within the Holy Soul Realm, but more so from the dangers posed by other factions.
In the Holy Soul Realm, where there were no restraints, ancestors would likely slaughter each other frequently. Thus, if one's strength was insufficient, encountering Peak Domain Ancestors from other factions would certainly lead to a fight.
On the Green Dragon Ship.
The Peak Domain Ancestors sat cross-legged one by one, when they suddenly heard the voice of the Fire-Pattern War Ancestor.
"After entering the Holy Soul Realm, watch out for the Peak Domain Ancestors of the Taboo Holy Gate, the Darkness Holy Gate, the All Things Holy Gate, and the Firmament Holy Gate. Once you encounter Peak Domain Ancestors from these four Holy Gates, kill any that you are able to kill. You must also be wary of disciples from other Holy Gates. You are not permitted to kill each other, understood?"
"Yes, Lord Fire-Pattern War Ancestor!"
The many Peak Domain Ancestors nodded in response.
Soon, the Peak Domain Ancestors of the War Gate, riding the Green Dragon Ship, crossed a vast distance and entered a forbidden zone of the Dark Holy Territory—the Primordial Forbidden Zone.
This Primordial Forbidden Zone contained terrifying killing intent. As the Green Dragon Ship entered, countless killing strikes hammered against it, but they were all blocked by the ship.
Before long, the Green Dragon Ship entered the central area of the forbidden zone.
Here, a safe zone had long since been carved out by the Primordial Ancestors.
Soon, Ye Tian and the others flew out from the Green Dragon Ship and landed in this safe area.
"Is that the Primordial Ancestral Realm?"
Ye Tian gazed at an incredibly massive world in the distance. This world was even larger than the War Ancestor Realm; it was naturally the Primordial Ancestral Realm.
However, this Primordial Ancestral Realm was marked by three cracks. These three cracks ran through the entire Primordial Ancestral Realm, and it was only thanks to the realm's inherent strength that it had not disintegrated.
The aura of the Primordial Ancestral Realm was much stronger than that of the War Ancestor Realm, and its aura was incredibly violent, exerting immense pressure.
Furthermore.
The Primordial Ancestral Realm seemed to have no entrance whatsoever, and it didn't even allow for divine sense investigation.
When Ye Tian's divine sense extended toward it, it was blocked by a terrifying power. This power seemed to transcend his scope of understanding; likely even a One-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor would find it difficult to tear through this power.
"I suppose only Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, or even Primordial Ancestors, can send us in!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
The War Gate was not the first faction to enter this place; several other Holy Gates had already arrived.
Subsequently, several more Holy Gate Domain Ancestors arrived.
Then, the Peak Domain Ancestors of the Holy Lands arrived under the escort of their Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, though some Holy Lands were not qualified to enter this place.
After about several years, all the factions had finally gathered.
"Let it open!"
One Supreme-level Domain Ancestor after another spoke.
Everyone's tone was quite unpleasant. After all, they had likely all fought each other not long ago, and some factions had lost many Domain Ancestors; who would have a pleasant tone? Suddenly.
A massive claw, comparable in size to a small domain, emerged and tore through the invisible barrier outside the Primordial Ancestral Realm.
As this claw emerged, the Supreme-level Domain Ancestors all took on solemn expressions and retreated repeatedly, fearing they might be caught in the aftermath.
"A Primordial Ancestor!"
This thought surfaced in everyone's mind.
Only a Primordial Ancestor could possess such terrifying strength, and the entity was likely not a humanoid Primordial Ancestor.
"Is it that Primordial Ancestor from the Taboo Holy Gate?"
Ye Tian speculated.
Next, another Primordial Ancestor made a move, breaking through the world barrier of the Primordial Ancestral Realm with a single finger.
Following that, a staff was thrust directly into the Primordial Ancestral Realm, forming a passage that connected to the Holy Soul Realm within.
"Let these juniors enter!"
A series of voices filled with supreme majesty permeated the air.
These were the voices of the Primordial Ancestors.
"Yes!"
The many Supreme-level Domain Ancestors responded in unison.
Before Ye Tian could even react, a terrifying force lifted him and carried him through the passage, entering the Holy Soul Realm.

Chapter 1421: All Holy Soul Beasts Have Holy Talents!!!!

Chapter 1421: All Holy Soul Beasts Have Holy Talents
!!!!
The Holy Soul Realm.
One by one, the Supreme Domain Ancestors shuttled in, but because it was a random teleportation, everyone's landing location was different.
Ye Tian appeared in a forest within the Holy Soul Realm. He was the only Supreme Domain Ancestor around, and he didn't sense the presence of any others.
Clearly, he was quite far from the other Supreme Domain Ancestors.
Boom!!!! A powerful aura flew in from the distance.
"A top-tier Domain Ancestor-level creature!"
Ye Tian sensed it.
"Copy Talent, Investigate!"
Race: Holy Soul Wolf Race
Bloodline Talent: Supreme Grade
Source Power Talent: Super God-level Limit
Source Body Talent: Super God-level Limit
Source Speed Talent: Super God-level Limit
Holy Talent: Colossal Strength
....From the investigation of his Copy Talent, this Holy Soul Wolf possessed a Holy Talent.
"What's going on?"
Ye Tian was stunned.
Why did this Holy Soul Wolf have a Holy Talent? Could it be the descendant of a Transcendent Domain Ancestor? "No, the Holy Soul Realm has opened more than once, and there are no Transcendent Domain Ancestors here. Otherwise, the Primordial Ancestors wouldn't dare let us juniors in!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Therefore, the Holy Soul Beasts here were, at their weakest, merely at the level of powerful Invincible Domain Ancestors; there wouldn't be any Transcendent Domain Ancestors.
So, how could Holy Soul Beasts with Holy Talents be born here? "Strange, so strange!"
Ye Tian muttered.
Of course, there were too many mysteries in the Dark Forbidden Zone. As the first ancestral realm of the Dark Holy Domain, it was normal for the Primordial Ancestral Realm to have some special circumstances.
"Copy Colossal Strength Holy Talent!"
Ye Tian succeeded.
Immediately, with a wave of his hand, the Golden Silk Holy Technique tore through the Holy Soul Wolf's body, killing it instantly.
A... Holy Soul Wolf with a Holy Talent had fallen. If this were the outside world, the death of such a... Holy Talent possessor would likely cause an earth-shattering sensation.
But here, it didn't cause a single ripple.
Upon the beast's death, a wisp of Holy Soul Power surged into Ye Tian's body and was absorbed by his soul.
Ye Tian then began to refine this Holy Soul Power, strengthening his Soul Holy Light.
A few months later, Ye Tian had completely refined the Holy Soul Power, and his Soul Holy Light had grown slightly stronger.
"It really works. If I kill enough Holy Soul Beasts, the progress of my Soul Holy Light will be very fast. In this Holy Soul Realm, I might actually be able to fully condense a Holy Soul!"
Ye Tian muttered.
Whoosh! Ye Tian shuttled through the air and soon discovered another... Holy Soul Beast. This one was stronger, at the level of a Supreme Domain Ancestor, and it also possessed a Holy Talent.
[Holy Talent: Meteor] This was a speed-type Holy Talent.
"Copy Meteor Holy Talent!"
Ye Tian succeeded and also slew this Holy Soul Beast.
Afterward, he absorbed the Holy Soul Power from the dead beast to strengthen his Soul Holy Light.
It had to be said that a Holy Soul Beast at the Supreme Domain Ancestor level contained more Holy Soul Power, and the effect was better.
But at this moment, Ye Tian was still puzzled as to why both Holy Soul Beasts he encountered had Holy Talents. "Could it be that the Holy Soul Beasts are a race of Holy Talents?"
Ye Tian thought.
If that were the case, he could copy countless Holy Talents. Moreover, Holy Talents could be fused together. Previously, he hadn't fused them because he had copied too few, and fusing them wouldn't have been very useful.
But if he had countless Holy Talents, once fused, would a talent above the Holy level be born? Although the Transcendent Domain Ancestors of the Battle Sect had said that Holy Talents were the... limit, they might not know everything. Perhaps they just hadn't seen a talent above the Holy level. Maybe something like an Ancestral Talent really existed?
"Hahaha, this place really is a blessed land for me! Even if I can't form a talent beyond the Holy level this time, by integrating so many Holy Talents, it will be much easier for me to practice Holy Techniques!"
Ye Tian muttered.
Subsequently, Ye Tian hunted Holy Soul Beasts to absorb Holy Soul Power and strengthen his Soul Holy Light while simultaneously copying Holy Talents.
Just as he suspected, all the Holy Soul Beasts here possessed Holy Talents.
The only pity was that these Holy Soul Beasts didn't know Holy Techniques; they could only use their Holy Talents to exert their power, which was a complete waste of the talent.
Of course, at the same level, the strength of a Holy Soul Beast still crushed ordinary cultivators. Only true geniuses could contend with a Holy Soul Beast of the same rank.
For example, the Supreme Domain Ancestor Holy Soul Beast Ye Tian encountered earlier probably had the combat power of a second-tier Supreme Domain Ancestor. A weak Supreme Domain Ancestor would truly be killed in an instant by such a beast.
Unfortunately, in Ye Tian's eyes, these Holy Soul Beasts were like ants, easily killed in an instant.
As time passed, Ye Tian's Soul Holy Light grew stronger and stronger, and he copied more and more Holy Talents.
One day, several decades later.
Ye Tian saw a giant black tree that towered into the clouds.
Three fruits grew on this giant black tree. Ye Tian could tell at a glance that these three fruits were extraordinary, not ordinary fruits.
"Could this be..."
Ye Tian thought of the name of a treasure.
"Black Scale Holy Fruit. Rumor has it that a single Black Scale Holy Fruit can create an Invincible Domain Ancestor, and there are three here, enough to create three Invincible Domain Ancestors! Moreover, for a... Supreme Domain Ancestor who has birthed Soul Holy Light, it can also strengthen that light!"
Ye Tian muttered.
In terms of value, a single Black Scale Holy Fruit was no less valuable than a Holy Soul Realm Flower.
Previously, Ye Tian had consumed the Holy Soul Realm Flower, which was originally intended for his wife. Now that he saw these Black Scale Holy Fruits, he could give them to her to help her step into the Invincible Domain Ancestor realm in the future.
"These Black Scale Holy Fruits belong to me!"
Ye Tian flew over.
Just then, he sensed the presence of a stone python.
Through his Copy Talent, he discovered that this stone python was also a Holy Soul Beast and possessed a Holy Talent called Petrification.
Furthermore, its realm was not that of a Supreme Domain Ancestor, but an Invincible Domain Ancestor.
And not far from the stone python, three humanoid stone statues stood there.
"Three Supreme Domain Ancestors have been petrified!"
Ye Tian was somewhat surprised.
The Supreme Domain Ancestors who could enter this place were naturally not weak; even the worst among them likely had first-tier Supreme Domain Ancestor strength. He hadn't expected such Supreme Domain Ancestors to be killed.
This showed that the stone python's strength was terrifying, likely possessing the combat power of a nine-step Invincible Domain Ancestor or higher.
The stone python didn't attack Ye Tian. Perhaps as long as one didn't approach its territory, it wouldn't strike.
"Someone is coming!"
Ye Tian sensed it.
Whoosh whoosh whoosh!!! Two Supreme Domain Ancestors appeared. They were very unfamiliar; Ye Tian had never seen them before.
But through his Copy Talent investigation, he learned of their identities.
"Supreme Domain Ancestors of the Dark Holy Sect!"

Chapter 1422: Slaying the Stone Python!

Chapter 1422: Slaying the Stone Python
!
Before coming to the Holy Soul Realm, Ye Tian had also looked into the Supreme Domain Ancestors on the rankings of the various Holy Sects in the Dark Holy Sanctuary. Unless they were hidden Supreme Domain Ancestors, he recognized everyone on the rankings.
The two Supreme Domain Ancestors he sensed were not on the Dark Holy Sect's rankings, so their strength likely wasn't that great.
"Black Scale Holy Fruits!"
The two Supreme Domain Ancestors from the Dark Holy Sect also spotted the Black Scale Holy Fruits, and looks of greed immediately appeared on their faces.
This item was of high value, and they naturally desired it. Refining it themselves would be a waste; they could trade it to those Supreme Domain Ancestors who were struggling to break through to the Invincible Domain Ancestor level, and it would definitely fetch a high price.
These two Supreme Domain Ancestors also noticed Ye Tian, but they were somewhat uncertain of his strength.
Although they were very confident in their own power, none of the Supreme Domain Ancestors entering the Holy Soul Realm this time were weak. Even some Supreme Domain Ancestors from certain Holy Lands possessed immense strength, not necessarily weaker than those on the rankings, and perhaps even stronger than themselves.
Therefore, it was better to be cautious.
"Your Excellency, there are three Black Scale Holy Fruits. How about one for each of us?"
The two Supreme Domain Ancestors asked.
"Let's deal with this Stone Python first!"
Ye Tian suggested.
"Fine!"
The two Supreme Domain Ancestors from the Dark Holy Sect also sensed the Stone Python and discovered the three petrified Supreme Domain Ancestors.
However, they estimated that those three must have been relatively weak Supreme Domain Ancestors. As members of the Dark Holy Sect, their own strength was very close to the combat power of those on the rankings, so they did not fear the Stone Python.
Boom!!!! Ye Tian and the other two attacked the Stone Python together.
Just then, the Stone Python struck.
Swish! A flash of white light passed by, and the attacks of the three were directly petrified.
At the same time, the Stone Python erupted with a terrifying aura, shattering the void with a strike as it lunged toward them.
"Not good, this Stone Python's strength is comparable to a Seven-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor!"
The two Supreme Domain Ancestors from the Dark Holy Sect were stunned.
A Seven-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor was not weak. Although Supreme Domain Ancestors like them could leapfrog levels to kill weaker Invincible Domain Ancestors, they had no way to contend with a Seven-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor.
Previously, they thought the Holy Soul Beasts of this world did not understand Holy Techniques and that their combat power would be inferior to geniuses of the same rank; even if they became Invincible Domain Ancestors, they shouldn't be a threat.
But they realized they had miscalculated; this Stone Python's strength was terrifying.
"Retreat!"
The two Supreme Domain Ancestors from the Dark Holy Sect made a split-second decision.
However, just as they wanted to flee, Ye Tian deployed the Five Elements Sealing, locking down the void.
Suddenly, the two of them could not escape.
"What is the meaning of this, Your Excellency? Why are you blocking us? If you don't run, you'll die!"
The two Supreme Domain Ancestors from the Dark Holy Sect roared in anger.
"No, the ones dying are you!"
Ye Tian said with a smile.
If they were Supreme Domain Ancestors from other factions, he might have let it go, but they were from the Dark Holy Sect. The relationship between the Battle Gate and the Dark Holy Sect was terrible; even the Fire-Patterned Battle Ancestor had said that if he encountered Supreme Domain Ancestors from the Dark Holy Sect, he should kill them all if possible.
Therefore, he would not let these two go.
"No!"
The two Supreme Domain Ancestors from the Dark Holy Sect frantically attacked Ye Tian, but before they could land many hits, the Stone Python's petrification talent covered them.
The first time, they resisted the petrification talent, but they used up their life-saving treasures.
The second time, they couldn't hold out and were directly petrified, their life force gradually withering away until they died.
....Outside the Primordial Ancestral Realm.
In a patch of darkness, a figure sat perched.
He was the Progenitor of the Dark Holy Sect—the Dark Progenitor. Of course, this was merely a clone, not his true body.
The Dark Progenitor opened his eyes. He sensed that the soul tablets of two Supreme Domain Ancestors from the Dark Holy Sect had shattered. He couldn't help but mutter, "Two Supreme Domain Ancestors dead. They fell so shortly after entering. What useless trash!"
He didn't care much; the two deceased were not on the rankings. No matter how many such Supreme Domain Ancestors fell, he wouldn't feel the sting.
Ye Tian didn't actually need to use the Stone Python's power to kill those two; he could have killed them easily. But he did so to gauge the Stone Python's strength.
"Combat power of a Seven-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor, not bad at all!"
Ye Tian smiled, not panicking in the slightest.
Long ago, when he fought the two Five-Step Invincible Domain Ancestors from the Qingyuan Holy Land, he had suppressed and killed them.
Although he had used the power of the Profound Void Holy Realm back then, his true strength had definitely reached the level of a seven or eight-step Invincible Domain Ancestor.
Now, his Soul Holy Light had increased significantly, and his combat power had definitely stepped into the level of a Six-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor.
Using the strength of a Six-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor to kill a Seven-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor was not particularly difficult.
Boom!!!! Ye Tian struck, using the Void Slash Holy Technique to continuously bombard the Stone Python's massive body.
Crack, crack, crack!!!! The scales on the Stone Python's body shattered under the assault of the Void Slash, and countless amounts of blood sprayed out.
The Stone Python's wounds healed continuously at a very fast rate. This wasn't because it possessed a special recovery method, but rather the instinctive recovery ability of an Invincible Domain Ancestor.
The recovery speed of an Invincible Domain Ancestor was very fast. Unless the disparity in strength was truly massive, killing one would take a long time.
"Kill!"
Countless golden threads surrounded the Stone Python. This was Ye Tian's Golden Silk Holy Technique. Although its power wasn't as great as the Void Slash, it could provide a continuous stream of attacks, which was more effective here.
Under Ye Tian's barrage of various Holy Techniques, the Stone Python had no way to resist. Its petrification ability couldn't affect Ye Tian either; it was directly blocked by several of Ye Tian's defensive Holy Techniques at the Limit Realm. Even if a sliver of petrification power invaded Ye Tian's body, it would be restored by his Indestructible Holy Technique.
Thus, its methods were useless against Ye Tian.
Several months later, this Stone Python was ground to death by Ye Tian.
"A pity. This Stone Python's strength was actually very close to a Six-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor. If it knew a petrification Holy Technique, its power might even exceed a Six-Step. If it truly practiced a petrification technique to a very high level, its combat power would likely jump to the level of a four or five-step Invincible Domain Ancestor instantly!"
Ye Tian evaluated.
However, there are no "ifs." The Holy Soul Beasts of this world cannot leave, but it is thanks to the rules of this world that they can be born with Holy Talents.
Thus, there are gains and losses.
But for Ye Tian, this world was... a place of truly great opportunity.
"I must strive to copy countless Holy Talents as soon as possible and see if a qualitative change occurs after merging them!"
After picking the three Black Scale Holy Fruits, Ye Tian left the area.

Chapter 1423: Ancestral Talent, Ancestral Technique!

Chapter 1423: Ancestral Talent, Ancestral Technique
!
In the days that followed, Ye Tian searched for various resources and treasures while copying Saint Talents, and hunted Saint Soul Beasts to absorb Saint Soul power to strengthen his Soul Saint Light.
It had to be said that Ye Tian's strength was formidable, and thus his harvest was naturally plentiful.
Furthermore, there were so many Saint Soul Beasts in the Saint Soul Realm that there were naturally many Saint Talents, completely exceeding his imagination.
In the blink of an eye, ten thousand years passed.
By this time, Ye Tian didn't even know how many... Saint Talents he had copied. The Copy Talent panel was densely packed with Saint Talents, and he had fused them one by one.
On this day, Ye Tian prepared to fuse a specific category of Saint Talents to see if he could trigger a transformation.
"I'll fuse strength-type Saint Talents then!"
Ye Tian decided.
Because strength-type Saint Talents were relatively common, many Saint Soul Beasts possessed them.
Fusing Saint Talents took a long time. To avoid wasting time, Ye Tian took out a Saint Object containing time rules and activated it with full force, supported by countless energy treasures, initiating a time acceleration of ten million years to one.
Of course, under these conditions, it was difficult for him to cultivate, but he didn't intend to; he only wanted to accelerate the fusion of Saint Talents.
Two Saint Talents fused! Three Saint Talents fused! Four Saint Talents fused! ....Ten! A hundred! A thousand! How could an ordinary Saint Talent user have so many Saint Talents? Even if an Ancestor had the greatest of opportunities, they wouldn't be able to give birth to so many Saint Talents. Besides, Ancestors looked down on Saint Talents and naturally wouldn't spend effort researching how to create them.
Only a monster like Ye Tian, who possessed the Copy Talent, could have such Saint Talents and even fuse them together.
Unknowingly, Ye Tian had spent a billion years fusing in the time-accelerated environment, while a hundred years had passed in the outside world.
By now, Ye Tian had fused over a hundred thousand strength-type Saint Talents, yet he still hadn't caused a qualitative change in the Saint Talent.
However, he felt that the new, unknown strength-type Saint Talent had reached an extremely powerful level, far exceeding ordinary Saint Talents, and was on the verge of a qualitative change.
"Continue fusing!"
After fusing a dozen more strength-type Saint Talents, the unknown strength-type Saint Talent finally completed its qualitative change.
Boom!!!!! Deep within his soul, Ye Tian's unknown Saint Talent, formed from the fusion of over a hundred thousand strength-type Saint Talents, was transforming. The talent mark expanded continuously, gradually turning into a single character—Strength! The talent mark taking the form of a character was something no one would believe if told, yet it happened.
At the same time, Ye Tian sensed the status of this Strength Saint Talent.
[Ancestral Talent: Strength] "There really is an Ancestral Talent. Perhaps this is the only one in the Dark Saint Domain!"
Ye Tian mused.
Of course, it was hard to say for sure; they might possess more secrets and might even be able to research Ancestral Talents.
It had to be said that after obtaining the Ancestral Talent, Ye Tian discovered that the power of the Ancestral Talent alone was comparable to a Saint Technique at the limit realm.
"If I continue to cultivate a strength-type Saint Technique, is it possible to break its shackles and turn it into an Ancestral Technique?"
Ye Tian wondered.
If he could truly achieve that, his strength would reach a terrifying level.
Next, Ye Tian continued to fuse other Saint Talents.
He had copied many of each category of Saint Talent. For instance, although he didn't dare provoke certain Saint Soul Beast groups, he could copy a large number of Saint Talents at once, so he was not lacking in Saint Talents at all.
Soon, one Ancestral Talent after another was born.
[Ancestral Talent: Speed] [Ancestral Talent: Defense] [Ancestral Talent: Gold] [Ancestral Talent: Fire] .... Ye Tian possessed many Ancestral Talents, but the only pity was that he couldn't form a Space Ancestral Talent or a Time Ancestral Talent. This was because there were fewer Saint Soul Beasts with Space and Time Saint Talents. After searching for so long, he had only encountered a few dozen Time Saint Talent beasts and over a hundred Space Saint Talent beasts.
Such a small number of Saint Talents simply couldn't trigger a qualitative change.
Therefore, if he wanted to give birth to Space and Time Ancestral Talents, he could only accumulate them slowly.
Having birthed so many Ancestral Talents, Ye Tian began to re-cultivate those Saint Techniques, specifically focusing on two: the Saint Armor Technique and the Gold Silk Technique.
These two Saint Techniques were not very difficult to cultivate, making it easier to break their shackles and become Ancestral Techniques.
Another few hundred thousand years passed, and Ye Tian's Soul Saint Light had reached fifty percent. This meant half of his soul had turned into Soul Saint Light. Consequently, Ye Tian's strength increased significantly again, reaching the peak of the Six-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor realm, very close to the Five-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor realm.
If he could condense a Saint Soul, he could definitely reach the combat power of a Five-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor.
Alternatively, if he cultivated a Saint Technique to the level of an Ancestral Technique, even if it was just the entry-level, he would definitely possess the combat power of a Five-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor.
On this day.
Ye Tian used an... Invincible Domain Ancestor-level Saint Soul Beast to practice his Gold Silk Technique. He didn't kill this beast, which was only an Eight-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor, but only sparred with it.
Puchi puchi puchi!!!! Strands of gold silk sliced at the Saint Soul Beast, while the beast continuously attacked Ye Tian, the two of them trading blows.
At the same time, Ye Tian kept his Gold Ancestral Talent active, sensing the power of the Ancestral Talent and the Gold Silk Technique.
At some point, Ye Tian seemed to fall into an epiphany, his consciousness extending into the source of the Saint Technique.
At this moment, he saw rivers of gold.
"Gold, sharpness, Ancestral Talent, origin, unity..."
In a sudden flash, Ye Tian seemed to grasp the essence of gold and finally understood a hint of the mysteries of the Gold Ancestral Talent.
It had to be said that the Gold Ancestral Talent was not just a talent; it was more like a guide, leading Ye Tian to comprehend deeper realms, second only to the effect of the Gold Ancestor Law.
However, in terms of comprehending Saint Techniques and Ancestral Techniques, the Gold Ancestral Talent far surpassed the so-called Ancestor Law.
Boom!!!!! The Gold Silk Technique transformed; it was no longer a Saint Technique.
Now, the Gold Silk Technique could be called the Gold Silk Ancestral Technique! "Gold Silk Ancestral Technique, Kill!"
A streak of golden light instantly flashed through the void, slicing the Invincible Domain Ancestor Saint Soul Beast in front of him into two pieces.
"As expected of an Ancestral Technique, the attack power is terrifying!"
Ye Tian was very satisfied.
Having comprehended the Gold Silk Ancestral Technique, Ye Tian's strength surged, reaching the combat power of a Five-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor. As long as he continued to cultivate the Gold Silk Ancestral Technique to the minor completion stage, or obtained more Ancestral Techniques, his strength would likely reach the limit of a Five-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor, second only to the combat power of a Four-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor.
By then, he would likely be able to sweep through the Saint Soul Realm.

Chapter 1424: Star Soul Sand!

Chapter 1424: Star Soul Sand
!
"Next, while practicing the Golden Silk Ancestral Technique, I will strive to break the shackles of the Holy Armor Holy Technique and turn it into the Ancestral Armor Ancestral Technique!"
Ye Tian arranged his next cultivation plan.
With the Defense Ancestral Talent, Ye Tian was not worried about being unable to upgrade the Holy Armor Holy Technique into an ancestral technique.
In the blink of an eye, another several hundred thousand years passed.
During these years, besides constantly copying holy talents and slaying holy soul beasts to strengthen his soul holy light, Ye Tian had been using the Holy Armor Holy Technique to fight in close quarters with numerous holy soul beasts, tempering the technique.
Countless times, Ye Tian's Holy Armor was shattered by the holy soul beasts, but between the breaking and repairing, Ye Tian's comprehension of the Holy Armor Holy Technique grew deeper and deeper. Moreover, because of the Defense Ancestral Talent, Ye Tian faced no bottlenecks in holy techniques; as long as the opportunity arrived, he could upgrade the holy technique into an ancestral technique. This was his advantage.
On this day.
While Ye Tian was fighting a group of holy soul beasts, he finally completed the transformation of the Holy Armor Holy Technique.
Buzz!!! A set of black-gold battle armor replaced Ye Tian's previous Holy Armor. This was a fundamental qualitative change in the technique; it was no longer a holy technique, but an ancestral technique! Ancestral Technique: Ancestral Armor! The power of this Ancestral Armor technique was terrifying, its defensive power many times stronger than the Holy Armor. Ye Tian stood there, allowing a large number of holy soul beasts to attack him, yet they could not break his defense.
Such defense could only be described as horrifyingly formidable! With the Golden Silk Ancestral Technique for attack and the Ancestral Armor Ancestral Technique for defense, Ye Tian's strength could be described as having surged exponentially.
If he could obtain a speed-type ancestral technique, he would be even more well-rounded.
"Next, I'll focus on fully upgrading the Flowing Light Holy Technique!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Originally, Ye Tian wanted to cultivate peacefully like this. After all... he could stay in the Holy Soul Realm for a long time and had plenty of time to enhance his soul holy light and practice holy techniques.
However, on this day, a transmission arrived.
"A transmission from Qingyu Domain Ancestor!"
Ye Tian was surprised.
According to the transmission, the supreme domain ancestors of Zhanmen and those from other factions had discovered a treasure land, a place of true great opportunity. They were currently in a dispute, and a battle could break out at any moment, so they sent a message asking him to come and support them.
Subsequently, other supreme domain ancestors of Zhanmen also sent transmissions to Ye Tian, requesting his support.
"A place of true great opportunity!"
Ye Tian was somewhat curious about this place, but the supreme domain ancestors of Zhanmen did not specify what the opportunity was. He didn't ask further and instead rushed over at his fastest speed.
In the Holy Soul Realm, within a void that resembled a starry sky, this was the interior of the treasure land where a group of supreme domain ancestors had appeared.
Suddenly.
A black sphere the size of a star appeared, immediately triggering a scramble among the supreme domain ancestors.
"This grain of Star Soul Sand is mine!"
Shouted a supreme domain ancestor on the Supreme Rankings.
However, a supreme domain ancestor on the Supreme Rankings was nothing here. A ten-meter-tall giant crushed that supreme domain ancestor to death with one hand.
This giant was not a cultivator but a forbidden creature appearing in human form.
He was the sixth-ranked supreme domain ancestor of the Forbidden Saint Gate—Wu Xiu! Wu Xiu's strength intimidated the other supreme domain ancestors. He instantly snatched the grain of Star Soul Sand and stored it in his soul sea, making it difficult for others to steal it back.
It wasn't that there were no supreme domain ancestors here comparable to Wu Xiu, but this treasure land's void was too vast, and the location where the Star Soul Sand appeared was unpredictable, so it was snatched by Wu Xiu.
"What a pity!"
One powerful supreme domain ancestor after another lamented.
"Wu Xiu, you dare kill a supreme domain ancestor from our Immortal Saint Gate's Supreme Rankings!"
An angry supreme domain ancestor who had just arrived shouted.
He was the seventh-ranked supreme domain ancestor on the Immortal Saint Gate's Supreme Rankings—Golden Snake Domain Ancestor! "Golden Snake Domain Ancestor, if you're not satisfied, then let's have a fight!"
Wu Xiu sneered.
"Hmph!"
Golden Snake Domain Ancestor snorted coldly but did not make a move.
Fighting Wu Xiu without any benefit was completely unnecessary... if he got injured, it would only hinder him from snatching treasures later.
"Coward!"
Wu Xiu chuckled.
Just then, Ye Tian arrived.
"Wanfa Domain Ancestor, you've arrived!"
The supreme domain ancestors of Zhanmen greeted Ye Tian upon seeing him.
Among them, Qingyu Domain Ancestor was also present but was significantly injured and was currently healing.
After all, Qingyu Domain Ancestor's strength was not particularly great. Even though his strength had improved over these years, he still couldn't compare to the top-tier supreme domain ancestors on the Supreme Rankings, hence his injuries.
"What kind of treasure land is this?"
Ye Tian asked.
Having just arrived, he didn't understand the situation and was curious about the circumstances here.
"This treasure land is very special; it can produce Star Soul Sand!"
Xihe Domain Ancestor, the thirteenth-ranked supreme domain ancestor of Zhanmen, introduced.
"Star Soul Sand!!!!!"
Ye Tian had naturally heard of this treasure. Though named "sand," its size was comparable to a small star, but in the context of the Dark Holy Domain, it was indeed just... a grain of sand. However, it was a treasure that could strengthen soul holy light.
The value of a single grain of Star Soul Sand was even more precious than a Soul Holy Realm Flower. Thus, one grain of Star Soul Sand was enough for a supreme domain ancestor to cultivate for a long time; after all, its size was large and difficult to consume entirely.
"No wonder it attracted so many supreme domain ancestors. If I obtain enough Star Soul Sand, it will definitely allow me to condense a Holy Soul!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
"Wanfa Domain Ancestor, once Star Soul Sand is discovered, we will work together to snatch it.
A grain of Star Soul Sand is born here almost every day, but it only appears for ten minutes. Therefore, it must be snatched within ten minutes, or it will disappear!"
Xihe Domain Ancestor suggested.
"Agreed!"
Ye Tian nodded.
In reality, he wanted to act alone, but since Xihe Domain Ancestor and Qingyu Domain Ancestor had alerted him to this place, it wouldn't be right to refuse cooperation.
If he helped them snatch enough Star Soul Sand, he could then propose to act independently without it being considered excessive.
Soon, the next day arrived.
At this time, at a location somewhat distant from Ye Tian and the others, a grain of Star Soul Sand appeared.
Wu Xiu wanted to snatch this grain of Star Soul Sand, but the distance was a bit far, while the Golden Snake Domain Ancestor of the Immortal Saint Gate was closer to it.
"Hahaha, I am the closest, no one can beat me to it!"
Golden Snake Domain Ancestor said excitedly.
However, a figure flickered—it was Ye Tian.
Ye Tian utilized the Space Holy Technique, Space Escape. The limit-level Space Holy Technique made Ye Tian's speed incredibly fast, arriving there in an instant.
At the same time, Ye Tian directly used the Five Elements Sealing to lock down the space around himself and the Star Soul Sand, isolating the Golden Snake Domain Ancestor.
"Whoosh!"
The Star Soul Sand was collected by Ye Tian.

Chapter 1425: Ye Tian Kills the Golden Snake Domain Ancestor!

Chapter 1425: Ye Tian Kills the Golden Snake Domain Ancestor
!
"Myriad Laws Domain Ancestor!!!!"
The Golden Snake Domain Ancestor roared in rage.
At this moment, he wanted to kill the Myriad Laws Domain Ancestor.
Rumor had it that the Myriad Laws Domain Ancestor was extremely powerful, capable of perfectly borrowing the power of a Holy Realm, making him practically invincible within his own Xuanxu Holy Realm.
He admitted that if they were in the Xuanxu Holy Realm, he would never dare to make a move against the Myriad Laws Domain Ancestor.
However, this was not the Xuanxu Holy Realm.
Furthermore, his strength was much greater than before; he had now condensed a Holy Soul, was one of the Holy Gifted, and had mastered two Holy Techniques to their limit.
Although everyone's foundation was different and their strength varied accordingly.
However, he did not believe that he was no match for Ye Tian.
"Die!"
The Golden Snake Domain Ancestor attacked Ye Tian.
He wanted to kill Ye Tian! So what if Ye Tian was one of the Holy Gifted? Who wasn't a Holy Gifted? Normally, a Holy Gifted only had one or at most two Holy Talents. Ye Tian had many, so many factions speculated that he wasn't the offspring of a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor, but rather the child of a Primordial Ancestor.
But this speculation didn't hold up under scrutiny. After all, there were only so many Primordial Ancestors in the Dark Forbidden Zone, and they all knew each other. The possibility of a Primordial Ancestor suddenly appearing was too low.
Therefore, Ye Tian was at most... the offspring of a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor.
If he killed Ye Tian, the Immortal Holy Sect behind him and his parents would be able to protect him.
So, while others were afraid to kill Ye Tian, he was not! "Golden Thorn!"
A top-tier Holy Weapon longsword appeared in the Golden Snake Domain Ancestor's hand, carrying the power of the Holy Technique "Golden Thorn" as it instantly pierced forward.
This sword strike was incredibly fast, and its power was terrifying.
Even a Supreme Domain Ancestor ranked around twentieth on the Supreme Ranking would be killed or heavily injured by such an attack.
After all, in the top twenty of the Supreme Ranking, the gap in strength between each rank was huge. In their eyes, Supreme Domain Ancestors ranked below twentieth were no more than ants.
"Get lost!"
Ye Tian unleashed the Holy Armor technique. He didn't use the Ancestral Armor; a mere Golden Snake Domain Ancestor didn't require him to use an Ancestral Technique.
Clang! The Golden Thorn struck the Holy Armor but failed to break through Ye Tian's defense at all.
Then, Ye Tian struck with a Void Slash, hitting the Golden Snake Domain Ancestor and piercing right through him.
Whoosh! The Golden Snake Domain Ancestor teleported away, looking at his body with a grim expression.
He was injured, and the injury was not light.
"The Myriad Laws Domain Ancestor is this strong?!!!"
This was beyond his expectations. He had thought all of Ye Tian's strength came from the Xuanxu Holy Realm, but he hadn't expected his own combat power to be so terrifying! "Why is it like this? He is also a Holy Gifted. Even if he knows more Holy Techniques, he hasn't condensed a Holy Soul yet. I should be stronger than him!"
The Golden Snake Domain Ancestor couldn't understand it.
But he didn't dare to attack Ye Tian anymore. In other words, he had chickened out! However, since he had attacked Ye Tian, Ye Tian would not let him go.
Suddenly.
Ye Tian appeared beside the Golden Snake Domain Ancestor, activating the Time Holy Technique: Eternal Holy Technique.
Buzz! Time in this area was frozen.
The Golden Snake Domain Ancestor was also affected. Although he quickly broke free from the time influence, Ye Tian's next round of attacks had begun, and he could no longer dodge.
"Void Slash!"
A near full-power Void Slash struck the Golden Snake Domain Ancestor. It was even more terrifying than the previous hurried Void Slash. This time, Ye Tian had channeled almost all the power of his Soul Holy Light into the technique.
The power of this strike definitely reached the level of a Six-step Invincible Domain Ancestor.
And the Golden Snake Domain Ancestor was not... a Six-step Invincible Domain Ancestor. At most, he could barely reach the level of an Eight-step Extreme Invincible Domain Ancestor, perhaps not even a Seven-step.
Only a Supreme Domain Ancestor like Wu Xiu possessed Seven-step Invincible Domain Ancestor combat power! Thus, the power of this strike...
The Golden Snake Domain Ancestor couldn't withstand it. Even with defensive holy items protecting him, he couldn't offset much of the attack's power.
Boom!!!!! Nearly half of the Golden Snake Domain Ancestor's body was annihilated. This time, he was completely and severely injured.
"Quickly, help me!!!"
The Golden Snake Domain Ancestor cried out for help to the Domain Ancestors of the Immortal Holy Sect.
However, how could the other Supreme Domain Ancestors of the Immortal Holy Sect dare to intervene? If they did, they would surely die; they couldn't even withstand the aftershocks.
Therefore, they could only call for help from even more powerful Supreme Domain Ancestors, such as the top five geniuses on the Immortal Holy Sect's Supreme Domain Ancestor ranking.
The top five geniuses of the Immortal Holy Sect all possessed combat power of a Seven-step Invincible Domain Ancestor or higher, so only they had a hope of saving the Golden Snake Domain Ancestor.
"This strength..."
In the distance, Wu Xiu showed deep wariness.
He only possessed Seven-step Invincible Domain Ancestor combat power, which was almost the limit, as he had also condensed a Holy Soul and would need to push for the Invincible Domain Ancestor rank once he left.
At the level of a Supreme Domain Ancestor, he no longer knew how to increase his combat power.
It could be said that it was extremely difficult for him to increase his combat power even by a tiny bit.
Among Supreme Domain Ancestors, even those on the Supreme Ranking, Seven-step Invincible combat power was the lifelong limit for most. No matter how they improved, it was hard to step into the Six-step level.
For example, the top five on the Forbidden Holy Sect's Supreme Ranking were basically only at the Seven-step level, merely infinitely close to the Six-step level.
Perhaps one or two of them had reached the Six-step level, but perhaps not.
But right before his eyes, Ye Tian's strength had truly reached the level of a Six-step Invincible Domain Ancestor!
"He cannot be provoked!"
Wu Xiu thought to himself.
The Golden Snake Domain Ancestor truly lived up to being a Holy Gifted with a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor for a father; his foundation was deep, and he had many life-saving items.
Without Ye Tian using an Ancestral Technique, it would take at least a minute to kill the Golden Snake Domain Ancestor.
Soon, the Golden Snake Domain Ancestor was on the verge of death.
"Myriad Laws Domain Ancestor, if you kill me, my father, the Golden Desolate War Ancestor, will definitely kill you!!!"
The Golden Snake Domain Ancestor brought up his father.
"Then let him come!"
Ye Tian was fearless.
The Supreme-level Domain Ancestors of the Dark Holy Region could not be deployed casually; otherwise, the Dark Holy Region would have fallen into chaos long ago.
If a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor from the Immortal Holy Sect tried to kill him, it would be a violation of the rules. The Primordial Ancestor of the War Sect would definitely step in to stop them. This was also the hint that the Fire Pattern War Ancestor had given them this time.
Therefore, within the Holy Soul Realm, everyone could kill freely without worrying about the other party's identity.
At the final moment.
The third-ranked Supreme Domain Ancestor of the Immortal Holy Sect—the Dark Red Domain Ancestor—arrived!
