Chapter 1426: Legendary Item: Holy Gold Sand!

Chapter 1426: Legendary Item
: Holy Gold Sand!
Dark Red Domain Ancestor was ranked third on the Immortal Holy Sect's Ultimate List. Her strength was incredibly formidable; she had condensed her Holy Soul long before entering the Holy Soul Realm, and her Holy Soul was much stronger than average. Her own foundation was also heaven-defying.
Additionally, she was a very ancient Ultimate Domain Ancestor who had practiced countless secret techniques and even obtained numerous opportunities, tempering her physical body to an incredibly terrifying degree. Possessing multiple holy artifacts, her combat power was immense, far beyond what Golden Snake Domain Ancestor could compare to.
In terms of strength, she had definitely reached the peak of Seven-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor combat power. As for whether she had reached... Six-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor combat power, no one could say for sure.
After all, on the surface, no one had been heard to have stepped into the realm of Six-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor combat power.
And Ye Tian was the first! "Domain Ancestor Wanfa, give me some face and release Golden Snake Domain Ancestor, will you?"
Dark Red Domain Ancestor said hurriedly.
"No!"
Ye Tian refused.
"No!" Golden Snake Domain Ancestor let out a terrified roar, but it was to no avail. Under another strike from Ye Tian, Golden Snake Domain Ancestor perished completely.
Seeing the fall of Golden Snake Domain Ancestor, Dark Red Domain Ancestor was extremely furious.
This was a monstrous genius in the top ten of the Immortal Holy Sect's Ultimate List; losing even one was a massive loss.
Furthermore, she had known Golden Snake Domain Ancestor for countless ages and had a decent relationship with him. Ye Tian had actually killed Golden Snake Domain Ancestor right in front of her, showing her no respect at all.
However, in the end, she did not make a move.
Golden Snake Domain Ancestor was already dead; that was a fact that could not be changed.
Although the Ancestors had the ability to reverse the life and death of an Ultimate Domain Ancestor, the price was too high and they wouldn't do it. Thus, dead meant... dead.
She didn't want to fight to the death with Ye Tian. Moreover, Ye Tian possessed the combat power of a Six-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor; unless she used her trump cards, she was simply no match for him.
She endured it! "She didn't move?"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
If Dark Red Domain Ancestor had attacked, he would have killed her as well while he was at it.
In the following days, Star Soul Sands appeared one after another. Ye Tian led the Ultimate Domain Ancestors of the War Sect to seize several grains. Some Star Soul Sands were too far away, and other Ultimate Domain Ancestors had extraordinary means, so they were seized instantly. Even with Ye Tian's speed, he couldn't snatch them all in time.
But even so, many Ultimate Domain Ancestors of the War Sect obtained several grains of Star Soul Sand.
But they were well aware that this was all thanks to Ye Tian and had little to do with them.
"Everyone, I plan to act alone!"
Ye Tian suggested.
The others had no objections. After all, they had already gained a huge advantage, and they would feel embarrassed to continue like this.
The Ultimate Domain Ancestors of the War Sect agreed, and Ye Tian separated from them, heading to another area of this treasure land to avoid competing with them for Star Soul Sand later.
As time slowly passed, grains of Star Soul Sand appeared, and Ye Tian, relying on his strength and speed, managed to snatch quite a few.
These Star Soul Sands were very effective at tempering Ye Tian's Soul Holy Light. If taken to the outside world, they could create many Invincible Domain Ancestors, but such a great opportunity only occurred once in countless ages.
The Primordial Ancestral World only produced this once in such a long time, making it an opportunity for the various Holy Sects to rise.
After this event, the various Holy Worlds would likely produce a large number of Invincible Domain Ancestors, but such a golden age had nothing to do with ordinary holy lands or sects.
"With so many treasures that can help Ultimate Domain Ancestors break through to the Invincible Domain Ancestor realm, the number of Invincible Domain Ancestors in the various Holy Sects must be staggering!"
Ye Tian suddenly thought.
In fact, he didn't even know how many Invincible Domain Ancestors the War Sect had.
Many Invincible Domain Ancestors were not in the War Ancestor World but were out adventuring in the outside world, some even leaving the Dark Holy Region to enter the boundless Dark Forbidden Region to seek other opportunities.
Otherwise, if they stayed in the Dark Holy Region, they would have few chances to break through to the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor realm.
Suddenly.
Not far away, spatial fluctuations emerged.
The gazes of many Ultimate Domain Ancestors turned toward that spot.
"Has another grain of Star Soul Sand appeared?"
Ye Tian began to warp over, but strangely, although the spatial fluctuations had emerged, the Star Soul Sand did not appear immediately.
Previously, the spatial fluctuations and the Star Soul Sand had always appeared simultaneously. This situation was somewhat special.
Boom!!!! A grain of golden Star Soul Sand, many times smaller than the regular Star Soul Sand, appeared. Its size was only about that of a small mountain, but its mass was terrifying, and the fluctuations it emitted were incredibly powerful.
"What kind of Star Soul Sand is this?"
Many Ultimate Domain Ancestors were dazed.
But someone still recognized it and exclaimed in shock: "This is Holy Gold Sand! It's a rare treasure rumored to allow the Holy Soul to undergo a second qualitative transformation. Even within the Holy Sects, there are very few such treasures!"
"Holy Gold Sand!!!!"
Many people went wild, their eyes filled with greed.
To allow the Holy Soul to undergo a second qualitative transformation—what kind of concept was that? Although the current Holy Sects had similar treasures, they were too few, and they were reluctant to give them to the disciples. Even the Holy Gifted were not qualified to use them, unless they were the offspring of an Ancestor. However, many Ancestors were unwilling to produce offspring, so Ancestral scions were exceptionally rare.
But what if one day an Ancestor wanted to have offspring? Then the incredibly rare resources within the Holy Sect would be given to that Ancestral scion.
There were Holy Gifted among them, but legendary items like Holy Gold Sand were beyond their wildest dreams.
At this moment, Ultimate Domain Ancestors like Wu Xiu and Dark Red Domain Ancestor went mad.
At the same time, those Ultimate Domain Ancestors from all over the Holy Soul Realm who had previously looked down on this treasure land also rushed over.
Holy Soul Sand wasn't very effective for those Ultimate Domain Ancestors who had already condensed their Holy Souls, so if there were other opportunities, those Ultimate Domain Ancestors wouldn't come to this treasure land.
But now, Holy Gold Sand had appeared, and those Ultimate Domain Ancestors immediately abandoned other opportunity sites and rushed here one by one.
"The Holy Gold Sand is mine!"
Wu Xiu's eyes were bloodshot as he directly revealed his Forbidden Body.
Boom!!!! Wu Xiu transformed into a massive ape hundreds of millions of feet tall, his aura incredibly terrifying, very close to a Six-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor. He had hidden a portion of his strength before, but now he revealed almost all of it.
And Dark Red Domain Ancestor was no exception, her aura fully unleashed as if she had already stepped half a foot into the level of Six-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor combat power.
They all reached out to seize the Holy Gold Sand.
But a treasure like Holy Gold Sand also had an automatic self-protection ability; streaks of golden light shattered the powers and techniques of the various Ultimate Domain Ancestors.
Clearly, taking the Holy Gold Sand would require some time.

Chapter 1427: Massacre, Supreme Domain Ancestors Fall One After Another!

Chapter 1427: Massacre, Supreme Domain Ancestors Fall One After Another
!
The Sacred Golden Sand was firmly fixed in the void of this treasure land. A nearby Supreme Domain Ancestor wanted to collect it into his internal world, but his speed was far too slow.
Boom! Another powerful Supreme Domain Ancestor attacked him, heavily wounding him in an instant.
The slaughter began! And Ye Tian also made his move, killing everything in his path and striking down Supreme Domain Ancestors one by one.
As the Supreme Domain Ancestors fell one after another, the others grew terrified and retreated, no longer daring to compete.
At this moment, only Ye Tian, Wu Xiu, An Hong, and a few other Supreme Domain Ancestors remained. These Supreme Domain Ancestors were by no means weak; they were all monstrous geniuses ranked in the top ten of their respective Sacred Sects' Supreme Rankings. Each possessed combat power comparable to a Seven-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor, though some were slightly weaker while others were infinitely close to the combat power of a Six-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor.
Their auras were locked onto Ye Tian, as if they were about to strike him simultaneously.
"Wanfa Domain Ancestor!"
Wu Xiu and the others blocked Ye Tian, preventing him from seizing the Sacred Golden Sand.
"You aren't fighting for the Sacred Golden Sand, yet you're blocking me. Aren't you afraid others will take the chance to snatch it away?"
Ye Tian sneered.
An Hong Domain Ancestor said, "The Sacred Golden Sand is firmly connected to the void. It will take some time to remove it, so we aren't afraid of others snatching it.
Wanfa Domain Ancestor, your strength is comparable to a Six-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor. If we don't unite against you, we won't have any chance of seizing the Sacred Golden Sand."
Wu Xiu also added, "Wanfa Domain Ancestor, you have two choices now: retreat immediately and swear an oath not to fight for the Sacred Golden Sand, or we will join forces to kill you!"
For the Sacred Golden Sand, it was worth the risk to kill Ye Tian.
"I give the same warning to you: retreat immediately, or I will kill you all right now!"
Ye Tian threatened back.
"Do it!"
Wu Xiu and the others attacked.
They didn't dare waste time. After all, every second wasted meant a more powerful Supreme Domain Ancestor might arrive. If they delayed too long, even if they killed Ye Tian, their own chances of seizing the Sacred Golden Sand would be greatly reduced.
They weren't... true allies; they were still competitors. It was only because Ye Tian was too great a threat that they were forced to unite.
Therefore, killing Ye Tian and then competing among themselves for the Sacred Golden Sand was the best choice. Time was of the essence.
Nearly ten experts from the top ten of the Supreme Ranking attacked together. Such a deterrent was enough to threaten a Six-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor.
Among these Supreme Domain Ancestors, some used Soul Sacred Techniques, some used binding-type Sacred Techniques, and others used bizarre Sacred Techniques, but most used offensive Sacred Techniques.
Furthermore, they all utilized Sacred Objects and Sacred Weapons. Under their collective outburst, even a Six-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor would be heavily wounded.
"Wanfa Domain Ancestor!"
The Supreme Domain Ancestors of the Battle Sect grew nervous and began to worry.
However, they didn't dare step forward because their strength was too low. If they intervened, they wouldn't be able to help and might even become a burden.
Now, they could only hope that Ye Tian was strong enough or that other top-ten experts from the Supreme Ranking would arrive to support him.
But Ye Tian didn't panic at all.
"I originally wanted to keep a low profile, but since you're seeking death, I'll let you see my true strength!"
Ye Tian said coldly.
"Ancestral Armor!"
Boom!!!!! The Ancestral Technique, Ancestral Armor, protected Ye Tian, allowing him to withstand the numerous attacks without his defense being shaken in the slightest.
Then, with a wave of his hand, Ye Tian sent out countless golden lights that transformed into threads, slicing toward the Supreme Domain Ancestors.
One Supreme Domain Ancestor, whose strength was comparable to a weaker Seven-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor and who was ranked ninth in the Dark Sacred Sect, was instantly disintegrated when sliced by Ye Tian's Golden Silk Ancestral Technique.
In an instant, this Supreme Domain Ancestor fell! It could be said that the strength Ye Tian now displayed was no longer that of a Six-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor, but a Five-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor—and not a weak one, but a standard Five-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor, close to the middle tier.
It was very easy for a Five-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor to kill a Seven-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor. Moreover, Supreme Domain Ancestors were easier to kill than Invincible Domain Ancestors.
Thus, this Supreme Domain Ancestor was insta-killed by Ye Tian without any power to resist.
"No!!!!"
The Supreme Domain Ancestors were terrified. Those with slightly weaker life-saving abilities might have blocked one strike, but the golden light of the Golden Silk Ancestral Technique sliced through again and again, making it impossible to resist.
Soon, the Supreme Domain Ancestors fell one by one.
"Impossible! How can you know Ancestral Techniques, and two of them at that?!!!"
Wu Xiu said in disbelief.
Among the Invincible Domain Ancestors, such as the very top tier within the various Sacred Sects, there were likely very few who had comprehended Ancestral Techniques.
For example, among the Thirty-Six War Emperors of the Battle Sect, only the Five Thunder Domain Ancestor was known to have comprehended an Ancestral Technique.
Yet Ye Tian was only a Supreme Domain Ancestor, and his cultivation time was very short; he was an incredibly young Supreme Domain Ancestor. For such a young Supreme Domain Ancestor to have comprehended Ancestral Techniques—was that even possible? If someone had told him before that a Supreme Domain Ancestor could master an Ancestral Technique, he would have considered them a madman or a fool.
But now, he had seen with his own eyes Ye Tian perform Ancestral Techniques—two of them—with strength comparable to a Five-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor.
This was no longer a monster; this was a taboo existence!
"Escape!"
Wu Xiu prepared to flee, and An Hong Domain Ancestor also prepared to flee; otherwise, death was certain.
They spared no expense, even burning their Domain Bodies and Sacred Souls just to escape.
However, the golden threads of the Golden Silk Ancestral Technique pierced through the void.
Pfft! Wu Xiu's physical body was directly pierced; his so-called defenses were completely useless.
One life-saving item after another was applied to his body, and he even used an Ancestral Medicine to recover from his injuries, but he still couldn't repair the damage.
Soon, the golden threads pierced through again.
Under the repeated attacks, Wu Xiu finally let out a cry of unwilling despair as his massive body turned into a corpse, floating in the void.
Wu Xiu had fallen!
Now, only An Hong Domain Ancestor remained. However, Ye Tian had long since sealed the void. Although the power of the Five Elements Sealing couldn't completely lock down a powerhouse like An Hong Domain Ancestor, it could hinder her. Breaking the seal completely would take time.
And Ye Tian would not give her that time.
"Wanfa Domain Ancestor, how about you let me go? I am willing to pay a price!"
An Hong Domain Ancestor said hurriedly.
"No need!"
Ye Tian said coldly.
Since these Domain Ancestors dared to attack him, they had to be prepared to fall.
"Then let's die together!"
An Hong Domain Ancestor went mad.
She took out a treasure, and a terrifying power was faintly about to explode.

Chapter 1428: Detonating the World Source Core, Mass Death of Supreme Domain Ancestors...

Chapter 1428: Detonating the World Source Core, Mass Death of Supreme Domain Ancestors
!
"Ancestor of Myriad Laws, this is a World Source Core. It is a special treasure refined from an entire domain by a Half-step Primordial Ancestor. Once detonated, it is equivalent to the explosion of an entire domain. Even you would likely perish. If you continue to hunt me, we will all die together!"
Dark Red Ancestor had gone mad.
A treasure like the World Source Core was something even ordinary Half-step Primordial Ancestors wouldn't bother to refine. She had obtained it from the ruins of a Half-step Primordial Ancestor she once entered; it was her most important trump card.
However, this thing could not be controlled. Once detonated, she herself would be caught in the blast.
"Then detonate it!"
Ye Tian said coldly.
He was well aware of what a World Source Core was. Once detonated, it was powerful enough to kill an ordinary Five-step Invincible Domain Ancestor. However, it was still far from enough to kill him.
Boom!!!! Ye Tian continued his attack. A golden light pierced through, instantly impaling Dark Red Ancestor.
On the brink of death, Dark Red Ancestor detonated the World Source Core.
In the distance.
One by one, the Supreme Domain Ancestors fled frantically, escaping toward the distance at their maximum speed.
"Run, quickly! Dark Red Ancestor has gone mad, she’s actually going to trigger a World Source Core!"
"The range of a World Source Core is too vast! If we can't escape, we're dead!"
The Supreme Domain Ancestors who were relatively far from Ye Tian and Dark Red Ancestor were still able to flee, but those nearby were stunned.
The detonation took almost no time at all; it exploded instantly.
Buzz!!!!! More than half of the treasure land was covered by the power of the World Source Core, and it happened almost in a flash.
Immediately, countless spaces were annihilated. Supreme Domain Ancestors who didn't have time to dodge had their Supreme Domain Bodies obliterated. Even their souls, holy objects, and holy weapons could not be preserved, as if they were instantly erased from this world.
Naturally, Ye Tian wasn't foolish enough to block it head-on. He performed the Void Escape Saint Technique to dive into the deep layers of the void.
Of course, even after diving into the deep void, the power of the World Source Core's explosion would still penetrate through the layers of space to strike his physical body.
But Ye Tian possessed the Ancestral Armor Ancestral Technique, and his defensive power was terrifying, so he would be fine.
The explosion of the World Source Core continued to annihilate this area for several hours before it gradually dissipated.
Whoosh! A figure walked out from the depths of the void; it was Ye Tian.
At this moment, he looked a bit disheveled and was injured. After all, this was a lethal weapon capable of killing those with the combat power of an ordinary Five-step Invincible Domain Ancestor. It naturally posed a threat to him. If not for the help of the Void Escape Saint Technique and the Ancestral Armor, he likely would have been heavily wounded.
Now, he was merely injured.
"Undying Saint Technique!"
Under the recovery of the Undying Saint Technique, Ye Tian healed at an extremely fast speed.
He looked around. Not a single Supreme Domain Ancestor remained in this area, but the void of this treasure land was rapidly repairing itself. After all, even he couldn't destroy the source of this void; a mere World Source Core was naturally incapable of destroying this treasure land.

These Supreme Domain Ancestors were powerful existences ranked in the top five of their respective Holy Sects, and some were even the number one or two Supreme Domain Ancestors.
At this time, the remaining Supreme Domain Ancestors from the various Holy Sects hurriedly reported to these top-five powerhouses.
"It was the Ancestor of Myriad Laws who killed Ancestor Wu Xiu!"
A Supreme Domain Ancestor from the Forbidden Holy Sect sent a message.
When these top-five Supreme Domain Ancestors learned of the situation, they all turned to look at Ye Tian in anger.
"Ancestor of Myriad Laws, aren't you being a bit too excessive? You've slaughtered so many Supreme Domain Ancestors from the Holy Sects!"
Yuanlong Ancestor, the second-ranked Supreme Domain Ancestor of the Forbidden Holy Sect, spoke coldly.

Then, if an Invincible Domain Ancestor of our War Gate offends a Primordial Ancestor of your Immortal Holy Sect and knows he's going to die, can he slaughter countless living beings in the Dark Holy Domain, or even slaughter Supreme Domain Ancestors, Saint-Talented ones, and descendants of Primordial Ancestors from other Holy Sects, and then not be held responsible?"
Ye Tian used an analogy.
"That is a fallacy!"
Shengyun Ancestor quickly replied.
"The logic is... exactly that. I am not wrong. Dark Red Ancestor wanted to kill me, and I fought back; there was nothing wrong with that to begin with.
She was no match for me, so she used the World Source Core to perish together with me, wiping out a large number of Supreme Domain Ancestors in the process. In the end, instead of blaming Dark Red Ancestor, you blame me. How ridiculous!"
Ye Tian continued.

Of course, they didn't have a good attitude toward Ye Tian either and were very angry with him, as some Supreme Domain Ancestors from other Holy Sects had indeed fallen by Ye Tian's hand.

Chapter 1429: Condensing the Holy Soul, Strength Skyrockets!

Chapter 1429: Condensing the Holy Soul, Strength Skyrockets
!
Time passed slowly. Holy Gold Sand stopped appearing for a while, but Star Soul Sand continued to appear at a rate of one per day.
Ye Tian was the strongest and fastest, so he was often able to snatch the Star Soul Sand.
A hundred years later, on this day, a ripple of spatial fluctuation occurred.
"Holy Gold Sand is about to appear!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Sure enough.
A grain of Holy Gold Sand appeared, and it was relatively close to Ye Tian. Thus, Ye Tian appeared beside the Holy Gold Sand at his fastest speed and forcibly collected it. The Supreme Domain Ancestors of various Holy Sects, including those ranked first and second on the Supreme List, wanted to snatch the Holy Gold Sand, but Ye Tian severely injured them one by one.
After that, they didn't dare to try and snatch it anymore, and the Holy Gold Sand fell into Ye Tian's hands.
Next, almost every hundred years, Holy Gold Sand would appear once.
But Ye Tian didn't manage to snatch it every time. If it was far from him, some Supreme Domain Ancestors had peculiar methods and could take the Holy Gold Sand in an instant. Of course, they would pay a price, but compared to obtaining the Holy Gold Sand, that price was nothing.
Ye Tian was somewhat helpless about this; he also wanted to snatch all the Holy Gold Sand, but it wasn't realistic.
Time passed slowly in this manner, snatching Star Soul Sand and Holy Gold Sand.
A thousand years! Ten thousand years! A hundred thousand years! Three hundred thousand! A million years! On this day, many Supreme Domain Ancestors discovered that this treasure land was no longer producing Star Soul Sand. Day after day passed, but Star Soul Sand never appeared.
Moreover, they found that the void of this treasure land had become much more fragile.
"This treasure land is ruined!"
many Supreme Domain Ancestors lamented.
They waited for another few hundred years and finally had to accept the fact that this treasure land was ruined. Not only could Star Soul Sand no longer be born, but Holy Gold Sand had also completely ceased to appear.
In a million years, a total of 1,000 grains of Holy Gold Sand were born. Almost all the Supreme Domain Ancestors on the Supreme List had come here, so the competitive pressure was immense. Yet, in the end, Ye Tian still snatched 521 grains of Holy Gold Sand, showing his strength.
Most of the other Holy Gold Sand was snatched by the top ten Supreme Domain Ancestors on the Supreme List, while a few were taken by some lucky individuals.
In addition to several thousand grains of Holy Gold Sand, Ye Tian also obtained nearly ten million grains of Star Soul Sand.
What did ten million grains of Star Soul Sand represent? It was enough to create ten million Invincible Domain Ancestors! Of course, he wouldn't be so foolish as to use them to cultivate ten million ordinary Invincible Domain Ancestors. There was no need for that, and the War Sect wouldn't cultivate them that way either.
Moreover, he also needed a large amount of Star Soul Sand to strengthen his Holy Soul Light.
During these million years, Ye Tian had to constantly watch for the birth of Star Soul Sand and Holy Gold Sand, so he had very little time to cultivate. His cultivation time was very fragmented, but his soul had improved a lot under the influence of the Star Soul Sand. Now, the Holy Soul Light occupied sixty percent of his soul.
"Next, I'll go into seclusion for a while. Only by condensing the Holy Soul can my strength skyrocket and allow me to go to some of the forbidden areas of the Holy Soul Realm!"
Ye Tian murmured.
There were many opportunities in the Holy Soul Realm. According to the War Sect, some forbidden areas in the Holy Soul Realm contained immense opportunities. Unfortunately, some places were too dangerous; without strength comparable to the peak of an Invincible Domain Ancestor or the combat power of a Four-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor, one must never go there.
Those who entered the Holy Soul Realm were all Supreme Domain Ancestors; how could their combat power be that high? That was why those places were classified as forbidden areas.
But once Ye Tian condensed his Holy Soul and his strength surged, those places would no longer be forbidden areas, but his treasure lands! Ye Tian found a place and devoted himself to refining the Star Soul Sand.
It had to be said that the effect of the Star Soul Sand was indeed excellent.
While refining the Star Soul Sand, Ye Tian's Holy Soul Light grew rapidly.
At Ye Tian's refining speed, he could refine one grain of Star Soul Sand in almost a year. Ten thousand grains of Star Soul Sand could increase his Holy Soul Light from sixty percent to seventy percent, though the subsequent increases might be more difficult.
But according to Ye Tian's estimation, he probably only needed a hundred thousand grains of Star Soul Sand to have a 100% certainty of condensing the Holy Soul.
Refining a hundred thousand grains of Star Soul Sand would take him a hundred thousand years.
To be able to condense a Holy Soul in a mere hundred thousand years was extremely fast.
Ye Tian was refining the Star Soul Sand within a Time Array. In the outside world, only about a year would have passed.
From this, one could see how awesome the effect of the Star Soul Sand was! Grain after grain of Star Soul Sand was refined by Ye Tian, and eventually, a hundred thousand grains were consumed.
On this day.
Ye Tian was in the breakthrough stage. His Holy Soul Light almost filled his entire soul, with only a sliver of soul left that hadn't been completely transformed.
Thus, Ye Tian refined another grain of Star Soul Sand. Under its effect, the last sliver of his soul was also transformed into Holy Soul Light.
Finally, the qualitative change began!!! Countless rays of Holy Soul Light began to compress. It was as if Ye Tian's Holy Soul Light, which seemed to span hundreds of millions of feet in his soul sea, was gradually undergoing a qualitative change toward the size of a normal human body under infinite compression.
As the Holy Soul Light compressed, an incredibly terrifying soul pressure emanated from Ye Tian.
After a long time, Ye Tian's Holy Soul was finally condensed.
Once the Holy Soul was formed, Ye Tian clearly felt that his strength had improved significantly.
By activating the Holy Soul, his combat power would be terrifying. Furthermore, the power of the Holy Soul was nearly infinite and could recover quickly, allowing for sustained combat.
"My current strength should be comparable to the combat power of a peak Five-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor!"
Ye Tian estimated.
He didn't think his strength could cross the boundaries of Five-Step and Four-Step Invincible Domain Ancestors in one go; that was too difficult.
Above the Five-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor level, the strength gap between each step was enormous.
According to Ye Tian's estimation, unless he cultivated his Ancestral Techniques to the Minor Achievement stage or underwent a second qualitative change of his Holy Soul, it would be impossible to break through the combat power shackles and reach the level of a Four-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor.
"Cultivating Ancestral Techniques takes a long time, and I don't have time for that right now. However, as for the Holy Soul, I can definitely push it to undergo a second qualitative change!"
Ye Tian thought.
He still had many grains of Holy Gold Sand in his hands. Once he refined them, he could trigger a second qualitative change in his Holy Soul. The Holy Soul would then become even more terrifying, and it was said that special traits would be born, some of which were heaven-defying.
"Then let's refine the Holy Gold Sand!"
Ye Tian took out a grain of Holy Gold Sand and swallowed it into his soul sea, and his Holy Soul began to absorb its power.

Chapter 1430: Holy Soul Traits—Indestructible, Evolution!

Chapter 1430: Holy Soul Traits
——Indestructible, Evolution!
Although Holy Gold Sand was much smaller in size than Star Soul Sand, it far surpassed it in both quality and energy content.
As Ye Tian refined the Holy Gold Sand, it turned into golden light that showered over his Holy Soul, tempering it.
"My Holy Soul is truly being tempered and is strengthening rapidly. As expected of the legendary Holy Gold Sand!"
Ye Tian was excited.
This was a treasure that even the War Sect couldn't provide him, yet he had obtained 520 grains. This was more than enough to undergo a second qualitative change of his Holy Soul, with plenty to spare.
As time passed, Ye Tian consumed one grain of Holy Gold Sand after another.
His Holy Soul was far stronger than those of others, so achieving a second qualitative change naturally required more Holy Gold Sand. Fortunately, he had obtained a large amount; otherwise, he wouldn't have been able to sustain such consumption.
One grain! Ten grains! A hundred grains! It wasn't until Ye Tian had consumed 365 grains of Holy Gold Sand that his Holy Soul finally underwent its qualitative change.
Boom!!! Ye Tian's Holy Soul was covered in gold, and endless holy light radiated throughout his entire soul sea.
At the same time, Ye Tian's soul sea seemed to be expanding.
The soul sea appeared boundless, but in reality, the area perceived by the soul had limits. This expansion was a massive stroke of luck.
As the soul sea expanded, Ye Tian's Holy Soul also continued to strengthen. Densely packed rule patterns emerged on the Holy Soul. After a long time, the qualitative change was complete.
"My Holy Soul has strengthened fivefold!"
Ye Tian sensed it and murmured.
But that wasn't the main benefit; his Holy Soul had actually gained two additional traits.
Normally, a second qualitative change of the Holy Soul would only produce one trait, but his Holy Soul was likely too powerful, resulting in an extra one.
"Indestructible!"
"Evolution!"
These were the two traits of Ye Tian's Holy Soul.
The first trait, Indestructible, meant that Ye Tian's Holy Soul could not be destroyed. Unless a special method was used or the opponent's strength far exceeded Ye Tian's imagination, his Holy Soul could not be obliterated. This was one of the traits of the Holy Soul—Indestructible! The second trait, Evolution, was also incredibly powerful, but its side effects were significant.
Evolution allowed him to... deduce, derive, and upgrade any cultivation technique, Holy Technique, or Ancestral Technique. However, it consumed Holy Soul Source. Consuming even a little required a long time to recover. If too much was consumed, the Holy Soul Source would be severely damaged, causing heavy injury to the Holy Soul and potentially hindering future growth.
For others, they could only use Evolution once in a long while. It was helpful, but not game-breaking. This was normal; if it were too heaven-defying, it would be unnatural.
But for Ye Tian, the Evolution trait was terrifying! "I can clone my body. If I use the clone's Holy Soul to evolve techniques at any cost, that would be incredible! Even if the clone's Holy Soul collapses, it won't affect my main body. I can just clone myself again!"
Ye Tian said excitedly.
With this trait, his rise would be terrifyingly fast. In the future, he might even be able to deduce his own Ancestral Law.
After all, no matter how powerful the Copy Talent was, it couldn't deduce an original Ancestral Law, but the Evolution trait could.
Of course, without the Copy Talent, the Evolution trait would be practically useless! "My clone in the War Ancestor Realm is an old one and doesn't have the Evolution trait. I must dispel it!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Thus, Ye Tian's clone informed the higher-ups of the War Ancestor Realm and then directly dispelled itself to avoid any misunderstandings.
Afterward, Ye Tian spent ten thousand years inside a time acceleration formation. Once his copying ability was available again, he cloned himself once more.
As expected, the Copy Talent did not disappoint. The new clone not only possessed the Holy Soul but also both Holy Soul traits.
Then, Ye Tian had the clone begin the Evolution process.
"Evolve!"
Ye Tian's target this time was the Flowing Light Holy Technique. Perhaps he could use this evolution to upgrade it directly to an Ancestral Technique.
Boom!!!! Ye Tian's Holy Soul Source began to drain, but countless flashes of inspiration and insights flooded his mind. Under the effect of Evolution, the Flowing Light Holy Technique was constantly being refined and improved, evolving toward a higher level.
Time passed slowly, and the consumption of Holy Soul Source grew.
Before he knew it, one percent of his Holy Soul Source had been consumed. This was already a significant amount, enough to affect one's foundation.
But Ye Tian ignored it and continued the evolution.
After a long time, ten percent of the Holy Soul Source was gone! Twenty percent! Thirty percent! Ye Tian kept evolving, not caring about this clone at all.
Soon, fifty percent of the Holy Soul Source was consumed.
If it were a normal soul, it would surely be on the verge of collapse. However, Ye Tian's Holy Soul possessed the Indestructible trait, so even if ninety percent of the source was consumed, it wouldn't crumble or die; it would only suffer irreversible soul damage.
After another period of time, over ninety percent of Ye Tian's Holy Soul Source was exhausted. The Indestructible trait protected his Holy Soul from being annihilated.
At this moment, Ye Tian finally opened his eyes and smiled.
"Ninety-three percent of the Holy Soul Source is gone, but I've finally realized the key to upgrading a Holy Technique to an Ancestral Technique. However, I'll need to clone myself one more time and use the Holy Soul Evolution again to be certain of evolving the Flowing Light Holy Technique into an Ancestral Technique!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Thus, he dispelled the clone himself. Once the copying ability recovered, he cloned himself again and began the second evolution.
This time, after consuming only seventy percent of the Holy Soul Source, Ye Tian's Flowing Light Holy Technique was deduced into the Flowing Light Ancestral Technique.
"The Flowing Light Holy Technique has become the Flowing Light Ancestral Technique!"
Ye Tian performed the Flowing Light Ancestral Technique; its speed was far greater than the Holy Technique version! In the following days, Ye Tian continuously used the Evolution trait to deduce his Holy Techniques. Under this process, one Holy Technique after another was transformed into an Ancestral Technique.
However, the Space and Time Holy Techniques couldn't be upgraded to Ancestral Techniques for the time being. This was because Ye Tian had copied too few Space and Time Holy Talents to transform them into Ancestral Talents. Without Ancestral Talents, even the powerful Evolution trait struggled to upgrade Space and Time Holy Techniques unless he spent a vast amount of time on them.
He didn't have the time to evolve them over and over again. Moreover, time within the Holy Soul Realm was precious and could not be wasted.
With the boost from various Ancestral Techniques, Ye Tian's strength became incredibly formidable. Combined with the second qualitative change of his Holy Soul, his combat power now rivaled a Four-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor.
A Paramount Domain Ancestor rivaling a Four-Step Invincible Domain Ancestor—no one would believe it if told, but Ye Tian had truly achieved it.
"Next, it's time to check out those forbidden areas recorded by the War Sect!"
Ye Tian ended his seclusion and murmured.

Chapter 1431: Gray Crystal, Bestowing Spatial Saint Talent!

Chapter 1431: Gray Crystal, Bestowing Spatial Saint Talent
!
The Primordial Ancestral Realm has opened quite a few times since its inception, so the Battle Sect has naturally collected some information, including data on dozens of forbidden zones.
One piece of data piqued Ye Tian's interest. The forbidden zone in that data was somewhat special because the Saint Soul Beasts there possessed spatial abilities, and their strength was terrifying, even including Saint Soul Beasts at the Invincible Domain Ancestor level.
According to the data, without the combat power of a five-step peak Invincible Domain Ancestor, it would be difficult to survive inside; one would die instantly upon entry.
"That forbidden zone should be the territory of that... Saint Soul Beast race. Those Saint Soul Beasts might possess Spatial Saint Talents!"
Ye Tian speculated.
This was an opportunity. If it were true, he could copy a large number of Spatial Saint Talents, thereby elevating his own Spatial Saint Talent to the level of an Ancestral Talent. At that time, he could easily upgrade his Void Slash Saint Skill and Void Escape Saint Skill into Ancestral Skills, and his strength would increase significantly.
Swish! Ye Tian traveled quickly, and after some time, he finally arrived at that forbidden zone.
This forbidden zone was named the Void Realm of Unjust Death by the Ten Great Saint Sects of the Dark Saint Domain.
As soon as Ye Tian approached this forbidden zone, he felt a terrifying aura. However, this aura did not pose much of a threat to him. But for other peak Domain Ancestors, this was indeed an incredibly terrifying forbidden zone.
Naturally, other peak Domain Ancestors would not come to such a dangerous forbidden zone, so Ye Tian was the only one here.
Boom!!!! Ye Tian took a step and entered the Void Realm of Unjust Death.
Just as he entered the Void Realm of Unjust Death, Ye Tian immediately sensed groups of Saint Soul Beasts rushing toward him.
Among them, many Saint Soul Beasts were actually at the Invincible Domain Ancestor realm.
This wasn't just one or two, but many.
"No wonder this forbidden zone is so dangerous; there are too many Invincible Domain Ancestors!"
Ye Tian murmured.
These Saint Soul Beasts were almost all the same, looking like large plates that could split into countless tentacles.
These Saint Soul Beasts rushed over, their countless tentacles manipulating spatial power to form dense clusters of spatial spears. Each tentacle controlled a spatial spear, piercing toward him.
Ye Tian did not kill these Saint Soul Beasts immediately. Instead, he used his Copy Talent to investigate their talents.
As soon as the Copy Talent investigated, he immediately perceived their talents.
"They really do have Spatial Saint Talents!"
Ye Tian said joyfully.
[Saint Talent: Void Spear] "Copy!"
"Copy!"
"Copy!"
Ye Tian frantically copied these Void Spear Saint Talents. In the blink of an eye, he had copied a large number of them before finally taking action.
"Ancestral Armor!"
"Golden Silk Ancestral Skill!"
"Streamer Ancestral Skill!"
"Golden Body Ancestral Skill!"
"Tyrant Strength Ancestral Skill!"
.... Ye Tian performed one Ancestral Skill after another. His combat power was incredibly terrifying, and a single light strike could slay a group of Saint Soul Beasts.
After a short while, the area was littered with the corpses of Saint Soul Beasts. A significant amount of Saint Soul power dissipated from these corpses and merged into Ye Tian's soul. However, Ye Tian's Saint Soul had already completed its second qualitative change, so this small amount of Saint Soul power was useless to him.
Ye Tian swept through the area. There was even a Saint Soul Beast comparable to a five-step Invincible Domain Ancestor, but under Ye Tian's frantic attacks, it also turned into a corpse.
Day after day of slaughtering, Ye Tian didn't know how long he had been fighting.
There were many Saint Soul Beasts here, and most were at the Invincible Domain Ancestor realm, making them relatively difficult to kill. Naturally, it took more time.
A long time later, Ye Tian looked around and saw no more traces of Saint Soul Beasts. He had arrived at the center of the Void Realm of Unjust Death.
Here, he saw a gray crystal, the size of a star, suspended in the void.
"This is..."
Ye Tian observed it carefully but could not recognize the use of this gray crystal.
However, Ye Tian felt the power of space emanating from it. A special spatial power seemed to be influencing Ye Tian's soul, as if it wanted to transform it.
"Could it be that this gray crystal can allow someone to birth a Spatial Saint Talent?"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
If it were true, then this gray crystal was simply too heaven-defying! "Collect!"
Ye Tian tried to collect the gray crystal, but he did not succeed. It seemed to be a part of the Saint Soul Realm itself, making it very difficult to strip away.
Thus, Ye Tian used his full strength to collect it, even mobilizing all the power in his body. Only then did he slowly move the gray crystal into his internal world.
However, as soon as the gray crystal was collected, it actually began to shrink. Furthermore, its light became incredibly dim, and its spatial aura became very weak.
In the end, it turned into a crystal the height of a person, having weakened countless times over.
Holding the gray crystal, Ye Tian obtained a set of information from it.
"It can create nine Void Spear Saint Talent users!"
Ye Tian said in surprise.
Originally, it could probably create many Void Spear Saint Talents; the spatial talent race here was an example.
However, that was due to the special nature of the Saint Soul Realm. If it were taken outside, it would not have such a terrifying effect!
Therefore, after being stripped away, this crystal lost the amplification of the Saint Soul Realm and could only bestow the Void Spear Saint Talent to nine people.
But even so, it was still incredibly terrifying. If the Primordial Ancestors knew about it, they would likely be interested.
This gray crystal was undoubtedly Ye Tian's greatest harvest.
"Now that I've copied so many Spatial Saint Talents, it's time to try fusing them into an Ancestral Talent!"
Ye Tian sat cross-legged and began to fuse that large number of Spatial Saint Talents.
Under time acceleration, Ye Tian fused one Spatial Saint Talent after another. After a long time, he successfully fused all of them.
And the Spatial Saint Talent successfully transformed into a Spatial Ancestral Talent.
[Ancestral Talent: Space] Seeing these words, Ye Tian was extremely excited.
Subsequently, he began to duplicate his body and had the duplicates perform derivations to deduce and comprehend the Void Slash Saint Skill and the Void Escape Saint Skill.
Just like that, more years passed. The Void Slash Saint Skill and Void Escape Saint Skill finally became the Void Slash Ancestral Skill and Void Escape Ancestral Skill.
How powerful was the Void Slash Saint Skill? The Void Escape Ancestral Skill almost made Ye Tian invincible.
Therefore, with these two additional Ancestral Skills, Ye Tian's strength surged once again.
If he could cultivate these Ancestral Skills to the minor completion stage, Ye Tian's strength would likely reach the peak of a four-step Invincible Domain Ancestor's combat power.
"Time to check out the other forbidden zones!"
Ye Tian cast the Void Escape Ancestral Skill and vanished.

Chapter 1432: Breaking Through to the Invincible Domain Ancestor Realm!

Chapter 1432: Breaking Through to the Invincible Domain Ancestor Realm
!
Tens of millions of years passed.
Ye Tian ventured into one forbidden zone after another within the Holy Soul Realm. Relying on his combat power as a four-step Invincible Domain Ancestor, he obtained great benefits from various forbidden areas.
Furthermore, he frequently used his duplicate bodies to perform evolutions, evolving various Ancestral Techniques.
After all, his Ancestral Techniques were only at the Initial stage. If he could raise them to the Small Success stage, his strength would receive a terrifying boost.
Under normal circumstances, raising an Ancestral Technique to the Small Success stage would require a long period of bitter cultivation.
However, if he used evolution to improve them, it would be countless times faster.
Through repeated evolutions, the Holy Soul of Ye Tian's duplicate bodies collapsed time and again. Fortunately, the final results were indeed quite good.
Ancestral Techniques such as the Gold Silk Ancestral Technique, the Void Slash Ancestral Technique, and the Space Escape Ancestral Technique were all raised to the Small Success stage by Ye Tian. However, if he wanted to raise them to the Great Success stage, it would still take a long time even with the evolution trait.
The Holy Soul Realm was nearing its closing day. At that time, even if Ye Tian did not want to leave, once the Original Ancestral World sealed itself off, everyone would be forcibly kicked out. This was the rule of this world, and even an Invincible Domain Ancestor could not violate it.
At this moment, Ye Tian was organizing his gains.
He had no interest in organizing ordinary treasures; he only sorted through the more precious ones.
Star Soul Sand, Holy Gold Sand, and Space Holy Talent Crystals were the treasures he had obtained at the very beginning.
From the later forbidden zones, he had obtained many good things.
For example, the Ancestral Blood Grass, which could allow one's Holy Body to easily reach the limit realm; the Void Soul Stone, a supreme treasure that could instantly increase one's comprehension by a thousandfold; and the Holy Blood Marrow, which could reshape one's foundation.
Especially the Holy Blood Marrow—this item was of little use to Ye Tian, but for his family members, it was a supreme treasure.
After all, his family members initially lacked resources and inheritances, so their foundations were not very good. Although they were considered geniuses compared to ordinary Domain Ancestors, their talent and strength were only average compared to the true Holy Sons of the Dark Holy Domain.
But the Holy Blood Marrow could reshape one's foundation, allowing one to become a monstrous genius in a single step.
Previously, the Holy Blood Marrow was always out of stock on the Battle Gate's treasury exchange list; the Battle Gate simply didn't have any.
Even many Supreme-level Domain Ancestors were searching for Holy Blood Marrow, which showed its preciousness.
However, it could not be found.
This time, Ye Tian found ten pieces of Holy Blood Marrow in a forbidden zone. To obtain these ten pieces of Holy Blood Marrow, he fought for a long time with a terrifying existence in that forbidden zone, one that was at least as strong as a four-step Invincible Domain Ancestor. He used his duplicate body to forcibly cast the Five Elements Seal to trap the opponent, while his main body went to steal the Holy Blood Marrow. Only then did he manage to snatch them away.
Of course, he did not kill the opponent, nor could he.
Besides these treasures, there were many other treasures in great quantities. Once brought back to the human race, they would definitely cause the human race's strength to soar.
The only pity was that there were too few Time Holy Talents in the Holy Soul Realm, so he did not manage to fuse a Time Ancestral Talent. This was the only regrettable point.
Another few tens of thousands of years passed.
A repulsive force arrived.
Swish swish swish!!!! One by one, the Peak Domain Ancestors were sent out.
When Ye Tian regained his senses, he found that he had already appeared outside the Original Ancestral World. Then, the Supreme-level Domain Ancestors of the Battle Gate brought Ye Tian back to prevent experts from other factions from attacking him.
"Let's go, back to the Battle Ancestor World!"
The Fire Pattern Battle Ancestor of the Battle Gate spoke.
In the Battle Ancestor World, Ye Tian and a group of Peak Domain Ancestors had returned.
This time, one-tenth of the Battle Gate's Peak Domain Ancestors had fallen forever in the Holy Soul Realm, while some Holy Lands had lost all of their Peak Domain Ancestors, suffering even greater losses.
Of course, as long as one person returned, that faction would not lose out.
On this day.
The Fire Pattern Battle Ancestor gathered Ye Tian and the others, mainly to announce one thing: they hoped Ye Tian and the others would trade a portion of their treasures and resources to the Battle Gate, as many resources from the Holy Soul Realm were lacking within the Battle Gate.
Of course, this was not a free trade; they could obtain even more precious resources from the Battle Gate in return.
Ye Tian traded some Star Soul Sand and a small amount of Holy Gold Sand to the Battle Gate, and also traded many other resources one by one.
Subsequently, Ye Tian exchanged for an incredibly precious treasure from the Battle Gate—the Starry Holy Stele! The sole function of the Starry Holy Stele was to open a Starry Barrier. Once opened, even a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor would be unable to break through this barrier's defense in a short amount of time.
Ye Tian was also worried that a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor might take action against him or the Profound Void Holy Realm, which was why he exchanged for the Starry Holy Stele.
This way, if a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor attacked, he could promptly activate the Starry Holy Stele to block the enemy's attack and then request the Supreme-level Domain Ancestors of the Battle Gate to intervene.
However, the Starry Holy Stele could only be activated three times in total. After three times, it would turn into an ordinary holy stele.
But even so, the value of the Starry Holy Stele was extremely high, and Ye Tian only barely managed to exchange for this one treasure.
Using so many rare treasures to exchange for a single Starry Holy Stele, Ye Tian felt it was very much worth it.
Afterward, Ye Tian left the Battle Ancestor World and returned to the Profound Void Holy Realm.
Now wealthy and influential, Ye Tian very extravagantly used a Ten Thousand Void Star Leaf and soon arrived at the Dao Mountain Domain, returning to the Profound Void Holy Realm.
In the Profound Void Holy Realm.
Ye Tian manifested the Starry Holy Stele and linked it with the origin of the Profound Void Holy Realm, ensuring that the Starry Holy Stele could be activated at any time.
"With the Starry Holy Stele, I don't need to worry about safety issues. Next, it's time to charge into the Invincible Domain Ancestor realm!"
Ye Tian murmured.
He had already reached the limit of the Peak Domain Ancestor realm, and even his Holy Soul had completed its second qualitative change. Therefore, there was no need to continue accumulating in the Peak Domain Ancestor realm.
Choosing an auspicious day, Ye Tian entered the Holy Stele World to charge into the Invincible Domain Ancestor realm.
For Ye Tian, breaking through from Peak Domain Ancestor to Invincible Domain Ancestor was very simple. He had already condensed a Holy Soul, and it was a Holy Soul that had undergone a second qualitative change, making the breakthrough to Invincible Domain Ancestor extremely easy.
Boom!!!!! The shackles were broken, and his Peak Domain Body began to transform toward an Invincible Domain Body.
Countless amounts of Chaos Origin Energy surged into Ye Tian's body, assisting him in completing the transformation of his Domain Body.
At the same time, Ye Tian's Holy Soul also underwent a change, becoming stronger and stronger.
Furthermore, a brand-new Holy Talent was born deep within Ye Tian's Holy Soul. This was his Natal Holy Talent, and it was also the Holy Talent that suited Ye Tian best.
After a long time, the breakthrough was complete.
And the first thing Ye Tian did was not to check his strength, but to see what that Natal Holy Talent was.

Chapter 1433: Innate Ancestral Talent: Copy!

Chapter 1433: Innate Ancestral Talent
: Copy!
[Innate Ancestral Talent: Copy] Seeing the words "Ancestral Talent," Ye Tian was stunned.
"An Ancestral Talent, not a Holy Talent?"
Ye Tian originally thought he would give birth to an Innate Holy Talent, but he didn't expect it to be an Innate Ancestral Talent.
"Could it be related to the second qualitative change of my Holy Soul?"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
"No!"
Ye Tian shook his head. "It's definitely not just the second qualitative change of the Holy Soul. In the Dark Holy Domain, there are people who have achieved the second qualitative change, but none have ever possessed an Innate Ancestral Talent.
It should be related to my large number of Ancestral Talents. I fused too many Holy Talents, which in turn fused into various Ancestral Talents. This directly affected my Holy Soul, causing the most suitable Innate Holy Talent to evolve into an Innate Ancestral Talent!"
The Innate Ancestral Talent 'Copy' was indeed related to his copying ability; it was a talent perfectly suited for him.
Ye Tian's consciousness connected with the Innate Ancestral Talent 'Copy,' and he learned the effect of this Ancestral Talent.
This 'Copy' was different from his Copy Talent; it copied skills.
For example, Holy Skills and Ancestral Skills—he could copy them and make them his own.
This ability was terrifying, second only to his Copy Talent! It could even be said that the birth of this 'Copy' Ancestral Talent was influenced by his original Copy Talent.
Without the existence of the Copy Talent, he wouldn't have been able to form the Innate Ancestral Talent 'Copy.'
"This way, I won't need to exchange for Ancestral Skills anymore!"
Ye Tian thought.
Of course, while this ability seemed incredible, Ye Tian wouldn't copy too many Ancestral Skills; ordinary Ancestral Skills weren't very useful to him.
Moreover, with his vast number of Ancestral Talents and the Evolution trait, he could fully deduce Holy Skills to the level of Ancestral Skills. Thus, the Innate Ancestral Talent 'Copy' was merely the icing on the cake.
Besides, there were very few Domain Ancestors in the Dark Holy Domain who knew Ancestral Skills, so he likely wouldn't find many good ones to copy anyway.
"If I get the chance in the future, I'll copy a few good Ancestral Skills!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Now that he had just broken through to the Invincible Domain Ancestor realm, it was a time for rapid growth, so he did not end his seclusion but continued to cultivate.
Tempering the Invincible Domain Body was extremely difficult; reaching the limit would likely take a very long time.
However, he had gained too many benefits from the Holy Soul Realm. Many of those resources could be used to temper the Invincible Domain Body, so he wasn't worried about his cultivation speed.
But for now, he wanted to improve the strength of the Human Race.
For instance, he had obtained Spatial Holy Talent Crystals from the Holy Soul Realm, which could grant nine people the Spatial Holy Talent.
Additionally, he had obtained a lot of Star Soul Sand and Holy Gold Sand, which could easily create Invincible Domain Ancestors.
"Son, daughter, Yue'er, Xiao Yu, come here!"
Ye Tian sent a message to his family.
Soon, Xiao Yue, Ye Xingchen, Ye Hai, and Ye Yu arrived.
"Husband!"
"Father!"
"Brother!"
They called out.
"This Holy Blood Marrow can reshape your foundation. After taking it, your foundation will be reshaped to rival the top monstrous geniuses!"
Ye Tian took out the Holy Blood Marrow and handed it to the four of them.
"Holy Blood Marrow!"
They hadn't heard of it, but they knew it was extremely precious just by the name.
They didn't stand on ceremony with Ye Tian; they each took it and consumed the Holy Blood Marrow in front of him.
Boom!!!! The four of them began to transform; their entire beings started to undergo a metamorphosis.
From their physical bodies to their souls and then to their origins, everything was changing. This was what it meant to truly reshape one's foundation.
While some treasures could cause a qualitative change in the physical body, they couldn't change the soul or the origin; that wouldn't be called reshaping the foundation.
After reshaping their foundations, they would have a period of adaptation. During this time, as long as they worked hard, they could improve rapidly.
Days passed, and a full ten thousand years went by before the four of them completed their foundation reshaping.
At this time, Ye Tian stripped some Holy Talents from himself and gave them to the four of them.
In this way, they also became Holy Talent Users.
In the past, he hadn't dared to do this for fear of leaking the existence of Holy Talents, as the impact would have been too great.
But now he wasn't afraid. He had obtained the Spatial Holy Talent Crystals from the Holy Soul Realm. He would choose a few human geniuses and grant them the Spatial Holy Talent.
This way, other forces would discover that he had obtained such a treasure that could grant Holy Talents. Although they would be envious, since Ye Tian would have already used it, they naturally couldn't seize it.
In that case, they would also believe that the Holy Talents of Xiao Yue and the others were created using treasures like the Spatial Holy Talent Crystals.
At that time, they would only think that Ye Tian's luck was extraordinary and would never suspect his Copy Talent.
In the following days, Ye Tian began to select suitable candidates from among the human geniuses, placing character as the top priority and even personally conducting multiple assessments.
After a million years and numerous assessments, he selected eight human geniuses to be granted the Spatial Holy Talent.
The Human Race Holy Temple.
Eight human geniuses arrived here, witnessed by many human Domain Ancestors.
Ye Tian took out the Spatial Holy Talent Crystal and said, "This treasure was obtained by me from the Holy Soul Realm. I'm not sure of its exact name, so I call it the Spatial Holy Talent Crystal. Today, I will use it to grant the eight of you a Spatial Holy Talent.
Once you obtain the Spatial Holy Talent, you will become Holy Talent Users, and your talent will instantly leap above countless geniuses!"
Holy Talent Users!!! Upon hearing this, the eight human geniuses were immediately ecstatic.
They naturally knew what Holy Talent Users were! There weren't many Holy Talent Users in the Dark Holy Domain... only the descendants of Supreme-level Domain Ancestors had a hope of being born with a Holy Talent! They never expected that ordinary cultivators like themselves would one day have the chance to obtain a Holy Talent.
The other human Domain Ancestors were extremely envious, wishing they could seize the Spatial Holy Talent Crystal, but they didn't dare. It was Ye Tian's treasure, and they had no right to it.
Boom!!! Ye Tian activated the Spatial Holy Talent Crystal, and eight beams of light erupted from it, shooting into the bodies of the eight human geniuses.
Instantly, the souls of the eight human geniuses felt as if they were being remodeled by a terrifying, supreme power. Each of them was in great pain, but they all endured it.
Days passed, and it took a full few months before the Spatial Holy Talent was completely born within them.
At this moment, they sensed their souls slightly and realized the existence of the Spatial Holy Talent, making them all incredibly excited.
Immediately, they thanked Ye Tian one after another before withdrawing.
Afterward, Ye Tian went to the Battle World Tower and contacted the Fire-Pattern Battle Ancestor.
He planned to trade the Spatial Holy Talent Crystal to the Battle Sect to prove that the human race's Spatial Holy Talents truly came from the crystal and were not from a fabricated origin.
This was why he had left one remaining slot for the Spatial Holy Talent.
After such a transaction, the Battle Sect would not suspect him, and other forces wouldn't either.

Chapter 1434: Hunyuan Ancestral Water, Invincible Domain Ancestor Perfection!

Chapter 1434: Hunyuan Ancestral Water, Invincible Domain Ancestor Perfection
!
Boom!!!! Fire Pattern War Ancestor appeared in the War World Tower and came before Ye Tian.
"Ye Tian, were you looking for me?"
Fire Pattern War Ancestor asked.
He saw that Ye Tian's cultivation was no longer that of a Supreme Domain Ancestor, but an Invincible Domain Ancestor.
He then continued, "It shouldn't be about your breakthrough to the Invincible Domain Ancestor realm, right?"
"Lord Fire Pattern War Ancestor, it is naturally not about my breakthrough. Rather, I have a treasure I wish to trade to the War Gate. However, this treasure is quite valuable, so I needed Lord Fire Pattern War Ancestor to step forward!"
Saying this, Ye Tian took out the Space Saint Talent Crystal.
As soon as Fire Pattern War Ancestor saw this Space Saint Talent Crystal, he was instantly shocked. "A Saint Talent Stone, and a Space Saint Talent Stone at that? You actually have such a treasure?"
"Is its name the Saint Talent Stone?"
Ye Tian felt that his naming was quite accurate, having only added the word 'crystal.'
"This Space Saint Talent Stone of yours has had some of its Saint Talents used up; there's only one quota left, right?"
Fire Pattern War Ancestor suddenly asked.
"Yes!"
Ye Tian admitted, "I bestowed Space Saint Talents upon some geniuses of our Human Race, leaving only one slot. I plan to trade it to the War Gate. The War Gate should be interested, right?"
"Hahaha, the War Gate is certainly interested. Even I am interested. Not a few of my descendants lack Saint Talents. Why don't you trade it directly to me? How about it?"
Fire Pattern War Ancestor asked.
"That is fine, but I hope Fire Pattern War Ancestor can spread the news of this trade!"
Ye Tian suggested.
Fire Pattern War Ancestor was startled for a moment, then smiled.
He understood Ye Tian's purpose and nodded. "Fine, I will let it be known. You don't need to worry about the matter of so many Saint Talent users appearing in your Human Race!"
"Then, many thanks to Lord Fire Pattern War Ancestor!"
Ye Tian said gratefully.
Subsequently, Ye Tian and Fire Pattern War Ancestor completed the trade.
The Space Saint Talent Stone now belonged to Fire Pattern War Ancestor, while Ye Tian obtained a very precious treasure from Fire Pattern War Ancestor—Hunyuan Ancestral Water.
Hunyuan Ancestral Water was a very precious cultivation resource that was of great help to Invincible Domain Ancestors, allowing them to quickly temper their Invincible Domain Bodies.
As long as one refined the Hunyuan Ancestral Water, they could advance from the initial stage of the Invincible Domain Ancestor realm to the perfection stage, without needing endless ages to slowly temper the Invincible Domain Body and increase their cultivation.
Therefore, for a newly promoted Invincible Domain Ancestor, once they possessed Hunyuan Ancestral Water, they could rapidly increase their strength and raise their cultivation to the perfection stage of the Invincible Domain Ancestor realm.
Other resources were not of much help to Ye Tian. Perhaps others would be more eager to obtain treasures that could add a hint of breaking the physical limit, such as turning a Saint Body into an Ancestral Body or a Saint Skill into an Ancestral Skill.
But Ye Tian did not need those treasures; he needed a treasure like Hunyuan Ancestral Water more.
Once he used the Hunyuan Ancestral Water to raise his cultivation, his strength would increase to a terrifying degree.
For example, having just broken through to the Invincible realm, his combat power had directly jumped to the peak of a Step Three Invincible Domain Ancestor, only one step away from Step Two combat power.
If he broke through to the Perfection realm, his combat power would likely be comparable to the Five Thunders Domain Ancestor, which was combat power that surpassed a Step One Invincible Domain Ancestor!
After the trade, Ye Tian used his Life Ancestral Talent to look at Fire Pattern War Ancestor's Ancestral Skill.
[Ancestral Skill: Fire Pattern War Body]
Regarding this Ancestral Skill, Ye Tian had seen it before.
Back then, Fire Pattern War Ancestor had manifested this Ancestral Skill, turning into a terrifying existence comparable to the size of a domain, defeating a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor of the same rank in a single blow. Its power was incredibly fearsome.
Of course, this Ancestral Skill was actually quite ordinary; it was only because Fire Pattern War Ancestor's cultivation was high that it could erupt with such terrifying power.
"Copy it. It might be useful in the future!"
Ye Tian casually copied this Ancestral Skill.
Afterward, Ye Tian left the War World Tower, returned to the Saint Tablet World, and began his cultivation.
He took out a small bottle of Hunyuan Ancestral Water, extracted a single drop, swallowed it, and began to refine it.
Boom!!!!! Terrifying energy tempered Ye Tian's Invincible Domain Body, and his body was rapidly tempered and improved.
"What a terrifying improvement effect. Even Ancestral Medicines are useless to me now, but Hunyuan Ancestral Water has such a terrifying effect. The value of just this one drop is more precious than an ordinary Saint Artifact!"
Ye Tian murmured.
He continued to cultivate, refining drop after drop of Hunyuan Ancestral Water, and his cultivation progressed rapidly!
Initial Invincible Domain Ancestor! Middle Invincible Domain Ancestor! Late Invincible Domain Ancestor! Great Perfection Invincible Domain Ancestor!
When Ye Tian had completely raised his cultivation to the perfection stage of the Invincible Domain Ancestor realm, about 10% of the Hunyuan Ancestral Water remained. He could save it for his wife and children to use in the future.
Boom!!!! An endless pressure spread out, but it was blocked by the Saint Tablet World. Otherwise, this pressure alone could have blanketed the entire Dao Mountain Domain.
"I am very strong!"
Ye Tian discovered that he was far, far stronger than when he was at the initial stage of the Invincible Domain Ancestor realm... He could easily crush his former self with a casual hand.
Moreover, his Saint Soul had also strengthened dozens of times. After all, as his cultivation rose, his Saint Soul naturally improved along with it.
However, this was not yet the true limit!
Many Invincible Domain Ancestors who cultivated to the perfection stage only had the combat power of a Step Three or Four Invincible Domain Ancestor, but they could slowly improve to Step Two or even Step One combat power in the future.
That was because the physical body of an Invincible Domain Ancestor was too terrifying; many Invincible Domain Ancestors were unable to fully exert their own power.
It might seem like they were exerting 100% of their power, but in many cases, they could continue to gain more control.
After an Invincible Domain Ancestor reached the perfection stage, it was a process of achieving complete control.
And this kind of control was very difficult to cultivate. Controlling the physical body to exert its inherent power was just ordinary control. If one could exert ten times their own power, that was impressive control. If one could control a hundred times their own power, it could be called peerless genius.
If one could control 365 times their own power, they would reach their own limit.
At that point, one could attempt to break the physical limit and undergo a transformation of the Invincible Domain Body.
Back then, Gu Heng Domain Ancestor had completed three transformations of the Invincible Domain Body. Once nine transformations were completed, one could promote to a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor.
And wanting to control 365 times one's physical strength was very difficult. For example, Five Thunders Domain Ancestor had not achieved it, though that also had to do with him reaching the Half-step Ancestral Body.
In short, the stronger the physical body, the harder the control. If one was monstrous enough to have cultivated to the level of an Ancestral Body, it would be even harder to control.
This was also why Five Thunders Domain Ancestor was much stronger than Gu Heng Domain Ancestor but had not yet broken the limit.
But for an Invincible Domain Ancestor like Five Thunders, once they broke the physical limit in the future, their strength would be terrifying.
"I expect I will try to control my physical strength after I have refined the Ancestral Body!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
After all, he wanted to become the strongest Invincible Domain Ancestor, Supreme-level Domain Ancestor, and Progenitor-level being. Therefore, he naturally had to reach an incredibly terrifying level in every realm.

Chapter 1435: Successful Evolution, Eternal Indestructible Ancestral Body!

Chapter 1435: Successful Evolution, Eternal Indestructible Ancestral Body
!
The Ancestral Body is the evolved version of the Holy Body. Under normal circumstances, it is many times more difficult for an Invincible Territory Ancestor to master an Ancestral Body than to master Ancestral Techniques.
Within the Battle Sect, only the Five Thunder Territory Ancestor had mastered a half-step Ancestral Body, and he was still some distance away from a true Ancestral Body.
"If I want the Eternal Indestructible Holy Body to break through its limits, ordinary resources are useless. I can only rely on the Evolution trait!"
Ye Tian murmured.
The Evolution trait, deducing the Eternal Indestructible Holy Body—this was more reliable than any resource.
Perhaps the Five Thunder Territory Ancestor had obtained a rare supreme treasure to break the Holy Body's limit, but Ye Tian didn't have such a treasure, nor did he know where to find one.
All he had was the Evolution trait.
Of course, Ye Tian knew very well that even with the Evolution trait, breaking the Holy Body's limit would likely take a very long time and require countless body replications.
Fortunately, Ye Tian had broken through to the Invincible Territory Ancestor realm. His Holy Soul was many times stronger, enough to support the Evolution trait's deductions for a long time, with much better results than before.
"Replicate body!"
Ye Tian replicated his body once more, and the replicated body began to evolve, deducing the Eternal Indestructible Holy Body.
He deduced the Eternal Indestructible Holy Body toward the Ancestral Body realm step by step. Previously, Ye Tian had no clue, but with the help of the Evolution trait and the continuous consumption of his Holy Soul's origin, he deduced it bit by bit.
After a long time, Ye Tian's Holy Soul origin was completely exhausted, and the replicated body died instantly.
"The progress is about one-ten-thousandth!"
Ye Tian estimated.
In other words, he needed to replicate his body ten thousand times and exhaust his Holy Soul origin ten thousand times through the Evolution trait to truly deduce the Ancestral Body and break the Holy Body's limit.
What did it mean to exhaust the Holy Soul origin ten thousand times? If anyone else had obtained the Evolution trait, they only had one life; they wouldn't dare exhaust their origin. Even a slight depletion would take ages to recover.
Therefore, even if others obtained the Evolution trait, it wouldn't be of much help. Only for Ye Tian was the Evolution trait incredibly powerful.
Time passed, and in the blink of an eye... a billion years had gone by.
The human race had over a dozen Saint Talent users, and after a billion years, these dozen or so individuals had naturally risen to prominence.
Many human Territory Ancestors, after reaching the peak of the Supreme Territory Ancestor realm, could exchange for a grain of Star Soul Sand from the Saint Hall at a very low cost to give birth to Soul Holy Light and charge into the Invincible Territory Ancestor realm.
Now, after a billion years, the human race had produced hundreds of Invincible Territory Ancestors.
This was mainly because reaching the Supreme Territory Ancestor realm was no simple feat, and growing the soul to a certain level at the peak of that realm was also difficult.
Additionally, Ye Tian was strict with the exchange requirements for Star Soul Sand; it wasn't... given away freely.
Thus, only about a thousand people had obtained Star Soul Sand. Some human Supreme Territory Ancestors, even after birthing Soul Holy Light, wanted to birth a Holy Soul first and weren't in a hurry to charge into the Invincible realm; otherwise, the human race would have already produced over a thousand Invincible Territory Ancestors.
The ones who made the most progress were undoubtedly Ye Tian's family members.
With the help of Saint Blood Marrow, they all established their foundations. With the massive resources Ye Tian provided, they also gained Saint Talents and mastered Saint Techniques one by one.
Moreover, they had Star Soul Sand and Saint Gold Sand. Ye Tian was not stingy with these resources and supplied them all to his family.
Consequently, Xiao Yue, Ye Xingchen, and the others all condensed Holy Souls and underwent a second qualitative change.
Now, they had all broken through to the Invincible Territory Ancestor realm and mastered several Saint Techniques. Although their cultivation hadn't reached the peak of the Invincible realm yet, they had reached the peak of the early stage, not far from the middle stage.
Their combat power had also reached the level of a Four-Step Invincible Territory Ancestor, which wasn't considered weak even in the Dark Saint Domain.
...."I've finally understood it!"
Just as his replicated body was about to exhaust its origin, Ye Tian's eyes snapped open, filled with joy.
By now, he had completely understood the key mysteries of breaking the shackles of the Eternal Indestructible Holy Body to reach the Ancestral Body realm.
"Then, let's break through!"
Ye Tian's main body began to charge toward the Ancestral Body realm.
Boom!!!! The Holy Body cracked bit by bit. Through repeated cracking, reconstruction, and more cracking and reconstruction, the interior of his body underwent countless evolutions and reorganizations. After trillions of reorganizations, the shackles were finally broken.
This was a method Ye Tian had deduced himself; it was only applicable to him and not to others.
Because everyone's body is different, and since he evolved based on himself, it could only be used by him.
The shackles were broken; the limit of the Holy Body was shattered.
