Five Thunders Domain Ancestor, Guhai Domain Ancestor, and others were dumbfounded when they learned of this event.
"What? Myriad Law Domain Ancestor killed a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor?"
Guhai Domain Ancestor was dazed.
He felt that it wasn't that long ago—only a few billion years or so. To him, this amount of time was merely the duration of a single secluded meditation session.
The Myriad Law Domain Ancestor, Ye Tian, who was once very weak and required his help, had now surpassed him. Moreover, he had slain a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor, placing him far above himself.
"An Invincible Domain Ancestor killing a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor... how is that possible?"
Five Thunders Domain Ancestor was also dazed.
He had condensed a Half-step Ancestral Body and comprehended Ancestral Techniques, making him incredibly monstrous—to some extent, even more so than some Supreme-level Domain Ancestors.
But in terms of actual combat power, he could at most exchange a move or two with the weakest, newly promoted Supreme-level Domain Ancestor. In a real fight, he wouldn't be able to defeat one.
And Jinchen Holy Ancestor of the Qingyuan Holy Land was a mid-stage Supreme-level Domain Ancestor. It was said he was injured, but by now, his injuries should have mostly recovered.
If Ye Tian could kill Jinchen Holy Ancestor, he could probably crush him with ease!
"Myriad Law Domain Ancestor is truly terrifying!"
Five Thunders Domain Ancestor lamented.
Ye Tian did not know the evaluation other Invincible Domain Ancestors had of him. At this moment, he had returned to the Xuanxu Holy World in the Daoshan Domain.
After Ye Tian returned, he went to the Battle World Tower with doubts and met Fire-Pattern War Ancestor.
"Fire-Pattern War Ancestor, I have some matters to consult you about!"
Ye Tian said very seriously.
"Oh? What is it?"
Fire-Pattern War Ancestor asked.
"Fire-Pattern War Ancestor, while I was fighting Jinchen Holy Ancestor, he brought out something that injured me. If it weren't for my Undying Ancestral Technique, I'm afraid I would have been heavily wounded!"
Ye Tian described that piece of paper, or rather, the talisman. He particularly described the phantom image in detail, even manifesting it for Fire-Pattern War Ancestor to see.
At this moment, Ye Tian noticed that Fire-Pattern War Ancestor's expression became very solemn.
"Ye Tian, regarding that phantom, it is actually a great secret of the Dark Holy Region—no, it should be said, the Dark Forbidden Region. It's a secret even greater than those of the Dark Destruction Region. Basically, only Supreme-level Domain Ancestors are qualified to know it, and orders have been given not to leak it.
Now that you have slain Jinchen Holy Ancestor, you are indeed qualified to know this secret!"
Fire-Pattern War Ancestor said seriously.
"What secret?"
Ye Tian was shocked.
Fire-Pattern War Ancestor said, "You should have heard that Jinchen Holy Ancestor was injured and had been healing.
Although Jinchen Holy Ancestor had a home-field advantage in the Qingyuan Holy World and could exert stronger power, in reality, a Holy World doesn't provide much of a boost to a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor, and the arrays of a Holy Land aren't of much help either. Otherwise, Jinchen Holy Ancestor would have fled into the Qingyuan Holy World long ago.
Rumors outside say that Jinchen Holy Ancestor was hiding from a rival Supreme-level Domain Ancestor and didn't dare leave the Qingyuan Holy World.
But if there really were such a rival Supreme-level Domain Ancestor, the Qingyuan Holy World wouldn't be able to stop them; they would have charged in long ago!"
"That's true, it doesn't make sense!"
Ye Tian only now realized this problem.
For someone with his level of strength, the Xuanxu Holy World no longer provided much of a boost.
But ordinary Domain Ancestors didn't know this and thought that a Holy World still provided a massive boost to Supreme-level Domain Ancestors. Thus, those outside rumors were simply unrealistic.
"Then how was Jinchen Holy Ancestor heavily injured?"
Ye Tian asked.
"He was... heavily injured by the kind of terrifying existence you described, which is why he had to return to the Qingyuan Holy World to heal.
He likely sealed the aura of that terrifying existence and utilized it. I must say, Jinchen Holy Ancestor was also something of a genius!"
Fire-Pattern War Ancestor said.
"What exactly is it?"
Ye Tian was extremely curious.
"The Nirvana Race!"
Fire-Pattern War Ancestor said, his eyes seemingly revealing a trace of fear.
To be able to make Fire-Pattern War Ancestor feel fear showed just how terrifying this so-called Nirvana Race was!

Chapter 1440: I Am Simply a Genius!

Chapter 1440: I Am Simply a Genius!
!
After a long silence, the Fire-Pattern War Ancestor finally spoke: "The Nirvana Clan is an existence that brings extinction to all things. They do not seem to exist under the Great Dao; they transcend time, space, and rules. From the moment they are born, they are comparable to Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, and the elites among them are even comparable to Primordial Ancestors!"
"What!"
Ye Tian's eyes widened, his face filled with disbelief.
Comparable to Supreme-level Domain Ancestors at birth, with elites rivaling Primordial Ancestors.
Was the Nirvana Clan truly that terrifying? If so, what was the point of cultivation? How could anyone possibly compare to the Nirvana Clan? No wonder even the Fire-Pattern War Ancestor was so fearful; this Nirvana Clan was simply too monstrous! "If the Nirvana Clan is so terrifying, why haven't I heard of them? Logically, they should have invaded the Dark Holy Region long ago!"
Ye Tian asked in confusion.
"Because of the resistance of the Primordial Ancestors!"
The Fire-Pattern War Ancestor said, "Where do you think the Primordial Ancestors are? Do you really think they are in the Dark Holy Region? No, those remaining in the Dark Holy Region are merely the incarnations of the Primordial Ancestors.
Even during the last struggle for the Primordial Ancestral World, it was only the incarnations of the Primordial Ancestors who acted.
The true bodies of the Primordial Ancestors are far more powerful than their incarnations, and they are busy holding back the Nirvana Clan.
Furthermore, some of the Supreme-level Domain Ancestors from the Ten Great Holy Sects are also helping to resist the Nirvana Clan. Even certain Holy Lands must dispatch Supreme-level Domain Ancestors to guard the front; whichever Holy Land is called upon must send someone.
For instance, the Golden Star Holy Ancestor of the Qingyuan Holy Land was chosen. He returned heavily injured and has been healing ever since."
"In fact, there are more Supreme-level Domain Ancestors in the Dark Holy Region than you know. Even the number of Primordial Ancestors isn't just ten, but twenty-three. Moreover, the Primordial Ancestors of the Dark Destruction Region must also go to guard the front, and they have even more Primordial Ancestors than we do.
Our Dark Holy Region and the Dark Destruction Region can kill each other all we want; as long as it doesn't involve the Primordial Ancestor level, it doesn't really matter, even if some Supreme-level Domain Ancestors fall.
But when it comes to resisting the Nirvana Clan, there is no room for negotiation—we must resist.
Otherwise, if we fail to hold them back, both the Dark Holy Region and the Dark Destruction Region will be finished.
Additionally, the Dark Forbidden Region is vast. There are also some rogue Primordial Ancestors and rogue Supreme-level Domain Ancestors. Once their tracks are discovered, they must go to guard the front, or they will inevitably be hunted down by all the Primordial Ancestors.
Back then, some Holy Sects suspected there was a Primordial Ancestor behind you, which is why they tested you time and again. When they found no evidence, they eventually dropped the matter!"
"So that's how it is!"
Ye Tian understood completely.
"Where is the Nirvana Clan?"
Ye Tian asked this final question.
"At the edge of the Dark Forbidden Region, in the Endless Space-Time Corridor. The Dark Forbidden Region seems boundless, but in reality, when the Primordial Ancestors travel through space-time, they can reach any part of it. The capabilities of the Primordial Ancestors far exceed those of Supreme-level Domain Ancestors. Even if a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor flies for billions upon billions of eons, they would never reach the end of the Dark Forbidden Region, but the Primordial Ancestors can reach the end by walking through space-time.
Long ago, while traveling through the depths of space-time, the Primordial Ancestors discovered a dark area in the Endless Space-Time Corridor. That area had permeated into the depths of space-time, which puzzled the Primordial Ancestors greatly. After investigating, they finally discovered the existence of the Nirvana Clan.
A great war broke out; one Primordial Ancestor fell, and six were heavily injured.
Afterward, the Primordial Ancestors gathered together, and only then did they manage to hold back the Nirvana Clan."
"The Nirvana Clan seems to possess no wisdom and cannot be communicated with. Through calculations, it was learned that if the Nirvana Clan isn't stopped, they will extinguish everything, returning all things to one and bringing space-time back to its starting point. The Nirvana Clan can affect and permeate space-time—that is the most terrifying part!"
The Fire-Pattern War Ancestor said with a hint of dread.
Then, he calmed down again, saying: "Myriad Law Domain Ancestor, you don't need to worry. The Primordial Ancestors have held back the Nirvana Clan, so for now, there are no issues.
If the Dark Holy Region gives birth to more Primordial Ancestors, there might even be hope of wiping out the Nirvana Clan in the future!"
"Fire-Pattern War Ancestor, I'm not worried!"
Ye Tian had a very good mindset.
He believed he would definitely become a Primordial Ancestor and might even be able to wipe out the Nirvana Clan single-handedly in the future.
"That's good then!"
The Fire-Pattern War Ancestor was relieved.
He was afraid that after learning about the Nirvana Clan, Ye Tian would lose his motivation to progress and give up on himself; that would be bad.
Suddenly.
Ye Tian asked again: "Fire-Pattern War Ancestor, what is the deal with the Mirror of Time? Why is a person only allowed to enter once in their lifetime? Is it really impossible to enter a second time?"
"The Mirror of Time?"
The Fire-Pattern War Ancestor smiled and said: "That thing was actually forged from a core fragment of a Nirvana Clan Primordial Ancestor's corpse. The Nirvana Clan can erode space-time, so the Mirror of Time can both influence and erode space-time. If you enter a second time, you have already left an imprint within the Mirror of Time.
After all, during the first entry, almost everyone stays until they are at their limit before leaving. The second time, the impact is even greater; you will be directly unable to resist the erosion of space-time and will be assimilated by time, or rather, assimilated by the power of the Nirvana Clan.
The Mirror of Time cannot assimilate a Primordial Ancestor, but it is also useless to them, or simply doesn't work on them.
And those below the Primordial Ancestor level have no way to resist the erosion of time, which is why it can only be entered once!"
"So that's the reason."
Ye Tian understood.
In other words, the first time he entered the Mirror of Time, it remembered him. Entering a second time would subject him to the erosion of time, which those below the Primordial Ancestor level could almost never resist; they would one hundred percent be eroded and wouldn't even be able to withdraw in time.
But now that Ye Tian understood the principle behind the Mirror of Time, it actually wasn't that mysterious.
If he used his Copy Talent to copy someone else's body and then entered the Mirror of Time, he would be equivalent to a different person.
He would only need to pay the cost to open the Mirror of Time; it wouldn't matter how many times he used it.
However, once he stepped into the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor realm, the Mirror of Time would likely be of little use to him, as ordinary cultivation insights can hardly be improved rapidly there.
Aside from providing a long duration of time, the Mirror of Time had no other special benefits.
"Then I'll use the Mirror of Time to practice Ancestral Techniques. I'll strive to use that endless stretch of time to practice each Ancestral Technique to the Great Success or even the Perfection stage."
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Of course, when copying someone else's body, that person must also possess Ancestral Talents. Otherwise, a body without Ancestral Talents would gain nothing from entering the Mirror of Time; even after practicing for endless years, they wouldn't be able to improve their Ancestral Techniques!
For others, this was an unsolvable problem, but for Ye Tian, it was simple.
He could capture some sinful Domain Ancestors, bestow upon them various Ancestral Talents, then kill them and copy their bodies. The bodies copied this way would then possess Ancestral Talents.
"I am simply a genius!"
Ye Tian couldn't help but praise his own plan.
Subsequently, he began to put this plan into motion.
Once the plan succeeded, he could practice his Ancestral Techniques to the Perfection stage in a short amount of time, and his strength would skyrocket many times over.

Chapter 1441: Entering the Realm of Time Hundreds of Thousands of Times!

Chapter 1441: Entering the Realm of Time Hundreds of Thousands of Times!
!
In the Dark Holy Region, there were many such sinful Domain Ancestors.
Ye Tian went to the Dark Holy Region and spent some time capturing a large number of evil Domain Ancestors. He sealed them within his internal world, bestowed Ancestral Talents upon them, copied their bodies, left a mark within the Copy Talent, and then reclaimed the Ancestral Talents.
This was also one of the abilities of the Copy Talent.
However, when Ye Tian bestowed his talents upon his own relatives, he naturally would not take them back.
Therefore, this was the first time he had ever performed such an act of reclaiming a talent.
In this manner, Ye Tian bestowed almost all of his talents and then took them back.
By doing this, he could copy many people's bodies, with each body possessing one or two Ancestral Talents.
On this day.
Ye Tian arrived at the War Ancestor Realm, at the entrance of the Time Hall.
Having slain a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor, Ye Tian's status within the War Gate had soared, making him equivalent to a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor.
Therefore, he ordered the two Domain Ancestors stationed at the Time Hall to leave; for the coming period, he would personally guard the Time Hall.
They did not dare to disobey Ye Tian's orders and complied accordingly.
Entrance to the Time Hall:
Ye Tian sealed off the area and then created a copied Domain Ancestor body.
This copied body possessed the Space Ancestral Talent. Thus, after entering the Realm of Time, this body specialized in practicing the Void Slash and Void Escape Ancestral Techniques, continuing until it was nearly assimilated by time before exiting.
"Go in!"
Ye Tian's copied body stepped into the Realm of Time. Ye Tian took responsibility for the energy consumption required to operate the Realm of Time, pouring a vast amount of various energy treasures into it to sustain its operation.
Boom! As soon as the copied body entered the Realm of Time, it began its cultivation, constantly comprehending and training the Void Slash and Void Escape Ancestral Techniques.
An unknown number of billions of years passed. When this copied body was nearly half-eroded by time, it withdrew.
Otherwise, if the copied body did not come out, the Realm of Time would remain isolated from the outside world, and the insights could not be brought out.
As soon as the copied body emerged, countless insights flooded in.
Boom! Ye Tian gained a much deeper understanding of the Void Slash and Void Escape Ancestral Techniques. In reality, for the main body, only a single moment had passed, yet he could significantly increase the realm of these techniques. This was incredibly cost-effective.
However, even after billions of years of hard cultivation in the Realm of Time, raising an Ancestral Technique to the Great Success stage was no easy feat, let alone reaching the Perfection stage.
Furthermore, his body within the Realm of Time lacked the Evolution trait, so he had no way to use it to deduce techniques. The speed of cultivation was naturally extremely slow, relying entirely on the accumulation of endless years.
"It's fine, I'll just condense another copied body!"
Ye Tian manipulated time, constantly accelerating it. While only a short while passed outside, Ye Tian lived through ten thousand years, and the Copy Talent could be used again.
Subsequently, Ye Tian copied another body and entered the Realm of Time.
In this way, one body after another entered the Realm of Time to comprehend the Void Slash and Void Escape Ancestral Techniques.
Ten copied bodies! A hundred copied bodies! It took several hundred copied bodies to finally train the Void Slash and Void Escape Ancestral Techniques to the Perfection stage.
Afterward, Ye Tian began practicing other Ancestral Techniques.
Once he ran out of copied bodies, he would go capture more Domain Ancestors, bestow talents, copy their bodies, and then kill them.
Using this method, Ye Tian's Ancestral Techniques reached the Perfection stage one by one.
"Hundreds of thousands of Domain Ancestors now!"
During this period, Ye Tian had captured hundreds of thousands of Domain Ancestors, and their fate was naturally death.
The Dark Holy Region did not lack Domain Ancestors. Hundreds of thousands of them didn't even cause a ripple there. Moreover, he only killed those who deserved to die, so he did not attract the attention of others.
He copied bodies hundreds of thousands of times and entered the Realm of Time hundreds of thousands of times.
Although not much time had passed in the outside world, Ye Tian had indeed spent an unimaginably long time within the Realm of Time. Even with his mental state, he had nearly collapsed.
Had it been back when he was a Peak Domain Ancestor, he wouldn't have dared to do this; his soul definitely wouldn't have been able to withstand such a long period of continuous comprehension.
But now his Holy Soul was incredibly powerful, and his mental state was naturally high, which was why he dared to do it.
Even so, Ye Tian felt incredibly mentally exhausted.
Fortunately, his efforts were not in vain. Almost all of his Ancestral Techniques had been trained to the Perfection stage.
Now, his strength had increased to a terrifying degree.
If he were to face a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor like the Golden Star Holy Ancestor, he could kill them in just a few moves.
"I can't continue practicing for now. I need to travel the Dark Holy Region for ten million years, enjoy myself everywhere, and relax my mind!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Thus, in the following years, Ye Tian spent his time eating, drinking, and having fun, completely forgetting about cultivation and everything else.
Sometimes, he even sealed his own memories and strength, living as an ordinary person.
Just like that, tens of millions of years passed.
In a small city within the Dark Holy Region.
Ye Tian stood in a small courtyard, his heart filled with peace.
At this moment, he unsealed his memories. His heart was no longer restless, nor did he feel any resistance toward cultivation.
"I've finally recovered. I can't do that next time. Besides, the Realm of Time is no longer useful to me!"
Ye Tian murmured.
He took a step forward, left the place, and soon returned to the War Ancestor Realm.
Then, he left an avatar in the War Ancestor Realm. As for his copied bodies, he would not leave them here. He still needed to use them for repeated evolution and deduction of body control in his future cultivation, so it wasn't convenient to leave them here.
His avatar's combat power was comparable to a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor. While it might not match the Fire Pattern War Ancestor's avatar, it certainly wouldn't be much weaker.
After Ye Tian returned to the Profound Void Holy Realm, he continued to master his body.
He had only mastered his body by a few dozen times; he was still far from 365-fold body control. Only by completely mastering his body 365 times could he break the limit of the Invincible Domain Body and complete one Invincible Domain transformation. After nine transformations, it would evolve to the level of a Supreme-level Domain Body.
In the blink of an eye, billions of years passed.
After such a long period of hard cultivation and countless evolutions of his copied bodies, he finally raised his body control to an extremely high level.

Chapter 1442: Complete Control of the Physical Body, One Invincible...

Chapter 1442: Complete Control of the Physical Body, One Invincible Domain Body Transformation!

"Just one step more and I can completely control my physical body at 365 times, reaching the true pinnacle of physical control!"
Ye Tian murmured.
He continued to condense duplicate bodies, letting them activate the Evolution trait to deduce physical control.
Soon, Ye Tian performed hundreds more evolutions and finally completed this last step.
Boom! The physical body finally reached the level of perfect control.
At this moment, Ye Tian was capable of exerting 365 times the power of his physical body.
A sense of consummate control permeated the air. At this moment, Ye Tian could break the limit of the Invincible Domain Body at any time and undergo the first Invincible Domain Body transformation.
"Then let the transformation begin!"
With a single thought, Ye Tian controlled the infinite cells of his body, each cell comparable to a world.
Infinite worlds evolved under Ye Tian's will at any moment.
Boom! The Invincible Domain Body transformed, evolving toward the Supreme-level Domain Body.
Crack! Ye Tian's physical body instantly shattered into countless particles, each particle equivalent to a world.
These particles transformed, becoming even stronger, and then combined once again to form Ye Tian's body.
This moment seemed to last a long time, but in reality, only an instant had passed.
By now, Ye Tian had completed the first transformation of the Invincible Domain Body. After nine transformations, it would evolve into a Supreme-level Domain Body.
This process was guaranteed to be completed; it just required a long time.
After completing the first transformation of the Invincible Domain Body, Ye Tian frantically absorbed various energies to supplement the needs of the transformation.
Ye Tian took out various holy medicines, forbidden crystals, and source spring water... Under the supply of massive resources, Ye Tian's Invincible Domain Body finally absorbed enough energy and completely stabilized.
At this moment, Ye Tian's physical strength had surged several times over again.
This was only after completing a single transformation, yet his strength had increased so much. If he completed all nine, to what terrifying level would his strength rise?
The transformation of the Invincible Domain Body could be achieved by following the cultivation steps. The reason it took so long was that he needed to regain control over his physical body.
Because his physical body had surged several times in power and undergone a transformation, he could no longer control it at 365 times. It would drop to around 20 times, thus requiring him to regain control, which took time.
Once he regained control to the level of 365 times, he could complete the second transformation.
This would continue until the ninth transformation.
Of course, since he had previously achieved the perfect control of 365 times, regaining it would be much faster than before.
Therefore, for an Invincible Domain Ancestor who had broken through to the transformation stage, they only needed to take their time to eventually step into the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor realm.
"I have the Evolution trait, so I can speed up each transformation of the Invincible Domain Body!"
Ye Tian thought.
He had nothing else to do for now, so he continued his secluded cultivation to regain control of his body.
....While Ye Tian was in seclusion, the Xuanxu Holy World continued to grow. A large number of holy items were born. Since the human race had complete control over the Xuanxu Holy World and did not allow outsiders to enter, Domain Ancestors outside the human race had no idea about the situation inside.
The Xuanxu Holy World produced a large number of holy items, even holy medicines, holy mineral veins, and Ancestral Script holy items.
Under these circumstances, the human Domain Ancestors were very puzzled.
Nowadays, the human Domain Ancestors also had contact with the outside world, so they knew the situation of ordinary Holy Worlds. The speed and quantity of resource production in the Xuanxu Holy World far exceeded other Holy Worlds, which was too abnormal.
However, they did not ask questions but buried this doubt in their hearts. Regardless, this was a good thing for the human race.
Furthermore, the human race had a large amount of Star Soul Sand, and more and more peak human Domain Ancestors were breaking through to the Invincible Domain Ancestor realm.
After long years of cultivation, the number of Invincible Domain Ancestors in the human race had reached several thousand, and it was still increasing.
Additionally, the growth speed of those few Holy Talent users in the human race was also very fast. They had long since stepped into the Peak Domain Ancestor realm and had become first-tier Peak Domain Ancestors, soon to reach the combat power level of those on the Peak Rankings.
These Holy Talent users were the ones Ye Tian valued more. In the future, they had the hope of stepping into the combat power of two-step or even one-step Invincible Domain Ancestors, qualifying them to become the foundation of the human race. A large number of ordinary Invincible Domain Ancestors were of little use.
For example, the Qingyuan Holy Land had many Invincible Domain Ancestors, but he could kill them all with a single thought.
Therefore, only having many powerful experts could truly increase the human race's strength and deter others. Ordinary Invincible Domain Ancestors could not achieve such deterrence.
He would often be in seclusion in the future, so the human race still needed to rely on those powerful Invincible Domain Ancestors.
In the blink of an eye, another few hundred million years passed.
One day.
A violent tremor occurred in the Xuanxu Holy World. To prevent any accidents, someone sent a message to Ye Tian.
Ye Tian came directly out of the Holy Stele World.
"Husband!"
Xiao Yue appeared by Ye Tian's side.
"Father!"
Ye Xingchen and Ye Xingyue also arrived.
"Father, what exactly happened?"
Ye Xingchen asked in confusion.
"I'm not sure yet!"
Ye Tian frowned.
Although he was the master of the Xuanxu Holy World, he had just come out and hadn't had time to check the situation.
Hum! Ye Tian's consciousness covered the entire Xuanxu Holy World, sensing its changes.
Soon, he discovered the cause of the tremor.
"That is..."
Ye Tian saw a source spring being born somewhere, and a world was forming in that place.
"Forbidden Ancestral Spring!"
Seeing this ancestral spring, Ye Tian was greatly shaken.
A Forbidden Ancestral Spring was no ordinary thing; it was something that even an Ancestral World might not necessarily produce.
For example, the War Ancestral World did not have a Forbidden Ancestral Spring, but the Forbidden Ancestral World of the Forbidden Holy Sect possessed one.
Among the Ancestral Worlds of the Ten Great Holy Sects, only five possessed a Forbidden Ancestral Spring.
A Forbidden Ancestral Spring was of little use to an individual, but for a power, its value was extremely high.
The forbidden spring water produced by the Forbidden Ancestral Spring could help a Domain Ancestor easily rise to the Peak Domain Ancestor realm, and it also helped in tempering the domain body and purifying internal energy.
But the greatest use of the Forbidden Ancestral Spring was not this, but rather ensuring immortality! In the core of the Forbidden Ancestral Spring, a special kind of forbidden energy could be born. This special energy could keep a person from dying, allowing them to cultivate various dangerous holy bodies and secret techniques to their heart's content inside.
Of course, for a holy body like the Eternal Indestructible Holy Body, once you cultivated it, it would be difficult to recover even with this, but for ordinary holy bodies, even if one died, they could recover again without any side effects.
Therefore, with the Forbidden Ancestral Spring, a large number of top-tier holy body disciples could be produced.
The only pity was that the special energy of the Forbidden Ancestral Spring was limited, accommodating at most a few people at a time. However, accumulated over long years, a power would produce a large number of terrifyingly talented disciples.
Thus, the Forbidden Ancestral Spring was too precious!

Chapter 1443: The Immortal Sacred Sect Strikes!

Chapter 1443: The Immortal Sacred Sect Strikes!
!
"The Taboo Ancestral Spring is far too precious. Back then, the Battle Sect lagged behind significantly in the Holy Wars precisely because they lacked a Taboo Ancestral Spring. If I hadn't appeared out of nowhere, the Battle Sect's performance in the Holy Wars would likely have been pathetic!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
In fact, it wasn't just once; in many Holy Wars, the Battle Sect's track record was poor. Because they lacked a Taboo Ancestral Spring, the Battle Sect was relatively mediocre when it came to cultivating Holy Sons.
However, at the level of Invincible Domain Ancestors, the Battle Sect was quite formidable, possessing many treasure lands capable of cultivating Invincible Domain Ancestors.
Of course, those treasure lands were of no use to the current Ye Tian, so he didn't bother going to them.
After all, his strength was already greater than that of an ordinary Supreme-level Domain Ancestor, so those treasure lands naturally had no effect on him.
"A Taboo Ancestral Spring has been born in the Profound Void Sacred World. Once this news leaks, even other Sacred Sects might be tempted to come and seize it!"
Ye Tian mused.
Indeed, a Taboo Ancestral Spring could be stolen; in essence, it was a mobile treasure land.
A Supreme-level Domain Ancestor could cut out a section of the void and carry the Taboo Ancestral Spring away.
"I'll try to keep the news hidden as much as possible. If it really is discovered, I'd like to see which Sacred Sect's Supreme-level Domain Ancestor dares to make a move," Ye Tian said coldly.
With the birth of the Taboo Ancestral Spring, Ye Tian began to vigorously cultivate the geniuses of the human race.
Because of the spring's existence, many top-tier Holy Body inheritances were established.
Furthermore, many human Domain Ancestors easily reached the Supreme Domain Ancestor realm with the help of the Taboo Ancestral Spring.
In a mere hundred million years, the number of human Supreme Domain Ancestors increased a hundredfold. What a terrifying improvement! Meanwhile, Ye Tian also made great progress, once again gaining control over 365 times his physical body, completing his second Invincible Domain Body transformation, and causing his strength to skyrocket once more.
...Human practitioners could not stay in the Profound Void Sacred World forever; they often practiced in the outside world, and some even traveled to the Dark Sacred Domain.
Some human practitioners perished outside and were captured by other experts, who interrogated them and accidentally extracted information about the Taboo Ancestral Spring.
Even though Ye Tian repeatedly emphasized the importance of the Taboo Ancestral Spring to the human race and forbade its disclosure, not everyone could keep the secret.
In the past, when they said the Profound Void Sacred World had many resources, it didn't attract much attention.
But a Taboo Ancestral Spring was different; once leaked, it would inevitably cause a massive uproar.
On this day.
The fact that the Profound Void Sacred World possessed a Taboo Ancestral Spring was exposed. As for who leaked it, Ye Tian could not find out.
The Ten Great Sacred Sects soon learned of this and immediately sent people to verify it.
The Battle Sect was the first to receive the news because they could directly question Ye Tian.
At the Battle World Tower.
Fire-Pattern Battle Ancestor questioned Ye Tian.
"Universal Law Domain Ancestor, is it true that a Taboo Ancestral Spring has been born in your Profound Void Sacred World?"
Fire-Pattern Battle Ancestor asked.
"It is true!"
Ye Tian admitted.
The news had already leaked, so there was no point in denying it. Moreover, since it was the Fire-Pattern Battle Ancestor of the Battle Sect asking, he naturally couldn't refuse to answer.
"Universal Law Domain Ancestor, you should be very clear about the value of a Taboo Ancestral Spring. It doesn't help an individual much, but it is incredibly precious for an organization.
Other Sacred Sects that lack a Taboo Ancestral Spring will likely try to seize the one in the Profound Void Sacred World.
I suggest you move the Taboo Ancestral Spring to the Battle Ancestor World. That way, other Sacred Sects won't come to snatch it."
Fire-Pattern Battle Ancestor suggested.
Ye Tian refused directly: "Fire-Pattern Battle Ancestor, this Taboo Ancestral Spring belongs to humanity. I cannot place it in the Battle Ancestor World.
As for any Supreme-level Domain Ancestors from other Sacred Sects who come to attack, I will block them myself!"
Fire-Pattern Battle Ancestor knew he couldn't persuade Ye Tian, so he stopped trying.
"Universal Law Domain Ancestor, be careful. If you find yourself unable to win, the Supreme-level Domain Ancestors of the Battle Sect will come to support you!"
Fire-Pattern Battle Ancestor said.
After all, Ye Tian also belonged to the Battle Sect. If Ye Tian ran into trouble, the Battle Sect naturally couldn't ignore it...
.
However, the Supreme-level Domain Ancestors of the Battle Sect were also very busy, needing to guard the Battle Ancestor World and focus on their own cultivation. It was impossible for them to be stationed in the Profound Void Sacred World at all times.
This was also why Fire-Pattern Battle Ancestor had suggested that Ye Tian move the Taboo Ancestral Spring to the Battle Ancestor World.
"Fire-Pattern Battle Ancestor, I will be careful!"
Ye Tian said.
...Immortal Sacred Sect, Immortal Ancestral World.
The Immortal Ancestral World happened to be... one of the Ancestral Worlds that had not birthed a Taboo Ancestral Spring. Now, news of the Taboo Ancestral Spring in the Profound Void Sacred World had arrived.
Subsequently, the Immortal Ancestral World sent people to investigate, and the news was quickly confirmed.
"The news is true!"
Upon learning this, the Supreme-level Domain Ancestors of the Immortal Sacred Sect were stirred.
In the core area of the Immortal Ancestral World, within an ancient Immortal Ancestral Hall.
One towering figure after another appeared—they were the Supreme-level Domain Ancestors of the Immortal Sacred Sect.
Soon, thirteen Supreme-level Domain Ancestors had gathered.
In reality, the Immortal Sacred Sect had more Supreme-level Domain Ancestors than this, but some were busy fending off the Nirvana Race. The ones present here were those with their true bodies available; otherwise, coming here would be useless.
"Everyone, a Taboo Ancestral Spring has been born in the Profound Void Sacred World. Although the master of that world belongs to the Battle Sect, our Ten Great Sacred Sects frequently clash, and seizing their treasures is nothing out of the ordinary.
I suggest we move immediately to seize the Taboo Ancestral Spring, lest the Universal Law Domain Ancestor moves it to the Battle Ancestor World. If that happens, we won't be able to take it! The Battle Ancestor World is guarded by an avatar of the Progenitor; no matter how many of us go, we'd just be seeking death!"
The Supreme-level Domain Ancestor—Black-Pattern Saint Ancestor—spoke up.
"We must go, but who should we send? If we all move out, it will definitely alert the Battle Sect. They will likely try to stop us or even take the opportunity to cause trouble for our Immortal Sacred Sect.
Therefore, I suggest sending one person to seize the Taboo Ancestral Spring with the greatest possible speed!"
Another Supreme-level Domain Ancestor said.
They discussed for a long time and finally decided to send Black-Pattern Saint Ancestor.
Although Black-Pattern Saint Ancestor was only at the middle stage of the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor realm, he had comprehended Ancestral Techniques. Thus, his combat power was far beyond that of a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor like Golden Star Saint Ancestor.
If he went to seize the Taboo Ancestral Spring, a mere Universal Law Domain Ancestor would be no match for him and would have no way to stop him.
"Black-Pattern Saint Ancestor, rush there as fast as you can. Don't waste time, or else if another Sacred Sect beats us to it, we'll suffer a great loss!"
The various Supreme-level Domain Ancestors urged.
"Fine, I'll be back shortly!"
Black-Pattern Saint Ancestor said with a smile.
Immediately, he activated a secret treasure, instantly piercing through time and space to cross the Dark Sacred Domain.
Battle Sect.
One by one, the Supreme-level Domain Ancestors looked toward the location of the Immortal Sacred Sect.
"Black-Pattern Saint Ancestor has left!"
Fire-Pattern Battle Ancestor noted.
Just as he was preparing to go support the Profound Void Sacred World, several Supreme-level Domain Ancestors from the Immortal Sacred Sect crossed through time and space and arrived at the Battle Ancestor Domain.
Should any Supreme-level Domain Ancestor from the Battle Ancestor World attempt to leave, they would engage them in "conversation."
As long as they could delay them for just a short while, Black-Pattern Saint Ancestor would be able to complete his mission.

Chapter 1444: Sealing the Dark Holy Ancestor, the Primordial Ancestor Steps In
!
Xuanxu Holy Realm.
Ye Tian had been guarding the Taboo Spring during this time; regardless... it was also a suitable place for cultivation.
Suddenly.
Ye Tian sensed the fluctuations of a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor.

Ye Tian immediately sealed off the Xuanxu Holy Realm, and his duplicated body promptly walked out of the Taboo Ancestral Spring, while his original body remained to guard the place. This ensured that the Xuanxu Holy Realm would not be stolen away.
Boom!!!! Outside the Xuanxu Holy Realm, Ye Tian stopped a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor who was traveling through space with a single hand.
Boom!!! Ye Tian threw a punch, directly knocking the opponent out of space-time.

The Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor threatened.

Ye Tian said coldly.

The Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor was furious.
Boom!!!!! A black light emerged from the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor's body, transforming into a strange stone statue.
This was his special Ancestral Technique—Stone Statue True Body! By performing this Ancestral Technique, as long as the technique was not broken, all damage dealt by the enemy would be transferred to the stone statue, while his original body remained unharmed.
Furthermore, the Stone Statue True Body could amplify his physical strength and physical defense by tenfold. Thus, this Ancestral Technique was extremely terrifying and was his primary reliance.
"Void Slash!"
Without a word, Ye Tian directly unleashed the space Ancestral Technique, Void Slash, at the Consummate Realm.
Rip! Hundreds of millions of territories of space-time shattered. The terrifying Void Slash seemed capable of annihilating all Great Dao space-time as it struck the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor directly.
Crack! The stone statue behind the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor cracked instantly, a massive fissure appearing that was difficult to heal.
"The Void Slash Ancestral Technique, and it's at the Consummate Realm? How is that possible? How could you possibly raise an Ancestral Technique to the Consummate Realm?"
The Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor was dumbfounded.
Back then, the images of Ye Tian's battle with the Golden Dawn Holy Ancestor had spread, and he had seen them.
Ye Tian indeed knew many Ancestral Techniques, but they were all at the Minor Success stage.
Raising an Ancestral Technique to Minor Success was manageable, but raising it to Great Success or the Consummate Realm was an exaggerated level of difficulty.
He had rarely seen any Domain Ancestors who could cultivate an Ancestral Technique to the Consummate Realm.
Moreover, Ye Tian's current cultivation was different.
Back then, Ye Tian had not fully mastered his body, but now he had not only gained complete control but had also completed two Invincible Domain Body transformations.
"This... how can there be such a rapid rate of improvement? Even if one practiced bitterly within a Time Array, given the best resources, and even with a Primordial Ancestor-level being personally guiding them, it would be impossible to have such a fast rate of cultivation progress!"
The Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor was completely stunned, unable to believe it at all.
Abruptly! Streaks of golden light transformed into silk threads, continuously cutting his body.
Each golden thread felt like the full-force strike of a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor. Under the attack of so many golden threads, he had no way to resist.
At the same time, Ye Tian's Void Slash Ancestral Technique struck from time to time, causing his stone statue to crack continuously.
Crack! The Stone Statue True Body was about to shatter. Once this Ancestral Technique broke, his physical body would be unable to withstand Ye Tian, and his Supreme-level Domain Body would soon be ground away by Ye Tian.
At this moment, the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor gritted his teeth and took out a small gray orb.
He crushed the gray orb, and a gray light shield immediately protected him. No matter how powerful Ye Tian's Void Slash was, it could not shake this gray light shield.
"Can't break it?"
Ye Tian frowned.
Immediately, he directly performed the Five Elements Seal Ancestral Technique.
"Seal!"
The Five Elements Seal directly extracted the power of the Five Elements Taboo Great Dao in this area, forcibly suppressing the gray light shield. Layers of seals compressed this area into a small ball, which appeared in Ye Tian's hand.
The Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor was sealed within this Five Elements Seal ball. Although Ye Tian could not break the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor's gray light shield, the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor could not get out either.
In the future, he could attack that gray light shield over and over again. After a long period of attacks, he didn't believe the gray light shield wouldn't break.
Void Slash! Void Slash! Void Slash! Ye Tian attacked repeatedly; regardless... he wasn't afraid of wasting time.
Inside the gray light shield.
The Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor also knew he had been sealed by Ye Tian, and sensing Ye Tian's continuous attacks on the gray light shield, he grew anxious.
This gray light shield was transformed from that small gray orb, which was a special sacred object he had occasionally obtained while traveling the Dark Forbidden Zone. It could withstand the full-force strike of a top-tier Supreme-level Domain Ancestor, and could even block the full-force strike of a Half-step Primordial Ancestor.
Even for himself, if he were to attack this gray light shield, it would take at least hundreds of thousands of years of attacks to have any hope of breaking it.
But at this moment, he felt that Ye Tian's attacks were too terrifying. This gray light shield would last ten years at most.
"Call for help, I must call for help!"
The Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor panicked.
In a certain territory of the Immortal Holy Sect, the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor had a weaker avatar stationed there.
This avatar immediately headed to the Immortal Ancestral Realm.
"Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor, what is the situation?"
Several Supreme-level Domain Ancestors of the Immortal Holy Sect asked.
"My true body has been sealed by the Myriad Law Domain Ancestor. His strength is many times greater than before, and he even possesses Ancestral Techniques at the Consummate Realm.
I must ask the Primordial Ancestor to save me, otherwise I will surely die!"
The Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor said urgently.
"What? You've been sealed?"
The Supreme-level Domain Ancestors were shocked.
"Immortal Primordial Ancestor, please save me!"
The Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor knelt at the entrance of the Immortal Primordial Ancestor's palace and pleaded.
"I understand!"
The Immortal Primordial Ancestor's voice came through. "I am a Primordial Ancestor, after all; it is inconvenient for me to take action against an Invincible Domain Ancestor.
How about this, I will go find the Battle Ancestor of the Battle Sect and have him persuade the Myriad Law Domain Ancestor to release you!"
"Thank you, Immortal Primordial Ancestor!"
The Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor hurriedly expressed his gratitude.
Boom!!!!! This avatar of the Immortal Primordial Ancestor condensed a sliver of will, crossed the long river of space-time, and arrived at the Battle Ancestor Realm.<
Immediately, the Battle Ancestor sensed it and met with this sliver of the Immortal Primordial Ancestor's will.
"Immortal Primordial Ancestor, what is it? Why have you suddenly come to find me?"
The Battle Ancestor asked curiously.
"Battle Ancestor, have your Battle Sect's Myriad Law Domain Ancestor release the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor. You name the conditions!"
The Immortal Primordial Ancestor said.

Chapter 1445: Compensation, Causality-type Ancestral Weapon!

Chapter 1445: Compensation, Causality-type Ancestral Weapon!
!
"Myriad Law Domain Ancestor, release your Immortal Holy Sect's Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor? What is the meaning of this?"
War Ancestor was also somewhat bewildered.
His avatar presided over the War Ancestor Realm, and he usually didn't pay much attention to outside affairs, so he didn't know what had happened.
The Immortal Primordial Ancestor explained the matter between the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor and Ye Tian.
After listening, War Ancestor couldn't help but sneer, "Immortal Primordial Ancestor, a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor from your Immortal Holy Sect tried to snatch a Forbidden Ancestral Spring from a Domain Ancestor of my War Sect and got captured. He deserved it! And yet you have the nerve to ask me to release him?"
The Immortal Primordial Ancestor hurriedly said, "War Ancestor, there's no use saying more. Let's talk terms. Besides, if the Dark Holy Domain loses a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor, its strength will also weaken by a fraction. There's no need to be so absolute!"

The Immortal Primordial Ancestor nodded.
....Profound Void Holy Realm.
A peculiar fluctuation appeared in the War World Tower.
A strand of will crossed the endless space-time directly from the War World Tower of the Dark Holy Domain and descended upon the War World Tower of the Profound Void Holy Realm.
This strand of will descended directly upon Ye Tian's residence.
"Who is it?"
Ye Tian asked solemnly.
"It is I, War Ancestor!"
The figure of War Ancestor emerged.
Although it was merely a thought, Ye Tian felt an incomparable power, as if a single thought from War Ancestor could suppress and kill him.
This was the strength of a Primordial Ancestor! "Greetings, War Ancestor!"
Ye Tian said respectfully.
"Myriad Law Domain Ancestor, did you capture the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor of the Immortal Holy Sect?"
War Ancestor asked.
"I did!"
Ye Tian admitted.
War Ancestor said, "The Immortal Primordial Ancestor of the Immortal Holy Sect came to find me. He wants to ransom the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor. If you are willing, state your conditions. If you are not, it doesn't matter even if you kill him. The War Sect does not fear the Immortal Holy Sect!"
Ye Tian pondered for a moment.
If he killed the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor, he would completely become an enemy of the Immortal Holy Sect and offend the Immortal Primordial Ancestor.
Moreover, killing the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor wouldn't be of much help to him.
If he released him, he could obtain some benefits.
"War Ancestor, I choose to release the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor!"
Ye Tian said.
"State your conditions, and I will relay them to the Immortal Primordial Ancestor."
War Ancestor said indifferently.
Ye Tian thought about what kind of treasure to demand. Ordinary treasures were useless to him, and given the value of a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor, he naturally wouldn't ask for something common.
After thinking it over, Ye Tian chose a treasure that would be helpful to him.
"I want a Causality-type Ancestral Weapon!" Ye Tian requested.
Ancestral Weapons were the weapons of Supreme-level Domain Ancestors. Ordinary sacred items and weapons were of almost no help to them, while Ancestral Weapons could enhance their combat power.
Of course, not all Supreme-level Domain Ancestors possessed Ancestral Weapons.
Rumor had it that Ancestral Weapons were forged from special materials, and only the Primordial Ancestors knew the specific forging process.
Thus, Ancestral Weapons were forged by Primordial Ancestors, and a very small number of Half-step Primordial Ancestors.
"A Causality-type Ancestral Weapon? That is quite a rare thing!"
War Ancestor smiled.
Ye Tian chose a Causality-type Ancestral Weapon because he wanted to protect himself.
Although he had cloned bodies, what if an enemy used a cloned body to kill his main body across space? The cloned bodies could not sever their causal connection with the main body. Therefore, if he possessed a Causality-type Ancestral Weapon, he could sever the causal link between his main body and his clones, completely mending his final flaw.
At that time, his cloned bodies could roam freely, and even a Primordial Ancestor skilled in Causality Ancestral Techniques would be unable to kill his main body from an infinite distance.
"I will go talk to the Immortal Primordial Ancestor. As for whether he is willing, I am not sure!"
War Ancestor laughed.
On the other side.
War Ancestor's will spoke, "Immortal Primordial Ancestor, the Myriad Law Domain Ancestor has spoken. One Causality-type Ancestral Weapon in exchange for the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor!"
"A Causality-type Ancestral Weapon? He really dares to ask! How rare is such a thing? Only the Causality Primordial Ancestor can forge them.
There are no more than ten in the entire Dark Holy Domain, and he actually wants one!"
The Immortal Primordial Ancestor was furious.
"Immortal Primordial Ancestor, the message has been delivered. Whether you are willing is your business.
At worst, you can ask the Causality Primordial Ancestor to forge one, even if it costs you a bit!"
War Ancestor said with a smile.
"Fine, fine, I'll give it to him. But it can only be the most basic Causality-type Ancestral Weapon. Wait ten years, and I will deliver it.
During this period, he must not harm the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor!"
The Immortal Primordial Ancestor said.
"No problem!"
War Ancestor agreed.
In the blink of an eye, ten years passed.
The Immortal Primordial Ancestor tossed a small orb to War Ancestor; this small orb was the Causality-type Ancestral Weapon.
War Ancestor then had Ye Tian enter the War Ancestor Realm and handed the orb to him.
"Myriad Law Domain Ancestor, this is the Causality-type Ancestral Weapon. I have checked it; the Immortal Primordial Ancestor did not tamper with it.
Now that you have this Ancestral Weapon, release the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor!"
War Ancestor said.
"Yes!"
Ye Tian replied.
Subsequently, Ye Tian released the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor.
When the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor regained his freedom, he breathed a sigh of relief and fled without looking back, fearing that Ye Tian might regret it and capture him again.
....Profound Void Holy Realm.
Ye Tian began to refine this Causality-type Ancestral Weapon.
It took several thousand years before he finally succeeded in refining it.
This Causality-type Ancestral Weapon was called the Void Fruit; that was its name.
With the Void Fruit, Ye Tian could shield the causal connection between his cloned bodies and his main body, while the actions of the cloned bodies remained unaffected.
"A very good Causality-type Ancestral Weapon. With this weapon, my shortcoming is truly mended!"
Ye Tian said happily.
It seemed that due to the incident with the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor, the Immortal Holy Sect had completely given up on the Forbidden Ancestral Spring.
Since this matter had involved Primordial Ancestors, even other factions did not dare to send stronger Supreme-level Domain Ancestors; otherwise, it would be bad if it triggered a war.
Furthermore, Ye Tian was indeed strong enough. Even the Black-Patterned Holy Ancestor had been captured, making him likely comparable to an ordinary late-stage Supreme-level Domain Ancestor.
Among the various major factions, many of those with such strength were stationed at the borders of the Dark Forbidden Zone to resist the Annihilation Clan.
Therefore, the matter was dropped, and no one else tried to target the Forbidden Ancestral Spring.
In the days that followed, Ye Tian remained in bitter cultivation, mastering his physical body and continuously completing transformations of the Invincible Domain Body.
Three transformations of the Invincible Domain Body! Four transformations!
With each transformation, Ye Tian's strength grew significantly.
Finally, after nearly ten billion years, Ye Tian was about to complete the ninth transformation of the Invincible Domain Body.

Chapter 1446: Finally Broke Through, Supreme Realm Ancestor!

Chapter 1446: Finally Broke Through, Supreme Realm Ancestor
!
Physical control 362 times! Physical control 363 times! ....At this time, Ye Tian was frantically deducing and calculating. His duplicated bodies collapsed time and again, only to condense once more, as his degree of physical control grew higher and higher.
As long as his physical control reached 365 times, he would charge toward the ninth transformation of the Invincible Realm Body, thereby stepping directly into the Supreme Realm Body stage.
At that time, he would be able to break through to the Supreme Realm Ancestor level.
Finally, on this day, Ye Tian achieved the perfect, ultimate control of 365 times physical control.
With a single thought, the Invincible Realm Body transformed.
Rumble!!!!! The ninth transformation of the Invincible Realm Body arrived, and countless amounts of energy surged into Ye Tian's body.
Densely packed, the various precious resources covering the Holy Monument World all turned into lakes of energy, pouring into Ye Tian's body to help him complete the transformation of the Invincible Realm Body.
Time passed, ten thousand years by ten thousand years. This transformation lasted for a full million years. It was unknown how many resources Ye Tian had consumed... it was likely enough to allow hundreds of Invincible Realm Bodies to promote to Supreme Realm Ancestors.
Finally, on this day, the Invincible Realm Body completely finished its ninth transformation, evolving into a Supreme Realm Body.
Furthermore, Ye Tian's Holy Soul and Realm Power began to undergo a qualitative change, skyrocketing frantically.
Another few million years passed before Ye Tian finally completed his breakthrough.
Since he broke through within a time array, not much time had passed in the outside world.
"My cultivation has broken through; I am now a Supreme Realm Ancestor. My current strength is more than a hundred times greater than before. If I were to fight the Black-Marked Saint Ancestor again, I could probably crush him with one hand!"
Ye Tian said with full confidence.
As for exactly how powerful he had become, that was hard to say.
He certainly couldn't compare to a Progenitor, and might not even match a Half-step Progenitor, but compared to the top Supreme Realm Ancestors, he could definitely hold his own in a fight...
Supreme Realm Ancestors are divided into the early stage, middle stage, late stage, and peak stage. After reaching the peak of the Supreme Realm Ancestor level, one could choose to create their own Progenitor Law or use the Progenitor Law of a fallen Progenitor to charge toward the Progenitor realm, or fuse a fragmented Progenitor Law to reach the Half-step Progenitor realm.
The Progenitor realm was still quite far from Ye Tian. His current goal was to raise his cultivation to the middle stage of the Supreme Realm Ancestor level—specifically, tempering his Supreme Realm Body to the middle stage. This step was extremely difficult.
Because there were too few treasures in the Dark Forbidden Zone that could help a Supreme Realm Ancestor temper their Supreme Realm Body, almost all Supreme Realm Ancestors had to temper their bodies slowly, making their cultivation progress very sluggish.
For example, the Black-Marked Saint Ancestor and the Golden Star Saint Ancestor had cultivated for an unknown number of realm epochs just to reach the middle stage of the Supreme Realm Ancestor level. This showed how difficult it was to increase one's cultivation at this level.
Ye Tian tried cultivating for a million years before pausing, as there was almost no progress.
"The Supreme Realm Body is hard to improve, but the Ancestral Body can still progress!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
There were no shortcuts for the Supreme Realm Body; it could only be tempered step by step unless one found treasures capable of tempering it, but such treasures were hard to come by.
The Ancestral Body was different. It was somewhat similar to Ancestral Techniques and could be improved through deduction and derivation. If one understood the mysteries of the Ancestral Body, they could progress rapidly.
It was just like how he had understood the mystery of promoting a Holy Body to an Ancestral Body, allowing him to easily break through the Holy Body stage.
Currently, Ye Tian's Ancestral Body was only at the entry level. If he deduced and derived it repeatedly, it would be enough to push it to the minor achievement stage.
As for Ancestral Techniques, Ye Tian could no longer improve them because almost all of his Ancestral Techniques had reached perfection.
"From the looks of it, the most promising area for improvement is... the Ancestral Body. Once I deduce the Eternal Indestructible Ancestral Body to the minor achievement stage, my strength will increase significantly again!"
Ye Tian murmured.
In the years that followed, Ye Tian continuously used his duplicated bodies to deduce and derive the Eternal Indestructible Ancestral Body.
After breaking through to the Supreme Realm Ancestor level, Ye Tian's Holy Soul was many times stronger than before, so the results of his deductions were naturally better.
Through repeated derivations, Ye Tian's understanding of the Eternal Indestructible Ancestral Body grew deeper and deeper.
Ten million years! One hundred million years! One billion years! Ten billion years! After a full thirty billion years of bitter cultivation and countless derivations, Ye Tian finally deduced the Ancestral Body to the minor achievement stage.
On this day.
Ye Tian began cultivating according to the results of his deductions, and his Ancestral Body soon broke through.
Rumble!!!!! Ye Tian's physical body began to undergo a qualitative change. The higher the level of the Ancestral Body, the stronger the physical body naturally became.
"Hahaha, I've become several times stronger again!"
Ye Tian said excitedly.
However, deducing the Ancestral Body to the grand achievement stage would be incomparably difficult.
After the breakthrough, Ye Tian was in a good mood and came out of seclusion.
After thirty billion years, the situation in the Daoshan Realm had changed significantly.
Now, the human race had completely occupied the Daoshan Realm. As for the original factions, they were too weak. Even though Ye Tian hadn't cleared them out, as the human population grew, even small human factions could sweep everything aside. Those non-human factions simply had no room to survive.
Some factions that had produced Ultimate Realm Ancestors were forced to leave the Daoshan Realm. Some went to the Dark Holy Realm, while others went to different realms. Only a few remained as subordinates to human factions, occupying small areas to survive.
The only faction that was doing reasonably well was Black Wind Mountain.
Black Wind Mountain had been granted a large territory by the humans. Additionally, some human martial artists had joined Black Wind Mountain, making it effectively half a human faction. It was doing quite well. The original three mountain lords of Black Wind Mountain had also become Ultimate Realm Ancestors. Ye Tian's former master, Dao Ancestor Xutian, was now Realm Ancestor Xutian. Having received a grain of Star Soul Sand from Ye Tian, he had become an Invincible Realm Ancestor, making him quite powerful in a small place like the Daoshan Realm.
For instance, Ye Tian's old friend Ouyang Jiu'er had also become an Invincible Realm Ancestor. Naturally, this was thanks to Ye Tian's favor; otherwise, she wouldn't have had the potential to reach the Invincible Realm Ancestor stage. In short, all of Ye Tian's old acquaintances were doing well now.
"My strength has been improving too slowly lately. It's time to go to the edge of the Dark Forbidden Zone and clash with the Nirvana Clan... perhaps I'll gain even more!"
Ye Tian murmured.
Of course, his true body wouldn't go. He would only send a duplicated body. Even if it died in battle, he wouldn't feel distressed.

Chapter 1447: Initial Understanding of the Silent Annihilation Clan!

Chapter 1447: Initial Understanding of the Silent Annihilation Clan
!
War Ancestor Realm.
Ye Tian's duplicate body arrived here to request an audience with the War Ancestor.
Soon, Ye Tian met the War Ancestor. "War Ancestor, I wish to go and guard the edge of the Dark Forbidden Domain to resist the Silent Annihilation Clan!"
Ye Tian stated his purpose.
"You actually want to take the initiative to resist the Silent Annihilation Clan?"
The War Ancestor was incredibly shocked.
He knew exactly how terrifying the Silent Annihilation Clan was. Even he was unwilling to go and resist them, but he had no choice.
Otherwise, if the Silent Annihilation Clan invaded, they would eventually reach the Dark Holy Sanctuary. By then, even the Dark Holy Sanctuary would be unable to stop their invasion.
Furthermore, as the area occupied by the Silent Annihilation Clan grew larger, their numbers would also increase.
Therefore, the Silent Annihilation Clan had to be stopped.
However, no one was willing to take the initiative to resist them; it was always a move of desperation.
As for the Myriad Law Domain Ancestor, Ye Tian, he was a newly ascended Supreme-level Domain Ancestor and would not need to resist the Silent Annihilation Clan for a very long time.
"War Ancestor, I truly wish to go and resist the Silent Annihilation Clan. This body is my special clone; it is no different from my main body. Even if it dies in battle, I will not truly perish!"
Ye Tian said.
"A clone? If you hadn't said so, I would have truly thought it was your main body.
Very well, since you want to go, then go. It just so happens you can replace a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor of the War Sect!"
The War Ancestor said.
Subsequently, the War Ancestor told Ye Tian many things regarding the Silent Annihilation Clan.
First, the Dark Holy Sanctuary and the Dark Destruction Domain had each established a continent at the places where they resisted the Silent Annihilation Clan. One was the Sanctuary Continent, and the other was the Destruction Continent. The Primal Ancestors and Supreme-level Domain Ancestors resided on these two continents, resisting the Silent Annihilation Clan at all times.
The place where the Silent Annihilation Clan was located was too far from the Dark Holy Sanctuary. If a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor tried to fly there, it was unknown how many... Domain Eras it would take to arrive; it would be an unimaginable figure.
Thus, only Primal Ancestors could send Supreme-level Domain Ancestors there.
"Myriad Law War Ancestor, prepare yourself. I am going to send you to the Sanctuary Continent!"
The War Ancestor said.
The Supreme-level Domain Ancestors of the War Sect liked to use the title of "War Ancestor." Since Ye Tian had broken through to the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor rank, he was called the Myriad Law War Ancestor.
If Ye Tian truly reached the Primal Ancestor level in the future, to avoid having the same title as the War Ancestor, he could take another Primal Ancestor name.
"Alright!"
Ye Tian responded.
Boom!!!! A powerful force enveloped Ye Tian's space-time, arriving at the Space-Time Source of the Dark Forbidden Domain, crossing an infinite distance in an instant.
This transmission took a full day before Ye Tian finally arrived at the Sanctuary Continent.
At this moment.
The connection between Ye Tian's duplicate body and his main body had become very weak. The distance was too great; even for information to pass between the two, it would likely take several thousand years.
"Something's not right, the environment here..."
Ye Tian sensed his surroundings. The spatial pressure here was immense, and time was extremely chaotic. Without the mind of a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor, one's consciousness would likely be eroded by the space-time power here.
Furthermore, it was difficult for him to exert his power.
"I'm afraid I won't be able to exert much of my strength here...!"
Ye Tian thought to himself.
Boom!!!! A Supreme-level Domain Ancestor appeared before Ye Tian, one whom Ye Tian did not recognize.
"You must be the Myriad Law War Ancestor?"
The newcomer asked.
"You are the Blood Dragon War Ancestor!"
Ye Tian said.
He had never met the Blood Dragon War Ancestor, but his Copy Talent had detected the name, thus revealing the Blood Dragon War Ancestor's identity.
The Blood Dragon War Ancestor was also one of the Supreme-level War Ancestors of the War Sect and one of its Vice Sect Masters.
However, this so-called Vice Sect Master title was actually just a title for the outside world. Within the War Sect, there was no such thing as a Vice Sect Master among Supreme-level Domain Ancestors.
"It is I. The War Ancestor notified me of your arrival. I'll introduce you to the situation of the Sanctuary Continent and the things you need to watch out for. These matters are quite complex, and the War Ancestor didn't have the time to explain them to you one by one, so he let me be your guide!"
The Blood Dragon War Ancestor said.
Afterward, the Blood Dragon War Ancestor brought Ye Tian to a manor.
"Myriad Law War Ancestor, you shall live here from now on!"
The Blood Dragon War Ancestor said.
Then, the two sat down, and the Blood Dragon War Ancestor explained the situation to Ye Tian.
"Myriad Law War Ancestor, deep within the space-time in front of our Sanctuary Continent lies the Space-Time Corridor. The other end of the Space-Time Corridor is... the territory of the Silent Annihilation Clan. Their power is invading this region of space-time. Our goal is to... hold them back. Otherwise, the position of the Space-Time Corridor will keep moving, and their territory will grow larger.
Additionally, this place is different from the Dark Holy Sanctuary. You should have felt that you cannot exert your full power, right? This is normal; it is the same for everyone!"
"There is no Taboo Power here, nor any other power. There is only the Silent Annihilation energy of the Silent Annihilation Clan.
Strictly speaking, the Silent Annihilation energy of the Silent Annihilation Clan fills this... space-time. Unfortunately, it is very difficult for us to refine their energy; only Primal Ancestors have the ability to refine Silent Annihilation energy.
Therefore, once we fight here and consume too much power, it is very difficult to replenish energy.
So, once the energy resources on our person are depleted, we need to exchange for energy resources from the Primal Ancestors."
"Furthermore, this region of space-time also gives birth to many rare treasures and even some opportunities. There was once a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor who obtained an opportunity in this space-time and eventually ascended to become a Primal Ancestor.
Additionally, there are many Taboo creature races on the Sanctuary Continent. They are also Supreme-level Domain Ancestors, and almost all of them are under the command of the Taboo Holy Gate."
"The Silent Annihilation Clan launches a small attack almost every few tens of thousands of years. We try our best to fight the weaker members of the Silent Annihilation Clan. Do not seek out the powerful ones, or you won't even know how you died!"
"The strength of the Silent Annihilation Clan is easy to judge. You only need to look at the grey stripes on their bodies. One grey stripe means a One-Stripe Silent Annihilation member, whose strength is equivalent to a general Supreme-level Domain Ancestor. Then there are Two-Stripe, Three-Stripe... once they reach Five-Stripe, they are comparable to a Half-step Primal Ancestor.
If it is a Seven-Stripe Silent Annihilation Ancestor, that is Primal Ancestor combat power. The most powerful is the Nine-Stripe Silent Annihilation Ancestor. Currently, only one has been discovered, but it requires the strongest Primal Ancestor of our Dark Holy Sanctuary and the strongest Primal Ancestor of the Dark Destruction Domain to join forces just to barely contend with it."
The Blood Dragon War Ancestor said many things, and Ye Tian recorded them all one by one.

Chapter 1448: The Terrifying Talent of the Nirvana Clan! Copy!

Chapter 1448: The Terrifying Talent of the Nirvana Clan
!Copy!
After understanding the situation here and the strength of the Nirvana Clan, Ye Tian felt nothing but solemnity.
The Nirvana Clan's strength was too terrifying, and they were very difficult to kill because once a member of the Nirvana Clan was too heavily injured, they could simply retreat.
Furthermore, the Nirvana Clan could absorb Nirvana energy during battle, whereas these Domain Ancestors had no way to absorb energy. In a long-term battle, those of the same level simply couldn't defeat the Nirvana Clan.
Additionally, their consumption was too great. If they didn't have the resources of an entire Dark Forbidden Domain as backup, they wouldn't be able to sustain such endless ages of fighting.
"War Ancestor Wanfa, your mission is... to guard this area. Once the Nirvana Clan invades from this area, as long as the opponent's strength does not exceed your limit, you cannot flee, nor can you call for help, understood?"
War Ancestor Blood Dragon said.
"I understand!"
Ye Tian nodded.
A few days later, Ye Tian flew out of the Sanctuary Continent and headed to an area in front of the Spacetime Corridor.
There were a total of six Supreme-level Domain Ancestors stationed in this area, the strongest of whom was at the peak of the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor stage.
But this... peak Supreme-level Domain Ancestor was not a cultivator, but a Taboo Creature.
When Ye Tian arrived here and saw this Taboo Creature, he was instantly shocked.
He recognized this... Taboo Creature at the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor level.
"Ancestor Peng!"
Ye Tian called out the other's name.
Before he had become a Half-step Domain Ancestor, the Profound Void Sacred Realm had not yet appeared. At that time, the world was called the Profound Void Ancient Realm, which was not even as good as a Domain Realm. In a Taboo Treasure Land, Ancestor Peng's consciousness had descended upon a Taboo Treasure.
He had fought with Ancestor Peng's phantom, and in the end, Ancestor Peng, seeing his high potential, passed on the Extreme Path Inheritance to him.
To the current him, the Extreme Path Inheritance was nothing, but back then his strength was very weak, and the Extreme Path Inheritance had been of immense help to him.
Therefore, Ancestor Peng had shown him kindness.
"Greetings, Ancestor Peng!"
Ye Tian said.
"Oh? Looking at your eyes, you know me?"
Ancestor Peng asked curiously.
"Ancestor Peng, you once taught me the Extreme Path Inheritance, do you remember?"
Ye Tian asked.
"Extreme Path Inheritance?"
Ancestor Peng thought back for a moment and finally remembered Ye Tian. "You are that... little fellow from some small realm? Back then, I saw you were somewhat interesting; in a place like a small realm, you could actually rival the geniuses in the Dark Sanctuary, so I casually gave you a copy of the Extreme Path Inheritance. I didn't expect you to grow to a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor so quickly!"
At this moment, Ancestor Peng was incredibly shocked.
He had praised Ye Tian back then, saying that Ye Tian had a chance to become a being like him.
But that was just a joke.
At that time, Ye Tian's talent only gave him a bit of interest, but there were countless people who surpassed Ye Tian. Some Sacred Talent possessors were incredibly monstrous from birth, yet in the end, they still couldn't break through to become Supreme-level Domain Ancestors.
Therefore, he didn't think Ye Tian had a chance to become a being like himself.
If calculated by probability, Ye Tian probably only had a one-in-a-billion chance of becoming a Supreme-level Domain Ancestor like him.
But now, Ye Tian had done it, and it hadn't even taken that long.
"Ancestor Peng's Extreme Path Inheritance laid a good foundation for me back then, thank you, Ancestor Peng!"
Ye Tian said gratefully.
"Hahaha, I just did it on a whim!"
Ancestor Peng laughed.
Immediately, the human and the Taboo Creature chatted for a long time before parting ways, returning to their respective posts to guard the area at all times and prevent any Nirvana Clan members from sneaking in.
Time slowly passed. Ye Tian guarded this place for tens of thousands of years without encountering a single Nirvana Clan member. However, the Nirvana Clan appeared in other places, but he couldn't leave his post, so he didn't go to watch.
One day.
While Ye Tian was cultivating, he suddenly sensed a special fluctuation.
"The Nirvana Clan is here; it's a Nirvana Clan squad."
Ancestor Peng's voice came through.
Boom!!! More than twenty Nirvana Clan members surged forward, led by a Six-Mark Nirvana Ancestor.
A Six-Mark Nirvana Ancestor was comparable to a top-tier existence among Half-step Primordial Ancestors. Ancestor Peng was far from being a match; once it charged over, they would be finished.
Suddenly.
A figure emerged; it was a Half-step Primordial Ancestor who had arrived just in time—War Ancestor Vajra, a Half-step Primordial Ancestor from the Myriad Things Sacred Sect.
Rumble!!! War Ancestor Vajra's strength was terrifying, far exceeding that of an ordinary Half-step Primordial Ancestor. He immediately blocked that Seven-Mark Nirvana Ancestor.
Meanwhile, Ancestor Peng blocked two Four-Mark Nirvana Clan members, and the other Supreme-level Domain Ancestors each chose two or more Nirvana Clan members to fight. After all, they were outnumbered, which was unavoidable, and nearby Supreme-level Domain Ancestors also arrived to support them in time.
Ye Tian chose one Two-Mark Nirvana Clan member and three One-Mark Nirvana Clan members.
But during the exchange, Ye Tian's Copy Talent enveloped them.
Nirvana Clan: Cha Bai. Ancestral Talents: Strength Ancestral Talent, Speed Ancestral Talent, Defense Ancestral Talent, Nirvana Ancestral Talent, Time Ancestral Talent, Space Ancestral Talent... Seeing such talents, Ye Tian couldn't help but secretly exclaim how heaven-defying they were.
With so many Ancestral Talents, no wonder they were such monsters.
In the area covered by his Copy Talent, the Nirvana Clan members he inspected all possessed these Ancestral Talents; they were all exactly the same.
And Ye Tian didn't even have the Time Ancestral Talent.
These Nirvana Clan members didn't have comprehension-type Ancestral Talents, so their comprehension was likely not high. Otherwise, with so many Ancestral Talents, each of them could be as monstrous as he was.
"Time Ancestral Talent, I don't even have it, and now I can copy it directly!"
Ye Tian immediately copied the Time Ancestral Talent.
Furthermore, he also copied the Nirvana Ancestral Talent. Although he didn't know what it was used for, copying it couldn't be wrong.
As for the other Ancestral Talents, he thought about it and copied them all as well, in case they could be fused into higher-level talents in the future. Boom!!! The battle began.
Ye Tian did not hide his strength; hiding his strength here was useless.
He directly unleashed the Eternal Imperishable Ancestral Body and performed the Void Slash Ancestral Technique.
Immediately, his Void Slash Ancestral Technique struck one of the One-Mark Nirvana Clan members, directly annihilating its body.
"Not good, he is an existence comparable to a top-tier Supreme-level Domain Ancestor!"
That Two-Mark Nirvana Clan member said in terror.
Instantly killing a One-Mark Nirvana Ancestor with one move was something only an existence like Ancestor Peng could do.
They had been careless. They didn't expect that Ye Tian's cultivation was only at the early stage of the Supreme-level Domain Ancestor realm, yet his combat power was so terrifying, leading to the direct fall of a One-Mark clansman.
